PSA 1:1 Blessim i kam long man husat i no go long ol tok bilong ol bikhet, na i no kam daun long rot bilong ol sinda, na i no sidaun long sit bilong ol laif na katim tok.
PSA 1:2 Bareket bilong en i stap long Lotu bilong Lod, na em i stap ting ting long em long de na nait.
PSA 1:3 Em i olsem diwai we i plantim besaida wara i kam doun, i bringim frut bilong en long taim bilong en, leaf bilong en i no drai, na em i stap strong long olgeta samting em i mekim.
PSA 1:4 Nogat olsem long ol pipol i no gat laif, ol i olsem awt bilong graun i punda long win.
PSA 1:5 Ol bikhet nau bai no inap stap long taim blong jedjment, na sinas bai no inap kam insait long assembli blong ol raitim man.
PSA 1:6 Bikpela i lukautim rot bilong ol dai na rait, tasol rot bilong ol nogut bai i paul.
PSA 2:1 Olgeta nesen i bagarap, na olgeta pipol i tok long tingting i no ken.
PSA 2:2 Kings bilong graun i stap strong na bosman i kam olgeta, long agivim LORD na wan we GOD i choosim:
PSA 2:3 Mipela bream len bilong ol, mipela kisim na kaskasim rop bilong ol.
PSA 2:4 Em i sibiben long heven i lakim; Lod i givim tok harim long ol.
PSA 2:5 Em i skulim ol long birua bilong En, na em i givim ol iet long popo bilong En:
PSA 2:6 Mi plantim King bilong me long Zion, long maunten bilong me we em i Sain.
PSA 2:7 Mi bai kirapim dispela tok olsem LORD i tok long mi: "Yu em i Pikinini bilong Mi; tudei mi kamap Papa bilong yu."
PSA 2:8 Askim Mi, na mi bai givim yu olgeta nesen blong yumi as inaet bilong yu, ol hap blong graun em i go longwe bilong yu olsem propati bilong yu.
PSA 2:9 Yu bai bagarapim ol long szepta airen; Yu bai krakim ol olsem kala pot.
PSA 2:10 King na praim minista, i gat save; jaj na bos bilong graun, yu yet long tok.
PSA 2:11 Serim LORD wantaim kros, na hamamas wantaim tetebilong.
PSA 2:12 Kisim Son, bikos em i masi bai em cross, na yupela i dai long pait bilong yupela yet, taim Furi blong em i kamap strong long wanpela taem. Ol man i happy tru long ol i go bek long em.
PSA 3:1 Wanpela Sang bilong Davit, wankain taem em i ranawe long pikinini bilong em Absalom. O Lo, mipela ol i stap i go, na ol eni bilong mi i kamap planti! Hamas ol i kirap long fait wantaim mi!
PSA 3:2 Ol i tok long me, “God bai no savim em.” Stap, yumi harim
PSA 3:3 Bareket, Papa God, yu stap olsem skild bilong me, glori bilong mi, na yu i go apim hed bilong mi.
PSA 3:4 Mi kisim bikmaus na kalim dispela LORD, na em i givim me ansa from hap bilong Maunten Sain bilong em. Selah
PSA 3:5 Mi lidong na slip; mi kam bek gen, wantaim Bikpela i helpim mi.
PSA 3:6 Mi no bin kirap bilong fear ol ten thousand na ten thousand i kam long me long ol sait.
PSA 3:7 Kam daun, Papa bilong mipela! Saveim mi, O God bilong mipela! Paitim ol enemy bilong mi long jaw; brisim tit bilong ol i no gat laif.
PSA 3:8 Sivik i bilong Bikpela; blesing bilong yu inap kam long ol pipol bilong yu. Selah
PSA 4:1 Ol i go long bikman bilong singsing. Wanpela ailan instrument i go. Wanpela sang bilong Dauid. Hearing mi wen mi singaut, o God bilong jastis bilong me! Yu kisim we i kam long me nau; yu givim mi graun na harim prea bilong mi.
PSA 4:2 Ol i go we long long taim bai yu bagarapim pes bilong me? Ol i go we long long taim bai yu laikim ol samting nogut na bai yu painim strongim ol toksave? Selah
PSA 4:3 Yu save olsem Bikpela i makim apart ol i stap gutpela long em yet; Bikpela i harim wen mi singaut long em.
PSA 4:4 Krosim gut, tasol no ken sin; long bet bilong yu, suskim het bilong yu na stap klos. Selah
PSA 4:5 Ofaim ol sakrifis bilong ol jastis na putim bilip long LORD.
PSA 4:6 Ol i askim planti, “Hu ina bai showim mipela gude?” Kailem lait bilong pes balus bilong yu antap long mipela, O Papa bilong olgeta.
PSA 4:7 Yu pilimapim bel bilong mi long moa yet sweetpela samting olsem taim kaukau na wain nupela i plenti.
PSA 4:8 Mi bai sindaun na kat i go long pis in peis, wantaim Yu alone, O Bikpela, yu mekim mi stap long ples we i gat sikiriti.
PSA 5:1 Long taim bilong singsing mastah, i gat sampela flaut ol i save paitim wantaim. Wanpela sang bilong Davit. Bikpela, harim tok bilong mi; tingim sori bilong mi.
PSA 5:2 Harim tok bilong klai bilong mi, Bikpela King bilong mi, na God bilong mi, bilong yu tanim mi go praid.
PSA 5:3 Long moning, GOD Papa, yu harim vois bilong mi; long taim bilong deibrek, mi putim bek bilong mi i go hap long yu, na mipela wait olsem.
PSA 5:4 Bikos yu em i God noi save laik ol samting nogut; ol samting nogut i no inap long stap wantaim yu.
PSA 5:5 Ol i savede inap no stap long pesens bilong Yu; Yu i hatim ol i wokim bikhet.
PSA 5:6 Yu bagarapim ol i save tok bikhet; Bikpela i no likim man i save kisim blod na givim tok bong.
PSA 5:7 Mipela bai go insait long haus bilong yu long plenti bilong lovignison bilong yu; mipela bai kruk long respek long tembol bilong yu we i stap holiholi.
PSA 5:8 Papa bilong ol, lidim mi long raitim bilong yu bilong ol i no laikim mi; waisim stret rot bilong yu bifo mi.
PSA 5:9 Olsem tok ol save tokim, nogat wanpela i kamap trast; bagarap i stap insait long ol. Teng ol i olsem hole graun, na toktok bilong ol i skulim na mekim birua.
PSA 5:10 Ol Bikpela i mas autim ol nogut; ol i mas pilim dai long olgeta samting ol i mekim narapela. Drivim ol i go long we bikos ol i mekim plenti samting nogut, ol i bin bagarap long Bikpela.
PSA 5:11 Bai olgeta i kam na kisim hik na stap long yu, bai ol i hamamas, ol i singautim rejois oltaim. Yu yet, yu givim bek pes bilong ol, na ol i yu lav wantaim nem bilong yu, bai ol i hamamas long yu.
PSA 5:12 Sori tru, Papa God, yu givim blesing long ol i stap insait long jastis; yu kamapim ol i go raunim ol long shiled bilong favaret bilong Yu.
PSA 6:1 Long ol bos bilong singsing. Wit instrument bilong streng, olsem Sheminith. Wan Psalm bilong Davide. O Lo, no kam bekim me long guriau bilong yu, na no kam skulim me long popoia bilong yu.
PSA 6:2 Papa God, sindim meri long me, bikos mi no strong; helemi, Papa God, bikos ol banis bilong me i go dae pinis, sik bilong insait i kamap strong.
PSA 6:3 Spiriti bilong me i go daun long trabel. Ong, PAPA olgeta, ong?
PSA 6:4 Tern, O Bikpela, salim sof elo bilong mi; savim mi bikos long toktok bilong yu husat i kirapim.
PSA 6:5 Nogat tok bilong yu long dae; husat ina pemai prisim yu long Ol Ples bilong Ded?
PSA 6:6 Mi les long ol i go pas bilong krung; ol nait mi mekim bengen bilong haus bilong mi i fulap wet long tirs, na mi wetim Haus kuk bilong mi wantaim tirs.
PSA 6:7 Mai ai i bagarap long sorom; ol i kamap dai bekos long ol eni a mi.
PSA 6:8 Kam bek gen long me, yusai ol wokman na meri bilong hevi, bikos LORD ibin harim ail bilong mi.
PSA 6:9 Papa God i harim krai bilong mi; Papa God i kisim praya bilong mi.
PSA 6:10 Ol enemies bilong me yai bai i stap shame na ol i skelim; bai ol i go bek klostaim long shame nating.
PSA 7:1 Wanpela Shiggaion bilong David, em i sangim long Papa God olsem toktok bilong Kush, wanpela man bilong tribe bilong Benjimin. O Papa God bilong mi, mi go bek long yu; saveim mi na kabrim mi long ol i go bek long mi,
PSA 7:2 Ol bai kilim spirit bilong me olsem gaun, na krungim me i go ol loa, na mi no gat narapela man i kam halivim me.
PSA 7:3 O Papa bilong mi, sapos mi mekim dispela, sapos hevi i stap long han bilong mi
PSA 7:4 Mi bin givim bek iet long patner bilong mi olsem nogut, mi bin bagarap enemy bilong me na mi no bin kisim bek long en.
PSA 7:5 Na inap mi yet, enemy bilong me i go bekim mi, na i kam apostim mi; i krungum mi long graun, na lusim pepa bilong mi i go daun long dus. Selah
PSA 7:6 Kam bek, Pikinini bilong Jehovah, kisim strong na go agens long hangre bilong enimi. Wek i go, God bilong mi, givim sentens.
PSA 7:7 Ol pipol i kam na sindaun arond long Yu; Yu sindaun long hait long ol.
PSA 7:8 LORD i jusim ol ples; bikim me rait, o LORD, olsem laik bilip long jastis na trutru.
PSA 7:9 Bikim hevi i stap long wei bilong ol i no gat laif, strongim na planim ol rait i kamap. O raitman God yu husat i salim na wariim ol het na tingting bilong ol man.
PSA 7:10 Skil bilong mi i stap wantaim God, em i save ol man i gat het bilong streit.
PSA 7:11 God em i jaj bilong jus, na God i man bilong belhat long ol dei.
PSA 7:12 I no peni yet, God bai skarim sop long bilong en; em i ben kisim na katim banis bilong en.
PSA 7:13 Em i redi nau, wanpela kain bilong em i dai olgeta, em i tokim ol arua bilong en long paia.
PSA 7:14 Behold, man i no gat laif i karim trabel wantaim hevi; em i save long hevi na kamapim lies.
PSA 7:15 Em i kisim hol na winim, em i wokim belo, na em yet i slip long piti em i wokim bilong en.
PSA 7:16 Hevi bilong em i kam bek gen long en, na strong bilong em i pilim i go daun long hed bilong em yet.
PSA 7:17 Mi bai givim sankyu long LORD long jastis bilong En, na mi bai singim prais long nem bilong LORD Wei I Gat Powa.
PSA 8:1 Long ol bosom music. Olsem Giti. Wan Psalm bilong David. O Lo, bikpela masalai bilong yu, kam strongpela i stap namel long ples! Yu putim glori bilong yu antap long heven.
PSA 8:2 Long maus bilong pikinini na ol pikinini Yu gim makim prais long ol, olsem wanem bai enemy na avenger i no inap tok, na bai ol i stap mute.
PSA 8:3 Wanpela taim mi lukim heven bilong yu, wok bilong finga bilong yu, mun bilong nait na sta bilong nait, we bilong yu i putim ol i stap—
PSA 8:4 Man i wanem, Yu save tok long em, o pikinini man, Yu givim karem long en?
PSA 8:5 Yu mekim em i liklik i no kamda long enjel; Yu kisim em i go long glori na hona.
PSA 8:6 Yu mekim em i bos long samting ol Yu mekim; Yu putim everything aninit long lek bilong em:
PSA 8:7 Ol sip na ol bulmakau, na ol kuskus na mani bilong bus,
PSA 8:8 Pisin bilong skai na pis bilong solwara, olgeta i go swim long rot bilong solwara.
PSA 8:9 O Lip Go, Lip Go bilong yumi, hamamas long nem bilong yu long hap graun!
PSA 9:1 Long kaporaseta bilong sang, "Deth bilong Pikinini". Psalm bilong Davit. Mi bai givim sankyu long LORD wantaim ol hart bilong mi; Mi bai tokolim ol samting nais yu mekim.
PSA 9:2 Bai mi amamas na kalap long yu; bai mi singim sang long nem bilong yu, O Moa Hait, Bikpela.
PSA 9:3 Taim neman bilong mi i go bek, ol i pilai na i dai bifor yu.
PSA 9:4 Yu bin sapotim kaos bilong mi we em i stap long wei; Yu siddown long throne bilong Yu, yu malim ol samting long wei bilong jus.
PSA 9:5 Yu bin krosim nesen olgeta; Yu bin bagarap ol i stap long wari; Yu bin pilim nem bilong ol long taim bilong taim.
PSA 9:6 Poilen i kam bek long daunpesa bilong taim, na Yu pullim oltaun siti blong ol; memori blong ol i los already.
PSA 9:7 Bareket LORD i stap oltaim; Em i makim thrown bilong en long stret.
PSA 9:8 Em i jujusim wol long jastis; Em i bosim ol pipol long ekuiti.
PSA 9:9 Bikpela i stap long husat i skulim, em i bikpela hap kas long taim bilong trabel.
PSA 9:10 Ol i save nem bilong yu, ol i putim trast long yu, Bikpela, yu no lusim ol i kam lukim yu.
PSA 9:11 Singim sang in honor bilong LORD, hu i stap long Zion; kirapim ol wok bilong em long namel ol narions.
PSA 9:12 Man bilong toktok long blokd blo ol man i spil i stap remember, em i no lusim wail bilong ol i skul na kisim trabel.
PSA 9:13 Sindim belasim long mi, o Bikpela; lukim ol enemies bilong mi i kam daunim mi. Kisim mi antap long gate bilong dai, em i mauswara bilong hell.
PSA 9:14 Ol bikim narapela ol samting yu praise, na mi hamamas long saveman bilong yu long gate bilong Pikinini Meri Sion.
PSA 9:15 Ol nesen i go daun long hole bilong wol i mekim; leks bilong ol i kisim long net ol i hide.
PSA 9:16 Papa God i stap klostu long justis, ol bikman i kam antap long net bilong wok bilong han bilong ol yet. Higgaion Selah
PSA 9:17 Ol bikman bai go bek long Sheol – ol nesen we lusi God long memory.
PSA 9:18 Ol noken tek hevi long ol, bai no olsem fergetim em foreva; na hop bilong ol i dai pinis, brukim tasol, nogat ken got.
PSA 9:19 Kam daun na sakim, Papa bilong mipela, no ken letim man i win; ol narapela kantri i mas jusim long bikos bilong yu.
PSA 9:20 Papa bilong mipela, bagarap na wikim ol nesen; ol nesen i save ol i manus tasol. Stap, na tingim
PSA 10:1 O PAPA bilong mipela, why yu stap longwe farawe? Why yu karamapim long taim bilong trabel?
PSA 10:2 Long ol pride, ol i nogut i pursuiim ol i no gat samting; ol i ken kisim bek long trap long ol plan we ol i mekim.
PSA 10:3 Man i no gat laif em i praizim desaire bilong het bilong en, em i blesim ol man i laik ka, na em i kilim tok long LORD.
PSA 10:4 Long taim em i pamin na, man i no gat hait long soim God, na long olgeta ka na em i mekim, Bikpela i no stap.
PSA 10:5 Em i stap strong long rot bilong en; jujument bilong yu i go longwe liklik long en; em i laikim ol i no save long ol eni man.
PSA 10:6 Em i tokim em yet, “Mai bai mi no inap rausim; long olgena taim mai fri long trabel.”
PSA 10:7 Maus bilong en i fulap long karim ol tok bilong kilim man, bilip masalai, na faul ple; trable na bagarap i stap ananit long tang bilong en.
PSA 10:8 Em i save stap bek long viles, long ambus em i kilim ol innocent, na ei bilong en i lukbek i go insait long ol weakeneds.
PSA 10:9 Em i stap bek long wei olsem lion long bus na grass i bikpela; em i pipia i kamdaun long bekim man i daun, i no inap standap; em i kisim man i no gat strong long net bilong fisi.
PSA 10:10 Ol i bruk na daun, na ol haples i go daun long streng bilong em.
PSA 10:11 Em i tok insait long en, “God i lusim ol memba bilong em, Em i kisim fak maski bilong en i go, na em i no lukim.”
PSA 10:12 Kam daun, Bikpela! Liftim up han bilong yu, Bikpela God! No lusim ol i no gat heli.
PSA 10:13 Man i no gat laif i lusaikim God, em i tok longtime olsem, "yu no ken kisim bek long akount."
PSA 10:14 Bikos Yu lukim i kam bek long trabel na sor; Yu laik bilipim bek long han bilong Yu. Victim i putim trast long Yu; Yu em i hap masalai long ol pikinini we mama papa i no stap.
PSA 10:15 Brekim arm bilong man i wok ol samting nogut, kisim bek i go long en long wok nogut bilong en, na narapela i no inap i kam.
PSA 10:16 LORD em i Kwin longwe na longwe; ol nesen i dai pinis long lan bilong Em.
PSA 10:17 Yupela i harim, Bikpela, desire bilong ol man husat i katpisa; Yupela bai givim strong long het bilong ol. Yupela bai lusim yutupela i go daun long han bilong yupela.
PSA 10:18 Long givim desis long ol pikinini i no papamama na ol i katol long trabel, na ol man long graun bai no inap kisim fear na paitim gen.
PSA 11:1 Long ol bosman bilong sing. Bilong Davide. Mipela putim trast long LORD. Olsem wanem yu ken tok olsem long me: “Ranawe olsem pisin i go long maunten bilong yu!”
PSA 11:2 Ol bikman i bengim banis bilong ol, na ol i putim araon long streng bilong kilim ol gutpela man husat i stap katol from wei insait long dark.
PSA 11:3 Sapos fundesen i brukim, na wei husat i ken mekim olsem long wei narawan?
PSA 11:4 Bikpela i stap insait long templa bilong en; Bikpela i save sindaun long sitbilong en long heven. Ai bilong en i lukim olgeta ka; ol i tseksaim ol manmeri.
PSA 11:5 Papa God triailim ol righteous na ol wicked; Soul bilong em i hatim ol man meri i lavim strong strong na givim pain.
PSA 11:6 Long ol wicked, em bai bringim daun kol bilong faia na salfata, na wain bilong hot i go long ol olsem posen bilong ol.
PSA 11:7 Bikos LORD i stap raite; Em i lakim jusis. Ol samting i go raite bai kam lukim pes bilong Em.
PSA 12:1 Long bilong mana meri i save sing. Olsem Sheminith. Wanpela Sang bilong Davide. Halivim, O Lo, bikos ol man i gat respek long God i no stap, na ol man i triu i los pinis long ol man.
PSA 12:2 Ol i tokokesol long olgeta; ol i tokim mipela wantaim maus bilong sweet talk na hap ret ren.
PSA 12:3 Mipela i harim Lord ina katim na kilim ol lip long ples we i givim tok isiisi, na ol tang yu i tok bikhet long em yet.
PSA 12:4 Ol i tok, “Long tung yu yet, yumi bai win. Maus bilong yumi em i stap long yumi — husat ina bai bosim yumi?”
PSA 12:5 “Long olgeta bilong ol i skul, na ol i kisim bek long painim help, ol i kisim bek long hariap,” Bikpela i tok, “Nau mi go kamap. Mi bai bringim sikuriti long dispela man i laik.”
PSA 12:6 Ol tok bilong LORD i kamap strong na strepela, olsem silva i go insait pot bilong het na i kamap klia, olsem gol i go insait pot seven taem na i kamap klia tru.
PSA 12:7 Papa bilong mipela, yu yet bai saveim mipela, yu yet bai lukautim mipela long dispela taim na longwe taim.
PSA 12:8 Ol pikinini i go wankain bai olgeta, na ol samting nogut i kamap bikpela long ol manmeri.
PSA 13:1 Long taim bilong song leader. Wanpela sang bilong Davit. O Papa God, yu no ken forgetim mi foreva? O Papa God, yu bai kaivim pes bilong yu long mi iusait long hap?
PSA 13:2 Oli mas husat baulim ikam long spirit bilong me, wantaim sori long het bilong me long hari? Oli mas husat poisen i kamap strong olgeta long me?
PSA 13:3 Kisim long ol bikpela na toktok long mi, O LORD bilong mi Bikpela. Givim lait long ai bilong mi, bikos mi no slip long dae,
PSA 13:4 Bai eni i tok olsem, "Mi winim em," na musu bilong mi hap hap long taim mi pilai.
PSA 13:5 Mi putim trast long lovingselo bilong yu; hati bilong mi bai kam ap ikam long siksave bilong yu.
PSA 13:6 Bai mi singim song long Jehovah, bilong em ol i givim mi gutpela.
PSA 14:1 Long taim bilong skul bosa. Bilong Dauid. Man i go long hevi bilong en i tok, "Ino gat Bikpela." Ol i bagarap; ol wok bilong ol i no gud. Ino gat man i wok gud.
PSA 14:2 Bikpela i luk dawn long heven upon ol pikinini man meri bilong si if eni save, if eni sarokim God.
PSA 14:3 Ol i turnim bek, ol i kamap strong olsem kela togeta; igat no wan man i mekim gupela, nogat wan.
PSA 14:4 Ol wokman bilong nogut bai ol i no lern yet? Ol i kaikaim ol pipol bilong mi olsem bun; ol i refus long kisim nem bilong LORD.
PSA 14:5 Ol i stap yet, ol i bikim birua na ol i gat siki long hed, wantaim ol i save tokol bilong God i kamdaun long ol righteous.
PSA 14:6 Yupela sinna i stap bagarapim plan bilong ol i daun katong, tasol LORD em i kam na i stap bilong ol long husat i save helpim ol.
PSA 14:7 O, bai laveman bilong Isrel i kam long Zion! Wanpela taim olgeta pisin bilong GOD i kam bek gen, Jakob i amamas, Isrel i hap!
PSA 15:1 Sang bilong Dauid. O Papa God, hu mas stap insait long haus bilong yu? Hu mas stap long maunten bilong yu we em i halow?
PSA 15:2 Man i go wantaim trut na save long law, em i praktisim gutpela pasin, em i tok alegeta trut long het bilong en.
PSA 15:3 Hu i no gat tok bung long tong bilong en, hu i no mekim bagarap long nek bilong en, hu i no kisim gen long pairen bilong en.
PSA 15:4 I gat despit long ol samting nogut, tasol em i givim ondulong long ol manmeri i fearim LORD, na em i no bin senisim promis bilong em we i kosit planti.
PSA 15:5 Em i givim mani long ol narapela long wei we em i no tek kam bek, em i no lusim kompi bai ol i givim baksait long ol narapela we ol i nogat bikos. Em i no biruaun, na em bai i stap strong long taim olgeta.
PSA 16:1 Wanpela Tok Bilong Song Bihaen Long Daavid. Savesim mi, o God, bikpela, long yu mi kam na kisim rest.
PSA 16:2 Mi tokim olsem long LORD, "Yu em i papa bilong mi; longwe yu, mi no gat gutpela samting."
PSA 16:3 Ol saint i stap long kantri, em i gutpela kain, na ol bikpela liklik joy bilong me i stap long ol.
PSA 16:4 Sori i go long olsem na i kamap planti long ol i ranawe na bilong go bek gena long narapela kina god. Mi no pilim oliban bilong bled, na mi no toktok nem bilong ol wantaim lip bilong mi.
PSA 16:5 Papa God em i ples bilong mi yet, kaps bilong mi; Yu gimme ka long ples bilong mi.
PSA 16:6 Ka bilong graun bilong mi istap long ples bilong winim hart; mipela inheritans bilong mi em i swit moa, na em i kamap strong long hart bilong mipela.
PSA 16:7 Mi blesim LORD we hu givim mi tok; long nait bilevuen, ma consiens i skulim mi.
PSA 16:8 Mi bin putim LORD oltaim bifor mi. Bikos em i stap long rait han bilong mi, mi no bai birua.
PSA 16:9 Long olgetting, hap bilong me i amamas, tang bilong me i singsing; bodi bilong me bai stap gut long ples.
PSA 16:10 Yu no go lusim spirit bilong me long hap bilong deat, na Yu no go letim Bikpela i Klin bilong yu i katim i go daun.
PSA 16:11 Yu bin sho mi long rot bilong laip; Yu bai kamapim mi long joi insait long presens bilong yu, wantaim plesa olsem i no kan aut long han rait bilong Yu.
PSA 17:1 Wanpela prea bilong Daud. Harim, O Lo, mipela prea bilong jusis; harim nau mipela krai. Kam herim mipela prea - em i kam long maus bilong man i no gat bilip masalai.
PSA 17:2 Dispela stret bilong mi i kam long ples bilong yu; mai yutupela i lukim olgeta samting i stret.
PSA 17:3 Yu traiim hart bilong mi; Yu kam bekim mi long nait. Yu traim mi na yu no finisim eni ken; Mi desisim olsem bai mi no sin long maus bilong mi.
PSA 17:4 Long ol tok bilong man meri - mipela i usim wod bilong maus bilong Yu, na mi lusim rot bilong ol man i save givim trabel.
PSA 17:5 Stap bilong mi i go long ples bilong yu; fet bilong mi i no slip.
PSA 17:6 Mipela i karim Yu, O God, bikos Yu bai givim mipela ansa. Yu raitim eria bilong yu long mipela; mipela i prea long yu, harim tok bilong mipela.
PSA 17:7 Suim mak i go long wondas bilongYu, yu hu i save ol i go kisim hevi long enimi bilong ol long han rait bilong Yu.
PSA 17:8 Kisim mi olsem apul bilong ai bilong Yu; haidim mi i go insait long wing bilong Yu.
PSA 17:9 Long ol wicked man we i bagarapim me, long ol enemy bilong mi ol i karim mi klostu.
PSA 17:10 Ol i kanakim het bilong ol, na maus bilong ol i tok bikpela.
PSA 17:11 Ol i kam bek long behainim na katim mipela, na nau ol i kapamua mipela; oli masalai wantaim olgeta iyari bilong ol, ol i laik pilim mipela i pundaun.
PSA 17:12 Olsem laion i laik kaikai sampela animal, olsem laion pikinini i waitim bek long ples i no klia.
PSA 17:13 Kam daun, Pikinini bilong God, go bekim ol, ol i katim gras na kamilong; salvimi long ol i no gat laik na sip bilong yu.
PSA 17:14 Long ol man olsem, o GOD, long han bilong Yu - long man bilong graun ol i gat shar bilong lif blo ol yet. Yu filim bel bilong ol man i Yu bikim valua, na givim planti kaikai long pikinini bilong ol, na ol bai lusim plenti strong long pikinini bilong ol.
PSA 17:15 Long me, bai mi lukim pes bilong yu long raitim; namba wan dei bai mi kamap, na bai mi amamas long presens bilong yu.
PSA 18:1 Long taem bilong songdaun i go. Bilong Dauid, manmeri bilong LORD, we i singim disfala song long LORD long dey LORD i bin saveim em long han bilong ol enemi bilong em na long han bilong Saul. Em i tok: Mi lavu yu, LORD, powa bilong mi.
PSA 18:2 Papa God em i rok bilong mi, kibung bilong mi, na saveman bilong mi. Papa God bilong mi em i rok, we bilong em yumi go bek long en, sip bilong mi, na horn bilong selimanu bilong mi, em i kibung tru bilong mi.
PSA 18:3 Mipela bai kolim Lord, hu i wail long givim prais, na mipela bai sev bem bek long enimi.
PSA 18:4 Sting bilong ded i kam raitlong me; wara bilong kaos i winim mi.
PSA 18:5 Ol rop bilong Sheol i kam bek long me; ol pit bilong dead i go inap long me.
PSA 18:6 Long taitim bilong mi, mi karim na kolim long LORD; mi kisim hap long God bilong helpim mi. Em i harim voys bilong mi from haus lotu bilong Em, na krai bilong mi igo antap long ek bilong Em.
PSA 18:7 Graun i shake na i cut long long, na bung bilong maunten i wikim; ol i wikim birua long birua bilong Em.
PSA 18:8 Smoak i go antap long nok bilong Em, na faia i kaikai olgeta i kam bek long maus bilong Em; kol blazim ap olsem kol i tanim strong.
PSA 18:9 Em i kirapim heven na i kam daun wantaim klaut darah aninit long lek bilong En.
PSA 18:10 Em i sakim kerubim na em i flai; em i sail i go long wing bilong win.
PSA 18:11 Em i mekim dak i go long ples bilong en, na klod storms olsem umbrela ibox long en.
PSA 18:12 Long lain bilong prezens bilong Em, kloud bilong En i kam antap - stoun hail na koal bilong faia.
PSA 18:13 Papa God i givim thunder long heven; vois bilong Bikpela i kamap strong—ston bilong rein na koal bilong faia.
PSA 18:14 Em i paitim arao bilong En na spredim ol enemy; Em i kisim laitning na kilim ol i ranawe.
PSA 18:15 Wanpela taim ol ren na wara i kamapim, na ol fonessian bilong graun i kisim, long tok bilong yu, Papa God, long win blong breth bilong sikmun bilong yu.
PSA 18:16 Em i go daun kas long hevi na em i kam holim mi; em i pulim mi aut long solwara i go daun i stap.
PSA 18:17 Em i skulim mi long ol enemies bilong mi ol i bikpela tru na mi no inap winim ol.
PSA 18:18 Ol i kam konfronim me long de bikos bilong trabel nau, tasol LORD em i stap bekim supot bilong me.
PSA 18:19 Em i bringim me longwe na kansel; em i save me bikos em i laik long me.
PSA 18:20 Papa God i bekim mi olgeta, olsem laik em i lukim kleanness bilong han bilong mi; em i givim mi bek olgeta, olsem laik em i no gat hevi long hart bilong mi.
PSA 18:21 Mi bin holim wei bilong Jehovah, na mi no go bek long tok bilong devil, olsem pagal, na mi no lusim God bilong mi.
PSA 18:22 Ol loa bilong En i stap bung long me; Mi no bin i go pasis long statut bilong Em.
PSA 18:23 Na mi kamap strong olsem bifo Em, na mi no go long ol samting nogut.
PSA 18:24 Papa God i bekim pe na mipela olsem laik long dai bilong righteousness bilong mipela, olsem laik long hap graun bilong hen bilong mipela long ai bilong Em.
PSA 18:25 Long ol pipel we trastim yu, yu yet showim yuself trastim ol, na long ol pipel we nogat hevi, yu yet showim yuself i nogat hevi;
PSA 18:26 Long ol pipel i kamap strong, Yu shamem yupela olsem pipel i kamap strong, tasol long ol pipel i no kamap strong, i krung, Yu shamem yupela olsem pipel i gat saveman.
PSA 18:27 Yu saveman pipol i kamap strong long suportim, bai Yu i bringim doun ol man i gat ai bilong pait.
PSA 18:28 Bikpela, yu limim lamp bilong mi; God bilong mi em i bringim lait long dekis bilong mi.
PSA 18:29 Long yu, mi ken go bekim ol solja, na wantaim Bikpela bilong mi, mi ken klimim banis.
PSA 18:30 Longol God, weiti bilong em i kamap strong; tok bilong LORD i kol kilim. Em i bikpela skid bilong olgeta husat i go bek long em.
PSA 18:31 Husat i God apa long LORD? Na husat i Roks tasol bikos em i God bilong mipela?
PSA 18:32 Em i God husat i givim mi strong, na i makim rot bilong mi i kamap klar.
PSA 18:33 Em i mekim lek bilong mi olsem lek bilong dea na em i stapim mi long hap bilong maunten.
PSA 18:34 Em i skulim han bilong me long pairap; arm bilong me i strong tumas, i ken bendim banis bilong bronzi.
PSA 18:35 Yu givim mi sip blo savasyon bilong yu; han bilong yu i holim mi, na jentlnes bilong yu i bringim mi antap.
PSA 18:36 Yu wail pikinim rot bilong me, na bilong bikosi bilong me i no ken slip.
PSA 18:37 Mi pusuisim ol enemy bilong me, na mi kisim bek gen ol, mi kamap befon ol; mi no turnabak, til ol i konsum.
PSA 18:38 Mi krungim ol, ol i no inap kam bek gen, na ol i pilak long lek bilong mi.
PSA 18:39 Yu givim mi strong bilong kamap long bikpela faet; Yu daunim ol enemy bilong mi na ol i go daun biloong mi.
PSA 18:40 Yu bin mekim ol enimigami bilong mi go bak long ples bilong ol; Mi bin putim pinis ol mana i no laikim mi.
PSA 18:41 Ol i kirap strong long helpim, tasol i no gat man i ken saveim ol – ol i kirap long han bilong Jehovah, tasol Hem i no ansa.
PSA 18:42 Mi krungim olsem aus long fas bilong win; mi daunim olsem mami long rot.
PSA 18:43 Yu bin kalim mi long faet bilong ol manmeri; Yu bin mekim mi hed bilong ol nesen; ol piple we mi no save long ol, bai ol i servim mi.
PSA 18:44 Wanpela taim ol hiaman harim tok bilong mi, ol i bihainim mi; man i no stap long ples ol i kirap long graun bifor mi.
PSA 18:45 Ol man i kam from nesen i lusim hait, na ol i kam bek i go inawe long ples bilong ol i strong.
PSA 18:46 Papa God i stap, blessim bikos Roc bilong me! Na God bilong salviesen bilong me, em i go apo!
PSA 18:47 Bikpela God we i tambuim mi, i daunim nesen olsem na bai i pulim i daun long talabong bilong mi.
PSA 18:48 I savem me long ol enemy bilong me; i lifim me antap long ol foe bilong me; i skulim me long ol man bilong vailens.
PSA 18:49 Mi bai givim prais long Bikpela, long olgeta nesen; Mi bai singim sang long nem bilong yu.
PSA 18:50 Em i bringim bikpela saveman long king bilong em, na em i showim bilip long man bilong em we em i choosim, long Dauid na ol desenden bilong en foreva.
PSA 19:1 Long man i save long sing. Wan Song bilong Daud. Heven i tokaut glori bilong God; skai i autim wok bilong han bilong Em.
PSA 19:2 De po de ol i kirapim tok, nait bihain nait ol i shouim save.
PSA 19:3 I gat tok pikinini o i gat langgus, na i no gat saut long harim,
PSA 19:4 Vois bilong ol i go kamaut long olgeta graun, toksave bilong ol i go long hap bilong warl. Long heven Em i putim han bilong san long haus.
PSA 19:5 Olsem wan husban i kam aut bilong rum blong en, olsem wan wari i amamas long ran i go long kos blong en.
PSA 19:6 Em i go ap long wan end bilong heven na em i wokabaut go long narakain end; nothing i no lak lukim het bilong em.
PSA 19:7 Lo Bilong God em i perfek, i bringim bak laip bilong spirit; tok bilong God em i triu, i mekim ol senis man i save.
PSA 19:8 Ol lakem bilong LORD i stret, i bringim bel hevi long het; ol komando bilong LORD i lait, i givim lait long ai.
PSA 19:9 Respek long LorD i klia, em i stap oltaim; lo bilong LorD ol i triu, ol i dai wankain, jistis.
PSA 19:10 Ol i mas precious na gol, na gol pia i go daun, ol i swit moa long hanisuk, na hanisuk bilong kom.
PSA 19:11 Ol i kam bek long ol, wokman bilong yu em i save long tok long bihainim ol, na i gat bikpela benefis.
PSA 19:12 Husat ina save pilimim nogut bilong em yet? Puripim mi long hevi bilong mi i no larim.
PSA 19:13 Lukim servan bilong yu, ol sin bilong Sikir Pakana, ol i no ken bossim mi, na bai mi kamap namba wan, sin tu, na mi bai i klia long bigpela pasin agens la.
PSA 19:14 Wods long maus bilong mi na tingting bilong het bilong mi i kamap strong long ai bilong yu, Papa God, olsem Rok bilong save na Man bilong baim bek bilong mi.
PSA 20:1 Long taim bilong singautim sang. Wanpela Sang bilong Davit. Mai Olgeta we i givim ansa long yu long de bilong trabel; mai nem bilong God bilong Yakob i stap bekim yu.
PSA 20:2 Em bai sendim hap long yu from haus lotu na givim strong long yu from Sain.
PSA 20:3 Em i mas yusim olgeta givim pinis long yu, na em i mas luk gut long ol samthing yu pilim na bungim. Selah
PSA 20:4 Em i givim yu ol samting yu laikim long haret, na em i mekim ol plan bilong yu i kamap strong.
PSA 20:5 Mipela mas singautim rejois long bikmoh bilong yu, putim banis long nem bilong God bilong mipela. LORD i mas givim ap ol bikmoh bilong yu.
PSA 20:6 Nau mi save, Bikpela i save ol i bilong en; Em i givim ansa long em from heven i halim long pawa bilong save na han bilong rait.
PSA 20:7 Nupela i trast long kar, nather i trast long hors, tasol mipela i trast long nem bilong LORD God bilong mipela.
PSA 20:8 Ol i kalap na ol i pis, tasol mipela i kamap na mipela i stap strong.
PSA 20:9 O Papa, saveman king. Givim ansa long dey em i kolim.
PSA 21:1 Long taim bilong song leader. Wanpela Psalm bilong David. O Papa God, king i amaze long strong bilong yu. Em i halela long saveman bilong yu!
PSA 21:2 Yu givim em desaire blong het blong en, na yu no holim bek long tok askim blong lip blong en. Selah
PSA 21:3 Yupela welkamim him wantaim blesings plenti; Yupela putim antap long hed bilong en kraun bilong golpela i paiawer.
PSA 21:4 Em i askim Yu long laip, na Yu i givim em — olsem namba bilong de, longtaim na longtaim.
PSA 21:5 Em i gat glori bilong em i bikpela long salvishen bilong yu; Yu givim em splenda na majesti.
PSA 21:6 Yu givim em blessing foreva; yu laik makim em i amamas long joi long ples bilong Yu.
PSA 21:7 King i putim trast long Lod; long stret bilong lav bilong God wei i gat powa biknem, em no ken kisim fear.
PSA 21:8 Han bilong yu em bai kamdaun ol eni bilong yu; han rait bilong yu, em bai kisim ol i no likim yu.
PSA 21:9 Yu bai putim ol long aun bilong faia wail nau yu kam ap, na long taim bilong weranga blong LORD, LORD bai kalapim ol, na faia bai kaikaim ol.
PSA 21:10 Yu bai wipim ol desenden bilong ol long graun, na ol pikinini bilong ol long ol manmeri.
PSA 21:11 Ol i laik mekim olsem long Yu, tasol ol ka na plan ol i wokim bai no inap win.
PSA 21:12 Yu bai putim ol i ranawe wensi bao bilong yu i redi long ol.
PSA 21:13 LORDE, yu kam longwe i go hap long strongpela bilong yu; yumi bai singim song na praisim pawa bilong yu.
PSA 22:1 Long bilong mana meri i sing. Long saund blo 'Doe bilong Mone'. Wan Psalm bilong Davit. O God bilong mi, o God bilong mi, why yu lusim mi? Why yu go longwe dai bifo yu save mi, longwe dai bifo wod bilong ai bilong mi?
PSA 22:2 Mi singaut long de bembe, o God bilong mi, tasol Yu no givim tok, na long nait, tasol Mi no gat pes.
PSA 22:3 Yu holî, yu soten long preis bilong Israel.
PSA 22:4 Long yu tumbuna i stap trastim; ol i trastim na yu savem ol.
PSA 22:5 Ol i kirap long yu na ol i lukAut; ol i putim trast long yu na ol i no bin dispela.
PSA 22:6 Mi stap olsem wanpela wok, nogat man, ol man i laik bikim mi matmat, na ol pipol i biruaim mi.
PSA 22:7 Ol i lukim me na katim tok long me; ol i kisim hevi na skruim hed bilong ol.
PSA 22:8 Em i putim trast long LORD, LORD ina saveim em, LORD ina kalim bek em, bikos bilong em LORD i amamas long em.
PSA 22:9 Yu bringen mi from bel bilong mama, yu mekim mi stap strong long susu bilong mama.
PSA 22:10 Long taim bilong kamap, yu bin kisim me na putim me i go long yu; long bel bilong mama bilong me, yu bin Bikpela bilong me.
PSA 22:11 Yu no go wel longwe ples bilong yu, bikos trable i kam antap long mi, na i no gat man i ken hilpim mi.
PSA 22:12 Plenti bulmakau i kam raitim mi; strongpela bulmakau bilong Bashan i karim mi.
PSA 22:13 Ol i opim maus bilong ol long me olsem lion ol i garm bilong ol, ol i kisim na krai.
PSA 22:14 Mi ol i go daun olsem wara, na olgeta bon bilong me oli brigal. Hart bilong me ol i olsem waks; em i pen amas long insait bilong me.
PSA 22:15 Strength bilong me i drai olsem poti bilong klia, na tongue bilong me i stick long ruf bilong maus bilong me. Yu laim mi daun long aus bilong ded.
PSA 22:16 Dog na i kam rait long me; ol man i no gat laik, ol i go raunim me; ol i bin kolim skru long han bilong me na leg bilong me.
PSA 22:17 Mi inap kauntim olgeta banis bilong me; ol i lukluk strong long me na kisim bel hevi.
PSA 22:18 Ol i kirapim klos bilong mi na ol i tokaut long klot bilong rusim em.
PSA 22:19 Papa bilong yumi, yu no inap longwe; O Strongim bilong mi, hariap i kam helpim mi.
PSA 22:20 Saviourim soul bilong mi long naji, laip bilong mi we em valuabl long pawa bilong dok bilong bus.
PSA 22:21 Saveman long maus bilong laion; long horn bilong bulmakau wil yumi givim ansa long me!
PSA 22:22 Bai mi tok namel long ol brata bilong mi; bai mi givim prais long yu long hap assembli.
PSA 22:23 Yu ol i poretim Lo, givim prais long Em! Ol desenden bilong Jakob, givim respek long Em! Ol pikinini bilong Iserel, tokaut long Em!
PSA 22:24 Em i no kisim olsem nogut na usim olsem bagarap sufuka bilong ol pipel i katim, na em i no skulim fac bilong en long ol, baimbai em i harim kirap strong bilong ol.
PSA 22:25 Praiz bilong me long yu i go antap strong long bihain bilong ol pipol; mi bai kamapim tok bilong mi bifor ol i bikpela tumas long yu.
PSA 22:26 Ol pikinini bai kaikai na kamilailai; ol i lukim LORD bai givim prais long em. Mipela hope haret bilong yu bai stap oltaim!
PSA 22:27 Ol hap bilong graun bai rememba na kambak long LORD, na ol famili bilong nesen olsem bai kus kus dai na lusim hed long en.
PSA 22:28 Pawa i bilong GOD, na em i bosim olgeta narapela kantri.
PSA 22:29 Ol ric bilong graun oli bai kaikai na worship; ol i go daun long graun, dat ogat strong igo daun, bai knel dao bifo Em - ol i nogat strong long save lif blong ol.
PSA 22:30 Olegeneresen bai sarveim God, ol i bikim tok bilong Lod long nupela jeneresen.
PSA 22:31 Ol i kam na birua raitim na toktok long rait bilong Em long ol pikanini i no born yet, olgets we Em mekim.
PSA 23:1 Sang bilong Dauid. Papa God em i givim mi shepherd, na mi no ino lak nas.
PSA 23:2 Em i makim mi sidown long grin pesa; em i lidim mi besain long wata sais.
PSA 23:3 Em i bringim bek gen mai laip; Em i lei mi long rot bilong dinau long namel bilong em.
PSA 23:4 Mi wok long vale blong shedow bilong deat, nogat, mi no ken fright long olgeta samting nogut, bikos Yu stap wantaim mi; Rod bilong yu na staf bilong yu i givim mi gutpela het.
PSA 23:5 Yu makim tebol bikosim mi long hap bilong emi I eni, na yu salim hed bilong mi wantaim oli; kup bilong mi i fulap.
PSA 23:6 Sorenti gutpela na mamamot i go behaind me long ol dei bilong mi laip, na mi bai stap long haus bilong LORD foreva.
PSA 24:1 Sang bilong Psalm blo Daavid. Graun bilong LORD olgeta, planti samting i go long em, wold na ol manmeri i stap insait long en.
PSA 24:2 Em i stapim bek long solwara, na em i planim i stap long wara.
PSA 24:3 Hu ina go ap long maunten bilong LORD? Hu ina stap long ples bilong em we i holy?
PSA 24:4 Man husat i gat han bilong en i klin, haret bilong en i birua, em i no liftimup spirit bilong en long hevi, na em i no tok bagarap long givim sol.
PSA 24:5 Em bai kisim berehet long Papa bilong olgeta na rikonisi pes long God bilong sevensesen i go.
PSA 24:6 Olsem na i kam long genarason bilong ol i sakim Em, ol i sakim pes bilong yu, O God bilong Yakob. Selah
PSA 24:7 Liftim up hevi bilong yu, ol gaten! Yu yet kam antap, olde dea bilong tumbuna, na King bilong Glori bai i go insait!
PSA 24:8 Husat i King bilong Glori? LORD i strong na powaful, LORD i powaful long bikpela faet.
PSA 24:9 Liftim up hevi bilong yu, o gates! Yu yet kam antap, o olde dei doroi, na King bilong Glori bai i go insait!
PSA 24:10 Hus i, dispela King bilong glori namba wan? LORD bilong ol ples we i gat solja olgeta—Em i king bilong glori. Selah
PSA 25:1 Bilong Davit. Long yu, Papa God, mi liftim up mai spirit;
PSA 25:2 Long yu, Bikpela bilong mi, mi putim trast. No ken let mi kisim shame; no ken let enemies bilong mi i kamap strong ol iwaits long mi.
PSA 25:3 Nogat wanman we weti long yu bai i kisim shame; tasol ol i we nogat traust, yu no gat rison, bai ol i kisim sori.
PSA 25:4 Soim mi wei bilong yu, Papa bilong olgeta; tisim mi long rot bilong yu.
PSA 25:5 Givim me lait lon toktok bilong Yu, tisaim mi, bikos yu Bikpela bilong saveman bilong mi; olde long de mi waitim yu.
PSA 25:6 Rimembiri, Papa God, pikinini bilong yu na givim yu laip long ol, ol kam long taim bifo na stap olsem long taim i go.
PSA 25:7 No ken long sin bilong yut mipela, na wok bilong bagarap mipela; no ken long min yet, strongim mi long stap fri long graun bilong yu, bikos yu givim bel isi, na gutpela, o Papa God.
PSA 25:8 Gutpela na stret i stap long Jehovah; olsem na em i mekim sinara i lukim rot.
PSA 25:9 Em i lei i go long olgeta man husat i stap daun long het bilong en na em i tisim ol long rot bilong en.
PSA 25:10 Ol rot bilong LORD i givim lav na wankain long ol pipol i save mekim kot bilong en na statut bilong en.
PSA 25:11 Long namel bilong yu, Bikpela, forgivim sin bilong me, bikos em i gat bikpela.
PSA 25:12 Husat i man i gat respek long Lod? Em bai instruktim em long rot i god choosim bilong en.
PSA 25:13 Spirit bilong em bai stap long prosperiti, na ol descendan bilong em bai kisim inheritan long graun.
PSA 25:14 Papa God i givim kauntim long ol manmeri we igat respek long em, na i shoim treaty bilong en long ol.
PSA 25:15 Ai bilong mi i stap olsem long LORD, na em bai tokautim fut bilong mi long net.
PSA 25:16 Wokim face long me na givim mi grit, bikos mi lonli na mi sori.
PSA 25:17 Hevi bilong het bilong mi i go antap; bekim mi long distres bilong mi.
PSA 25:18 Singsing long hap blong mi na kros blong mi, na kisim wei ol sin blong mi.
PSA 25:19 Singsing long enemi bilong mi, ol i plenti, na ol i hatim mi wantaim hat long tol.
PSA 25:20 Pikinua ol sel bilong me, kisim me na kam bek long yu; no ken skelim olsem na me kisim shame, bikos mi go bek long yu.
PSA 25:21 Mai olsem integriti na streit i save me, bikos mi wait long yu.
PSA 25:22 Selim Isrel, o God, long olgeta sorimi bilong en.
PSA 26:1 Bilong Dauid. Siosi long me, O LORDE! Mi go wankain wantaim jus; mi putim trast long LORDE na mi no bilipim i go bek.
PSA 26:2 Bikpela, tosim ol i go long me, traiim mi; lukim gut hat bilong mi na tok bilong mi.
PSA 26:3 Yu laikim olgeta i stap bifor ai bilong mi, na mi go wok long wei bilong yu.
PSA 26:4 Mi no sidaun wantaim ol man i gat bikpela lie, na mi no stap wantaim ol man i gat mauswara.
PSA 26:5 Mi no likim ol man i go het long ol samting nogut, na mi refusim long sit wantaim ol man i go long sin.
PSA 26:6 Mi wasim han bilong mi long nogut nius, dat mi mas go wankain long alta bilong yu, o LORD.
PSA 26:7 Mi kisim bek long ol voys bilong me long givim sanksem, na tok ol samting nais i yu wokim.
PSA 26:8 O GOD, mi lavim haus we yu stap, ples we glori bilong yu istap.
PSA 26:9 No ken takim spirit bilong me i go wantaim ol man i gat bikpela sin, o laip bilong me i go wantaim ol man i save kilim man.
PSA 26:10 Long han bilong ol i gat pikinini tok bilong ogota, na han rait bilong ol i fulap long moni bilong baksait.
PSA 26:11 Mipela bai i go wantaim stret na saveman; baim me bek long han bilong yu, na yu kirapim meri long me.
PSA 26:12 Mi go long graun i flat na mi stap, na long ol pipol bung, mi blesim LORD.
PSA 27:1 Bilong Davit. Papa God em i lait bilong mi, na em i selvation bilong mi - whom mi bam aim go fearsim? Papa God em i strangplesa bilong laip bilong mi - whom mi bam aim go dredim?
PSA 27:2 Taim ol bikhet i kam long me, ol i kaikai flesh bilong me, ol enemy bilong me na ol i no laikim me, ol i pilim i go daun na brom.
PSA 27:3 Maski ol solja i kam raunim mi, hat bilong mi bai no inap pret; maski wanpela fait i kam long me, mi yet bai holim trast bilong mi.
PSA 27:4 Wanpela samting mi bin askim long LORD; dispela em i wanpela samting mi laik: bai mi stap insait long haus bilong LORD ol dei bilong mi laip, bai mi lukim gutpela bilong LORD na bai yumi go bek long tembol bilong em.
PSA 27:5 Long de taim bilong trabel, Em bai kisim mi go hap insait long het bilong En, Em bai kisim mi go kaivim mi aninit long skar bilong tent bilong En, Em bai putim mi antap long rok i go yet.
PSA 27:6 Bai hed bilong me i go het longpela long hap bilong enemi ol i kamdaun long me. Long haus lotu bilong God, mi bai givim sakrisi wantaim kalap long joi; mi bai singautim song na wokim musik long LORD.
PSA 27:7 Harim, Papa bilong mipela, vot bilong mipela wén mipela singaut; sikirua na givim tok bilong mipela.
PSA 27:8 Hart bilong mi tok, "Suk finis pes bilong Em." Pes bilong yu, Papa God, bai mi go suk.
PSA 27:9 Kamautim face bilong yu long mi, na no raitim servant bilong yu i go bek long anga. Yu bin halivim mi; olsem, no lusim mi o legim mi, o Bikpela God bilong siksave bilong mi.
PSA 27:10 Sapos papa na mama bilong me lusim me, LORD bai karim me i go.
PSA 27:11 Tekim mi long wei bilong yu, Papa bilong ol, na lidim mi long pati i kol, bilong ol i bagarapim mi.
PSA 27:12 Yu no ken givim mi long vola blong ol enemy bilong mi, wantaim ol witness ia i go op long me, tasol ol i no toktok tru, na ol i kirap strong long mekim vailans.
PSA 27:13 Mi tok tru, mi bai lukim gutpela bilong God long kantri bilong ol samting i gat laip.
PSA 27:14 Wail patience long long bilong yu na stap bihainim Papa bilong olgeta; yu strong na kisim kuraj. Stap wait na no inap hariap, wail patience long long bilong yu na stap bihainim Papa bilong olgeta!
PSA 28:1 Long David. Mipela i karim Yu, GOD Bilong Yumi; no ken harim tok bilong mipela, Rok Bilong Sampela. Bikos if yu no ken toktok, mipela bai i kamdaun i go daun long Holo.
PSA 28:2 Harim tok bilong mi long meri wanpela taim mi singaut i go long yu long helpim mi, taim mi liftim up han bilong mi i go long ples santuari bilong yu we em i holiest.
PSA 28:3 Yu no ken kisim mi go long ol i nogut, na ol wokman bilong hevi, ol i tok pis pes long ol narapela, tasol bel het bilong ol i fulap bilong ken.
PSA 28:4 Pilim ol i go bek long ol long ol wok nogut ol i mekim, na brinim bek gen long ol olgeta ol mana ol i karim.
PSA 28:5 Ol i no ken tokim gut long wok bilong LORD, na ol samting han bilong Em i mekim, Em bai jekim ol i go daun, na nogat plantim bek gen.
PSA 28:6 Praiz i go long Bikpela, em i harim tok pisin bilong meri na em i givim meri long mi.
PSA 28:7 LORD em i pawa bilong me na shild bilong me; haret bilong me em i putim trast long Em, na mi helpim. Long olgetting, haret bilong me em i amamas, na mi givim sankyu long Em olsem wanpela sang.
PSA 28:8 Papa God em i ples strong bilong ol pipol bilong Em, na em i givim save long ol skelim pinis bilong En.
PSA 28:9 Sevim pipo bilong yu, givim blesing long inherittance bilong yu; pastorim ol, lukautim ol, na kisim ol i go foreva.
PSA 29:1 Sang bilong Psalm bilong Daavid. O yutupela hevenli bein, givim prais long LORD, givim prais long LORD ol glory na strong.
PSA 29:2 Givim glorii long olgeta belongs bilong LORD; wosipim LORD long splenda bilong halinis bilong em.
PSA 29:3 Vois bilong Lod i stap antap long wara; God bilong glori i tambulim, Lod i harim antap long planti wara.
PSA 29:4 Vois bilong LORD i powaful; vois bilong LORD i majestik, em i bikpela tru.
PSA 29:5 Vois bilong LORD i braim cedars; LORD i smasim cedars bilong Lebanon.
PSA 29:6 Em i mekim Labanon i go ap longlong olsem kot bus, na Sirion olsem bulmakau i no bin save long taim bifo.
PSA 29:7 Vois bilong LORD i paitim wantaim flae bilong faia.
PSA 29:8 Vois bilong LORD i skelim desot; LORD i skelim Desot bilong Kadesh.
PSA 29:9 Vois bilong Jehovah i karim oa na raitim, i biruaim busna olgeta. Na long haus lotu bilong En, ol i singaut, "Glory!"
PSA 29:10 LORD i sindaun long trotonem long ta na flod; LORD em i stap olsem King foreva.
PSA 29:11 Papa God i givim strong long ol pipol bilong en; Papa God i blesim ol pipol bilong en wantaim peis.
PSA 30:1 Wanpela Sang. Wanpela song long moningim haus lotu. Bilong Davit. Mipela bai lilim yu up, Papa God, bikos yu pilim mipela i go ap na yu no givimuspasi long ol i amamas long mipela.
PSA 30:2 O LORDE God bilong mi, mi kisim hap tok long yu, na yu helim mi.
PSA 30:3 Bikpela, yu kam bekim mi, yu pulim mi up long life; yu save mi from go daun long Hole.
PSA 30:4 Singim sang long LORD, o yupela saint bilong Em, na pritim nem holy bilong Em.
PSA 30:5 Asua bilong em i go daun kwik, tasol faevor bilong em i stap oltaim. Tears i stop long nait, tasol hammer bilong gladness i kamap long moning.
PSA 30:6 Long taim god na stap, mi tok, "Mi no inu bikim afraid."
PSA 30:7 Papa God, yu givim me bikpela hap; yu mekim maunten bilong mi i stap strong. Wen yu kaivim pes bilong yu, mi bel isi.
PSA 30:8 Mi karim aut long yu, LORD, na mi bihem long Lord bilong me long meri.
PSA 30:9 Wanem gutpela samting bai kam long blokd blut bilong mi, long wei bilong mi i go daun long hole bilong deat? Dust bai givim prais long yu? Bai em tokaut long save bilong yu?
PSA 30:10 Harim mi, Papa bilong olgeta, givim mi merci; Papa bilong olgeta, yu yet man bilong helpim mi.
PSA 30:11 Yu bin bringim bek dansing long munin bilong mi; Yu bin kisim wei sakklot bilong mi na yu bin givim mi joj.
PSA 30:12 Haret bilong me bai singim sang bilong preisim yu, na mi no ken siwit. O LORD Bikpela bilong me, mi bai givim sankyu foreva.
PSA 31:1 Long taim bilong singautim sang. Wanpela sang bilong Dauid. Mi go kisim hevi long yu, GOD; mi no ken skamen long taim bai i kam; yu save mi bekas yu gat jastis.
PSA 31:2 Kam daunim eria bilong yu long me; kam hariap long saveim mi. Yu yet, bipkaun bilong refij bilong mi, na stronpela hap bilong mi, we mi save go long em.
PSA 31:3 Bikpela, yu yet rok bilong mi, na yu yet kambil bilong mi; yu leadim mi go, na yu givim mi kaan tri long nem bilong yu.
PSA 31:4 Yu fri mi long stret bilong mi, tram na Yu i stap bilong mi.
PSA 31:5 Long han bilong yu, mi putim spirit bilong me; Yu bin bebaim mi, O Bikpela, God bilong treu.
PSA 31:6 Mi no likim ol man i stap holtim idol nogut, tasol long LORD mi putim trast.
PSA 31:7 Mai bai hamamas na balusim long renen bilong yu, bikos Yu lukim bekim bilong mi; Yu save long satim bel hevi bilong spirit bilong mi.
PSA 31:8 Yu no bin givim me long han bilong eni; Yu bin plantim leg bilong me long ples i op.
PSA 31:9 Papa bilong mipela, givim merisi long mi, wantaim mi stap long bikhet; mai i dai pinis from sori, spirit bilong mi na bodi tu.
PSA 31:10 Laip bilong mi i kamap moa long sorom, na yia bilong mi i go daun long bikmoh; hevi bilong mi i pilim bel bilong mi, na banis bilong mi i katim i go daun.
PSA 31:11 Long olgeta enemi bilong me, mi sham long ol, na long ol narapela ples bilong mi, moa yet. Mi i gat poret long ol fren bilong me — ol i ranawe wen ol si mipela long rot.
PSA 31:12 Mi ol i lusim olsem man i dai pinis, longwe na tingting bilong yu. Mi olsem bodi i break.
PSA 31:13 Mi harim tok bisor long olgeta; i gat bikpela fea long olgeta sait. Ol i mekim plan gen long mi, na ol i laik kilim mi.
PSA 31:14 Mipela putim hope long yu, o Papa bilong olgeta; mipela tok olsem, "Yu em i God bilong mipela."
PSA 31:15 Taim bilong mi i stap long han bilong yu; bekim mi long enemy bilong mi na long ol i bihainim mi.
PSA 31:16 Mekpela pes bilong yu shain long mi, wokman bilong yu; saveim mi na yu usim gutpela laip bilong yu.
PSA 31:17 Bikpela, nogat bai mi sem, bikos mi kisim nem bilong yu. Ol ianu i mas givim shame; ol i no tok, ol stap quieta long hap graun.
PSA 31:18 Maus lip long tok bilong lie bai i no toktok gen—lip i tok bagarap long ol righteous, i fulap long praid na despisa.
PSA 31:19 Hamas longwe tru long gutpela kareba bilong yu we yu givim i go long ol manmeri i gat respek long yu, na yumi stap bek long yu, na yu mekim igrasim long ai bilong ol pipol long ol i kam bek long yu.
PSA 31:20 Yu kisim ol i go hap long ples secret bilong presens bilong yu, longwe ol samting mak bilong ol manmeri. Yu kisim ol i go hap long het bilong yu, longwe tung bilong ol i tambu.
PSA 31:21 Praiz i go long LORD, from em i wokim mi lukim lav bilong en long taun we i klostu.
PSA 31:22 Long taim mi bel isi, mi tokthus, "Mi kat ol i go long ai bilong yu!" Be Yu harim bekim na ipi bilong mi taim mi kisim bekim na krai long yu.
PSA 31:23 Lovim Lord long heart, olgeta sant bilong em. Lord i save olgeta we i trastim, tasol i bekim moning long ol arapela.
PSA 31:24 Strongim yu yet, na katol long hed, all yumi husat i gat hop long LORD.
PSA 32:1 Bilong Daoud. Wanpela tokwis bilong ples na sori. Man i ambunt, em i husat i stap long kisim bekim pinis ol hevi pasin bilong en, husat i stap long kovim pinis ol bikhet bilong en.
PSA 32:2 Man i blest, LORD i no kanim olsem inikwiti bilong em, na spirit bilong em i no gat bikhet.
PSA 32:3 Wanpela taim mi still nau, ol ban bilong mi i kam strong olsem ais from we ol sklep bilong mi long de.
PSA 32:4 Long ol taim, de na nait, han bilong yu i kam strong ibgen me; bodi bilong me i go daun olsem san i hat long taim summer. Selah
PSA 32:5 Na mi tok tru long sin bilong mi ki, na mi no hideim hevi bilong hat bilong mi. Mi tok, “Mi kanfasim olega bilong mi long Papa God,” na Yu dokim skin bilong sin bilong mi. Selah
PSA 32:6 Olgeta i stap long wei bilong God, ol i mas prai long yu wail yu inap kas long yu yet. Nogat, taim wara bik i go antap, wara ia bai no inap kam klostu long yu.
PSA 32:7 Yu yet yu ples bilong mi hide. Yu saveman mi long hevi; Yu kisim mi i go long sang bilong siksave. Selah
PSA 32:8 Mi bai instruktem yu na tisim yu long rot bilong yu i go; mi bai givim yu kaunsil na lukautim yu.
PSA 32:9 Yu no ken sam olsem hos na mual, ol i nogat save nem, ol i mas kantriolim long bet na bridel, na ol i usim bridel tasol ol i kam bek gen long yu.
PSA 32:10 Ol i gat planti sori long ol bikman, tasol lovingseli i karim ol man husat i putim trast long Lod.
PSA 32:11 Amende long Jehova na halimun, o yupela i gat jastis; singautim sang i go hap, ol i stap straet long haret.
PSA 33:1 Ol man bilong jastis, kamapim hap bilong yu long LORD; em i stret long ol i stap straet praism Em.
PSA 33:2 Praizim LORD wantaim hap; wokim musik long em wantaim ten string.
PSA 33:3 Singim nau singsing nupela long em; pilai gita wantaim braun long olsem wise, na krai bilong joi.
PSA 33:4 Tok bilong Jehovah i streit, na olgeta wok bilong En i kamap trast.
PSA 33:5 Papa God i lakim gutpela sindaun na jusis; erop long graun i fulap long lav bilong em.
PSA 33:6 Long tok bilong GOD, heven i kamap, na ol sta yet ol i kamap long breth bilong maus bilong Em.
PSA 33:7 Em i pilimapim ap long wara bilong solwara; Em i putim olgeta dai buk long haus bilong stoar.
PSA 33:8 Olgeta graun i mas saves long LORD; olgeta piple long wol i mas givim respek long Em.
PSA 33:9 Em i tok, na em i kamap; Em i givim oda, na em i stap strong.
PSA 33:10 Papa God i bagarapim plan bilong nesen, Em i paulim pilka bilong ol pipol.
PSA 33:11 Kaunsil bilong LORD i stap oltaim, pasonal bilong het bilong Em i go long olgenarasyon.
PSA 33:12 Blesim i kam long nesen uswe em i gat God bilong en LORD, ol pipol em i bikim choosim olsem inheritance bilong en!
PSA 33:13 Papa God i luk daun from heven; Em i si olgeta pikinini manmeri.
PSA 33:14 Long hap bilong Em, Em i lukim ol mana meri na man i stap long graun.
PSA 33:15 Em i mekim haret bilong ol, na em i tingim olgeta wok bilong ol.
PSA 33:16 Nogat king i save long armi bilong em i gat planti man; nogat warrior i kamautim long strongpela bilong em i gat planti powa.
PSA 33:17 Hos i go long nating long salvesen; nem strongpela i no ina save.
PSA 33:18 Santing tru, ai bilong Lod i lukim ol man meri iu save fearim Em, ol i gat hop blong ol stap long lovingseli bilong En.
PSA 33:19 Bai savem ol long dai na kipim ol i stap ailan long taim bilong hangre.
PSA 33:20 Soul bilong yumi i wait long Bikpela; Em i help bilong yumi na em i shiled bilong yumi.
PSA 33:21 Het bilong yumi i amamas long Em, long bikos yumi putim trast long nem holy bilong Em.
PSA 33:22 O Bikpela, dioospla lamulimi bilong yu i mas kam daun long mipela, stap i go long mipela, na mipela putim hope bilong mipela long yu.
PSA 34:1 Bilong Dauid, wen ol i tok ol i longlong bifor Abimelik, na king i draivim em i go. Mi bai givim tankyu long LORD olgeta taim; Praise bilong em bai stap long maus bilong mi.
PSA 34:2 Soul bilong me i ples na i amamas long LORD; ol i dai pinis i harim na kisim hamamas.
PSA 34:3 Bikim bikpela i go long olgeta na mipela; mipela i go heviupim nem bilong Em tasol.
PSA 34:4 Mi go bek long Lod, na em i givim mi ansa; em i savim mi from ol samting we i bringim fear long me.
PSA 34:5 Ol i lukim bek long Em, bai ol i hamamas na wailis; pepa bilong ol i no bai shame.
PSA 34:6 Man bilong kuk i tokim i kam, na Bikpela i harim em; hem i skulim em long ol kros na hevi bilong en.
PSA 34:7 Ein bilong Jehovah i kampe long ol husat i teketaem em, na em i saveman ol.
PSA 34:8 Tastim na lukim olsem Papa God em i gutpela; man i bless long hem ol i go bek long Em!
PSA 34:9 Poroim ol i save respek long GOD, yu ol sant bilong Em, ol man we i poroim God, ol i no inus nogat.
PSA 34:10 Lain na yangpela lion i go nating na bai i belis, tasol ol man i sakim LORD i no missim nogut samting.
PSA 34:11 Kam, ol pikinini, harim tok bilong mi; mi bai tim yu long tok saves long Resis.
PSA 34:12 Husat i man, em i amesen long laip, i mas lukim dei narak?
PSA 34:13 Kisim tok bilong yu long wei bilong nogut, na lip bilong yu long tok bipo.
PSA 34:14 Lusim olgeta samting nogut na wokim gut; sukim pis na paitim i go.
PSA 34:15 Ai bilong Lod i stap long ol righteous, na eria bilong em i sindaun long klai bilong ol.
PSA 34:16 Bikpela i laikim ol samting nogut, na em i mekim ol i go dasol long rausim ol memori bilong ol long graun.
PSA 34:17 Ol righteous i singaut, na LORD i harim; Em i save ol long olgeta hevi bilong ol.
PSA 34:18 Papa God i klostu long ol man i stap long sorere na broknbilong hart; Em i save man i sorry long spirit.
PSA 34:19 Olgeta ken dai na gat sin i gat planti soram, tasol LORD i saveim em long olgeta.
PSA 34:20 Em i lukautim olgeta banis bilong en, nasel bilong ol i no ken bruk.
PSA 34:21 Ol kankaman bai kilim ol raskol, na ol i no likim ol righteous bai kondam.
PSA 34:22 Papa God i salvarim ol seran blong em, na olsem, yumi husat i go bek long en, bai yumi no ken kisim skul long em.
PSA 35:1 Long Daud. Paitim gen long ol i paitim me, Bikpela; kaisim strong long ol i kaisim mi.
PSA 35:2 Kisim ap shield na bakala bilong yu; kam daun, sarap na halivim mi.
PSA 35:3 Kisim spia na pikinini bilong pait long ol i go behain mi, tokim sol bilong mi: “Mi em i siksave bilong yu.”
PSA 35:4 Ol i sap seekim laif bilong mi, bai ol kisim shame na i stap klostu long shame; na ol i gat plan long bagarapim mi, bai ol tanim go bak na kisim konfusen.
PSA 35:5 Ol i ken olsem awt long win, olsem angel bilong LORD i puspela ol i go.
PSA 35:6 Rot bilong ol i tambu na slip, olsem angel bilong LORD i go bekim.
PSA 35:7 Bikos nogat rison, ol i planim net bilong ol long me; longwe nogat rison, ol i dikim hole bilong bikim ol i kilim spirit bilong me.
PSA 35:8 Mipela i laikim dagia i katim ol long taim nogut; net ol i kisim na karamapim bek long ol yet, bai ol i pundaun insait long wari ol i mekim.
PSA 35:9 Sol bilong me bai amamas long GOD na bai i amamas long salvishon bilong Em.
PSA 35:10 Olgeta bun bilong me bai tokaut, “Hu i stap liklik long yu, o Papa bilong mipela, hu igo long saveim ol i katol long ol birua, ol pobre na ol i peni long ol strongpela man?”
PSA 35:11 Ol witness i birua i kam bek long go petim tok, na ol i mekim ol kaek we mi no save long.
PSA 35:12 Ol i givim mi ol samting nogut long ol samthing gutpela, na em i bringim sorere na pain long spirit bilong me.
PSA 35:13 Wewan em i sik, na mi putim sakklot, mi bilong me i daun long fasting, tasol prerem bilong mi i go bek na i no kom bek gen.
PSA 35:14 Mi go wakabaut olsem poroman o brata; mi bin katol i go long sorow, olsem samting ya bilong krai long mama.
PSA 35:15 Taim mi pilai i go daun, ol i kam olgeta long hap; ol i kam olgeta long paitim mi. Ol i no save long me i tok nogut long mi, long taim olsem, stap olsem.
PSA 35:16 Ol i laik pagal jesta long ka bilong kaikai, ol i skrikim tit long me.
PSA 35:17 O Papa bilong olgeta, olsem wanem taim bai yu lukim i stap? Savesim sol bilong me from ol narapela i bagarapim, laif bilong me husat em precious from ol liones ili.
PSA 35:18 Mipela bai givim sankyu long Yu long asamblei bikpela; mipela bai praizim Yu long ol pipel planti.
PSA 35:19 No ken ol i no laikim mi nogat rison, na ol i hate mi nogat kuriositi bai ol i no kisim bel hevi long wail long ai bilong ol.
PSA 35:20 Ol i no tok pis, tasol ol i planim ol samting we i birua gen long ol pipel we i stap klostu long kantri.
PSA 35:21 Ol i wikim long me na ol i tok, 'Aha, aha! Mata bilong yumi i lukim!'
PSA 35:22 Papa bilong yumiyumi, Yu widda lukim; no ken siut long tok. Papa bilong yumiyumi, no go longwe bikos yu.
PSA 35:23 Kam na kirap, long lain bilong mi, long bikpela mateng bilong mi, o Bikpela God bilong mi na Lord bilong mi!
PSA 35:24 Bikim ol i save long mi long rok long bikpela justis bilong yu, o Bikpela Papa bilong mi, na no letim ol i laikim long mi.
PSA 35:25 Ol no ken tok long hart bilong ol, "Aha, em i lukim ol i laik!" Ol no ken tok, "Kaikai i kapim em!"
PSA 35:26 Ol man i gulip long sikirai bilong mi, bai ol i kisim sham na sem; na ol i go antap long me, bai ol i gat sham na tok baksait olsem klotes.
PSA 35:27 Ol i givim ap long mekim em i kamap, singautim sang i go hap long joi na glat; ol i mas tok olsem: "LORD i bikpela, em i laik long gutpela sindaun bilong servant bilong em."
PSA 35:28 Na tang mi bai tokautim jastis bilong yu na peletupela bilip bilong yu olgeta dei long.
PSA 36:1 Long bilong mana meri i save sing. Wanpela sang bilong Davit, wokman bilong LORD. Ol tok baibul i stap inside harim mi: long samting nogut bilong man bilong nogut, i no gat fear bilong God long ai bilong em.
PSA 36:2 Ai bilong en i kamap strong long praid, olsem na em i no inap diskaverim o hatim sin bilong em yet.
PSA 36:3 Tok bilong maus bilong en i ol birua na tok bilong bel, em i stap nogo long tokwis, na wok strong, em i no inap long mekim gud wok.
PSA 36:4 Long bed bilong en em i planim ol samting nogut; em i go long rot bilong en we i no gut; em i no inam raisim ol samting evil.
PSA 36:5 Lovin bilong yu, o Bikpela, i go long wei, fethfulness bilong yu i kamap long kloud.
PSA 36:6 Raitim bilong yu olsem maunten hai pinis; jijman bilong yu olsem solwara i go daun i stap. O Bikpela, Yu yet save manmeri na animol.
PSA 36:7 O God, lovink bilong yu em i preas, pikinini bilong ol man i kam na kisim kaer long shado bilong wing bilong yu!
PSA 36:8 Ol i kaikai long plenti bilong haus bilong Yu, na Yu givim ol wara long wara bilong hamamas bilong Yu.
PSA 36:9 Bikos wanpela fountain bilong laip i stap bikosim yu; long liget bilong yu mipela i lukim liget.
PSA 36:10 Strekim na lukim yu yet long ol geta bikpela karai bilong yu, na givim raitim skul bilong yu long ol man i gat bel isi.
PSA 36:11 No ken paitim lek bilong ol pikinini i no kam agensim mi, na han bilong ol i nogut i no drikim mi i go.
PSA 36:12 Ol man i mekim ol samting nogut i lain i go daun, triwen i go daun, na inabe long kam bek gen.
PSA 37:1 Bilong Daubid. No ken spak long ol man i mekim ol samting nogut; yu no inwe bilong ol man i wok long ol samting i no gut.
PSA 37:2 Ol i mati quiq olsem gras na ol i periutik olsem planis nogut.
PSA 37:3 Putim trast long Lok na wok gud; stap long kantri na karamapim faitful.
PSA 37:4 Em i kamapim bel hevi long LORD, na em bai givim yu liklik samting we yu laikim.
PSA 37:5 Tromwe rot bilong yu long LORD, yu mas trastim em, na Em bai mekim.
PSA 37:6 Em bai bringim bek rigtisnes bilong yu olsem san bilong moning, jastis bilong yu olsem san bilong de.
PSA 37:7 Stap strong long ples bilong LORD, wait long time na pasient i go long em; no ken kros wen ol man i kamap strong long wiket na ol bikhet plan bilong ol.
PSA 37:8 No ken tok long pait, lusim nakimoi; no ken birua – em i bringim bagarap tasol.
PSA 37:9 Ol i mekim ol samting nogut bai kat ol i go, tasol ol i gat hap bilong yu long LORD, bai pren namel long kantri.
PSA 37:10 Bai i go wail tasol, na ol bikman bai i no inap kam bek gen; maski yu lukim ol, bai yu no inap finim ol.
PSA 37:11 Man bilong peis bai katim gras long kantri na bai amamas long abandant prosperity, ol i laikim tumas gutpela taim.
PSA 37:12 Ol nogut i wokim planti long ol righteousness, na kisim tet bilong ol i kirap long ol.
PSA 37:13 Papa i laif, em i lukim ol dei bai kam.
PSA 37:14 Ol birua i kisim na putim sword long han bilong ol, na ol i ben na bendum banarang bilong kilim ol pikinini na ol i no gat samting, ol manmeri we i go long wei stret.
PSA 37:15 Sipena bilong ol i go kisim hart bilong ol yet, na bow aruw bilong ol i brik.
PSA 37:16 Liklik bilong dai na rait i beter na dan planti bilong ol i go long wei bilong nogut.
PSA 37:17 Strongpela bilong ol bikhet bai i bagarap, tasol LORD em i stap suportim ol righteous.
PSA 37:18 Papa God i save dei bilong ol man i nogat bibiya, na inheritans bilong ol bai i stap oltaim.
PSA 37:19 Long taim bilong evil, bai ol i no bin shame, na long de bilong famin, bai ol i kontents.
PSA 37:20 Bikhet na eni wantaim ol i no likim LORD bai dai pinis olsem glori bilong ples, bai lus pinis, na ol katol i go daun olsem smok.
PSA 37:21 Ol bikhet i lusim moni na ol i no peim bek, tapi ol righteous i stap long gratiti na givim.
PSA 37:22 Sori tru, ol i givim blesing bai inheretim graun, tasol ol i kukim bai dai pinis.
PSA 37:23 Stap bilong man i orden long LORD, na em i amamas long rot bilong em.
PSA 37:24 Em i go daun, tasol em i no ken gat bikim, wantaim Bikpela i holim han bilong en.
PSA 37:25 Mi bin yung yet, nau mi bikim old, nogat yet mi harim ol i stap riit i lusim, o ol pikinini bilong ol i bekim bret.
PSA 37:26 Ol i givim planti olgeta taim, na ol i bereit long helpim, na pikinini bilong ol i stap na em i bringim sampela gutpela samting.
PSA 37:27 Lusim olgeta samting nogut na wokim gutpela, bilong yu inap stap oltaim.
PSA 37:28 Papa God i lakim jusis na em no bikim ol sinis i go long we. Ol sinis i stap strong long taim bilong yap, tasol pikinini bilong ol nogut bai i dai pinis.
PSA 37:29 Ol jastis bai i inheritim graun na bai ol i stap insait long em foreva.
PSA 37:30 Maus bilong man i gohet long tok wis, na tang bilong em i tokim jusis.
PSA 37:31 Lo bilong God em i stap inside harim, na step bilong em i no ken slip.
PSA 37:32 Ol i no gat laif i stap bek long ples we, waitim man i go daun, na ol i sukim i kilim ol.
PSA 37:33 Papa God bai no lusim ol long paoa bilong ol, na bai ol i no birua long hapkas.
PSA 37:34 Wail bilong i God na yu stap long wei bilong em, na bai em lifim yu ap long kisim kantri. Taim ol pikinini i bagarap pinis, yu bai lukim.
PSA 37:35 Mi laikim man i no gat het, i kamap strong olsem diwai bilong ples ibin planim gut long graun.
PSA 37:36 Em i go pinis, i no stap gen; mi bin sotim, tasol i no inap finis.
PSA 37:37 Singsing na lukim ol i stap straigt, lukim ol i no gat skul bilong sin, wantaim ol desenden yet yet i wiatim man bilong peis.
PSA 37:38 Bain ol pipol we i go agens lo bilong God, ol i go daun na i dai; bihaen bilong ol man i no gat gutpela ka, em i kamap strong finish.
PSA 37:39 Sivim bek long ol raitman i kam from long LORD, Em i bikpela kot bilong ol long taim bilong trabel.
PSA 37:40 Papa God i helpim na baim bekim ol, em i skulim na sevem ol from ol birua, bikos ol i go kisim hevi long em.
PSA 38:1 Sang blo Dauid, long yumi i rememba. Papa God, no krosim mi long bel hevi bilong yu, na no disciplinim mi long wik bilong yu.
PSA 38:2 Ol arao bilong yu i kamapim mi strong, na han bilong yu i daunim mi.
PSA 38:3 Nogat gutpela i stap long bodi bilong mi bikos bilong bikpela i bosim yu, nogat rip long bon bilong mi bikos bilong sik bilong mi.
PSA 38:4 Hevi bilong mi i kamapim mi, ol i bikpela hatwok long mipela.
PSA 38:5 Wanpela wond bilong me i birua na i pakpak long olgeta sin bilong me.
PSA 38:6 Mi birua yet na kalabe; long oldei mi wakabaut i go long sampela taim bilong sorimi.
PSA 38:7 Bodili bilong me i kamap strong olsem paia, na ino gat ken stret long bodili bilong me.
PSA 38:8 Mi les na bruk i go long wel, na mi kisim sik long moning, na mi kisim bel.
PSA 38:9 Papa, olgeta laik bilong me i stap bungim yu; sori tru bilong me i no hidim long yu.
PSA 38:10 Hart bilong me i kam harimup, strong bilong me i go daun, na lait bilong ai bilong me i mati.
PSA 38:11 Ol i lakim na ol frien bilong mi, ol iraitim sik bilong mi, na ol wantok bilong mi, ol stap longwe.
PSA 38:12 Ol i saakim laif bilong mi i stap mekim trabol long mi, na ol i wilmixim nogut long mi i taktok long mekim bagarap, wokim pasal long givim rong olgeta de.
PSA 38:13 Olsem man i no harim tok, na olsem man i no save tok, mi no harim, mi no opim maus bilong mi.
PSA 38:14 Mi olsem man we i no inap harim, maus bilong mi i no givim tok bak.
PSA 38:15 Mi stap wait long yu, Papa bilong mipela; yu bai givim ansa, Bikpela bilong mi.
PSA 38:16 Mi tok, "Ol i no ken laifim solwara long me - ol i krungutim mi wanken mi slip."
PSA 38:17 Mi redei bai fal dawn, na pekpek i stap wantaim mi.
PSA 38:18 Mi bekim ol sorimi; mi birua long sin blong mi.
PSA 38:19 Plenti i no laikim me long nating, na plenti i hatim me long nating.
PSA 38:20 Ol i bikim ol i paibak gud nau long wei bilong mara, na ol i harim mi long ol i folowim gutpela.
PSA 38:21 No lusim mi, Papa God; no go longwe na kam kot long mi, o Bikpela bilong mi.
PSA 38:22 Kam nauqwik halivim mi, O Loid mana Sevia na mig.
PSA 39:1 Long man i save leadim sing. Long Jeduthun. Psalm bilong Davide. Mi tok, "Mi bai warisim wei bilong mi so mi no bai sin long tok bilong mi; mi bai kisim ka long maus bilong mi olsem musal, istap ol magma i stap.
PSA 39:2 Maius bilong mi i stop na mi stap silent, mi yet bungimaus, olsem nau sori bilong mi i wail long nek.
PSA 39:3 Hart bilong me i kam hat long taim mi stap ting, na faia i kuk. Na bai mi tok long tong bilong me:
PSA 39:4 "Showim mi, o LORD, end bilong me na pepa bilong dei bilong me. Givim mi save long olsem laif bilong me i go daun i stap, na mi laik save long strongim bilong taim bilong me."
PSA 39:5 Yu inaman, yu mekim dei bilong mi olsem hap brom, na taim bilong laip bilong mi i no got pek bilong valiu bifor yu. Tru olsem, hap man we i stap gutu olsem win blong pispis. Selah
PSA 39:6 Oli man i go olsem wan spirit nogut; oli i wok bung long nogat; oli i kisim pe long moni, tasol oli no save husait bai karim bek long en.
PSA 39:7 Nau dispela, olsem wanem na mi stap w8? Hop bilong me i stap long yu, o Lod.
PSA 39:8 Baim yu long saveim mi from olgeta sin bilong mi; no ken givim mi long kamap shame long ol man i no save.
PSA 39:9 Mai iamut, mai no ken opim maus bilong mi bilong ol samting yu mekim.
PSA 39:10 Kisim bek scopim bilong yu long me; mi laip i go daun long strepela powa bilong han bilong yu.
PSA 39:11 Yu skulim na korrekstom man long sin blong en, i kaikai olsem bulumakau ol samting em i hevi, bai ol man i go daun olsem smok bilong wara. Selah
PSA 39:12 Harim tok bilong mi, o Bikpela, kisim ka long kalabus bilong mi; no ken hait i go long waterai bilong mi. Mi man i kam bek long ples, nau mi stap wantaim yu, olsem man i no save ples olsem tumbuna bilong mi olgeta.
PSA 39:13 Wokim bek yu yet long me, na mi ken kamap hap again bipo mi lus na stap nogat.
PSA 40:1 Long man i save dirike sang. Sang Bilong Psalm bilong David. Mi waitpinis pasientli olsem LORD; Em i incline long me na em i harim wok bilong mi cry.
PSA 40:2 Em i kirapim mi long naraka na klai i stap klostu long graun, em i plantim lek mi long wanpela rok, na em i strongim fet bilong mi.
PSA 40:3 Em putim sang nupela long maus bilong mi, sang bilong preis long God bilong yumi. Planti manmeri bai lukim na bel hevi, na bai putim bilip bilong ol long LORD.
PSA 40:4 Man i gat bikpela blessim, em i trast long LORD, na em i no bihainim ol pikinini bilong pride, na em i no slip long rot bilong lie.
PSA 40:5 Bikpela bilong mipela, LORD, plantiailo wondas i stap, ol ples na plan em yu gat long mipela—nogat wan i kamap strong olsem yu—if sapos mi tokautim na skiraim olgeta, em i moa long ol narapela samting, mi no inap kauntim ol.
PSA 40:6 Sakrifis na Ofing yu no bin desai, tapi yu i opim mipela ear. Ol birua ofing na sin ofing yu no bin askim.
PSA 40:7 Nau mi tok, "Mi stap, mi kam—ol i raaitim tok long buk:
PSA 40:8 Mi amamas long mekim Vol ya; Lan ya i stap insait long het bilong mi.
PSA 40:9 Mi autim stret tinging long bikpela assembli; mi lukim, mi no klosim maus bilong mi, olsem yu, LORD, yu save.
PSA 40:10 Mi no bin harim tupela jastis bilong yu long heart bilong mi; mi bin tok klar tru na strongpela bilip na saveman bilong yu; mi no bin harim na kilim i go long ol gutpela laik na tru na strongpela bilip bilong yu long bigpela assembli.
PSA 40:11 O LORDE, no ken stapim meri blong yu long mi; yu bilong yu lovingkindness na faithful, bai ol i stap lukautim mi foreva.
PSA 40:12 Hevi nogat kaikai i karim ol longwe mi; sins bilong mi im go pasim mi, so mai no ina lukim. Ol i plenti longwe hairs bilong hed bilong mi, na hati bilong mi im bin brom we longwe insait long mi.
PSA 40:13 Vinavit i amesen long yu, Papa bilong yumiyumi, bai yu kilim mi; harim bikos dei i karim, Papa bilong yumiyumi, bai yu halivim mi.
PSA 40:14 Ol i lukim lif blong mi, baimbai ol i semak na krosim; ol i laik mekim olsem nogut long mi, baimbai ol i repela kisim shame na kros.
PSA 40:15 Ol i go tok long me, "Aha, aha!" i mas i stap tumas long sham bilong ol yet.
PSA 40:16 Ol pipel we i sakim Yu, bai ol i hamamas na glat long Yu; na ol pipel we i lovim salvishen Yu, bai ol tok, 'LORD i go antap!'
PSA 40:17 Mi bikpela i no ken, na mi narakain; Papa bilong mipela i tingim mi. Yu yet em i halivim mi na savim mi; O God bilong mi, no ken bihain.
PSA 41:1 Long taim bilong song, Wan Psalm bilong Davit. Man i gat bikpela hes, em i lukauti ol pikinini nogut; LORD bai saveim em long de bilong hevi.
PSA 41:2 Papa God bai kaivim na kisim bek i em, bai givim bikpela blesing long en i go long kantri, na i no ken surrenda i go long wi wantaim enemy bilong en.
PSA 41:3 Bikpela bai givim strong long em long bet bilong sik na bam bringim bek i stap gen long bet bilong sickness.
PSA 41:4 Mi tok, "O Papa bilong olgeta, yu givim mi graun long meri; yu helem mi, bikos mi mekim sin long yu."
PSA 41:5 Mipela i tok olsem wantaim bikhet: “Bai wanem taim em i dai na i no gat narapela toktok long en?”
PSA 41:6 Man i kam bekim tok bokis, em i pilim tok birua long het bilong en, na em i go aut na toktok olsem long ples.
PSA 41:7 Ol i no likim mi, ol i toktok klostu long mi, ol i tingim ol samting nogut long mi.
PSA 41:8 Sik bilong ken i kam long en, na em no inap kirap gen long ples we em i laip.
PSA 41:9 Narapela man i karim tok bilong mi, em i minisim olgeta long Tok Ples bilong en, man i kai kaikai wantaim mi, em i kilim bek hel bilong en long mi.
PSA 41:10 Bikpela, givim mi gras, kisim mi i go ap, na mipela bai ol i pajim bek.
PSA 41:11 Mi save nau, Yu amamas long mi, wantaim pikinini bilong Satan i no winim mi.
PSA 41:12 Long olgeta wei bilong mi, Yu yet yu save me, na yu putim me i stap long ai bilong yu foreva.
PSA 41:13 Praiz i go long LORD, God bilong Israel, long taim bipo na long taim i kam. Amen na Amen.
PSA 42:1 Long ol bos bilong singsing. Wanpela tok bung bilong pikinini belong Korah. Ol dok bilong bus i gat bel long wara bilong strems, na soul bilong mi save kamantait long yu, o God.
PSA 42:2 Soul bilong me i drai long God, em i God i alive. Bai wanem taim na mi go kamap long fron bilong God?
PSA 42:3 Tirs bilong me i kamapim kaikai bilong me, de na nait, traem ol man i askim mi long taem, "God bilong yu i stap we?"
PSA 42:4 Ol dispela kam long tok bilong mi bilem ol samting bilong spirit bilong man: mipela i go wantaim ol pipol i gat planti, na mipela i lidim ol pipol i go long haus bilong God, na ol i go na kisim pati long ol singaut i gat hamamas na prais.
PSA 42:5 Bai yu sori long bilong yu, spirits bilong mi? Why olsem bel isi i kamap long insait bilong mi? Putim hap bilong yu long God, stap trastim God, bikos mi yet bai givim prais long Em, sankyu long saveman bilong presens bilong God.
PSA 42:6 O God bilong mi, soul bilong mi i bagarap i go insait long me. Na mipela i remember Yu from kantri bilong Jordan na from antap long maunten Hermon – ritong long Maunten Mizar.
PSA 42:7 Dip koim tokim dip long sangpela sos bilong wara i go daun; olgeta warara na wapos bilong yu ol i kam daun long me.
PSA 42:8 Papa God i tokim bikos bilong en i stap long ol bai de, na nait time song bilong en i stap wantaim mi olsem praer bilong mi long Papa God bilong laip bilong mi.
PSA 42:9 Mi tokim God bilong me, Ston i givim mi strong, "Wai yu lusim ol memori long me? Wai mi mas i go long wei bilong sori bilong opresen bilong enemy?"
PSA 42:10 Olsem bagarapim skelton bilong me, enemi bilong me ol i krosim me, statim ol i tokim me long oldei, "Bikpela bilong yu i stap we?"
PSA 42:11 O spiris bilong mi, yu go daun, bilong go daun, na harim bek i no gut longpela insait long mi? Putim hop blong yumi long God, bikpela, olsem yumi yet bai givim prais long em, Bikpela Selver blong yumi, na God blong yumi.
PSA 43:1 Bikpela, givim mi rait, prem na tok bilong mi, kisim mi long han bilong yu; bikim mi fri long kantri i no gat laip, na ol man i gat bikhet, ol man i no inap.
PSA 43:2 Yu em God bilong ples bilong mi bai stap, wai yu lukim olsem mi narapela? Wai mi mas go long sorow bilong poisen na bagarap strong bilong enemy?
PSA 43:3 Kisim lamp na tok tru bilong yu, sandaun ol i go, ol i bihainim mi. Ol i bringim mi long maunten bilong yu we i stap halivim, na long ples we yu stap.
PSA 43:4 Mipela bai go long alter bilong God, em i renu bilong mipela, i bikpela. Mipela bai givim prais long yu wetim harp, o God, yu em God bilong mipela.
PSA 43:5 I stap daun, na hariap long spirit bilong mi? Why olsem bel isi longpela insait bilong mi? Mi putim hope bilong mi long God, olsem nau bai mi givim prais long Em, Savia bilong mipela, God bilong mi.
PSA 44:1 Long man i save sing song. Tok bilong pisin wisdom bilong ol pikinini bilong Korah. Mipela i harim na lukim dai, Bikpela, papa bilong mipela i tokim mipela wok yu mekim long taim bifo, long taim bilong ol tumbuna.
PSA 44:2 Wit yu han yu kisim aut na kuarim ol nesen, na yu plantim tumbuna bilong yumi long hap; yu daunim ol pipel, na yu kisim aut na tromwe ol.
PSA 44:3 Em i no bekim gras long sop bilong ol, na arm bilong ol i no bringim victory long ol. Em i bekim gras long han rait bilong Yu, long arm bilong Yu, na lait bilong pes bilong Yu, bikos Yu givim ap long ol.
PSA 44:4 O Bikpela, yu bilong me King, hu igo long givim win long Jakob.
PSA 44:5 Bikosim Yu, mipela paitim ol i go bak; long namel bilong Yu, mipela daunim ol i dai.
PSA 44:6 Mi no tristem long baul bilong mi, na sword bilong mi i no saveman me.
PSA 44:7 Yu saveman mipela long han bilong enimi; Yu mekim skul long ol i hatim mipela.
PSA 44:8 Long God mipela i bin tok bik olgeta dei, na nem bilong yu mipela bai givim prais foreva. Selah
PSA 44:9 Bikos Yu rimsim na kisim bek iet long mipela; Yu no go wakabaut gen long ples bilong fait wantaim ol soldier bilong mipela.
PSA 44:10 Ol i mekim yumui go bek long poi, na ol i hatim yumui i bin stilim sampela samting bilong yumui.
PSA 44:11 Yu givim mipela ap olsem sip long kaikai nau, Yu spredim mipela long ol narapela kantri.
PSA 44:12 Yu salim ol pipol bilong Yu long nating; nogat mani yu kambek long salim bilong ol.
PSA 44:13 Yu i mekim mipela olsem kros long nambis bilong mipela, wanpela lafta na sikir long ol i stap aronde mipela.
PSA 44:14 Yu bin mekim mipela ol tok bilong stori long ol kantri, na mipela i kam bek long ol i laikim gut long mipela long ol ples.
PSA 44:15 Ol dei long dispela sham bilong me i kamap befro migel, na shem i kambeng olgeta pes bilong mi.
PSA 44:16 Long tok bilong man bilong katim tok na man bilong laif, bikos ol i pikinim enemy i kam bek strong long pyapela.
PSA 44:17 Olgeta dispela i kam long mipela, nogat mipela i lusim Yu o mipela i bilasim kot bilong Yu.
PSA 44:18 Hart bilong mipela i no go bek; fet bilong mipela i no go na pasim rot bilong yu.
PSA 44:19 Bareket, yu kilim mipela long ples bilong jakal, na yu kapim mipela i go long dek darkness.
PSA 44:20 Mipela las olgeta nem bilong God bilong mipela o mipela i stretim han bilong mipela long god bilong narapela kantri,
PSA 44:21 Bikpela bai ikamaua olgeta, nau em i gat save long ol samting insait long het?
PSA 44:22 Yet bika nogat bilong yumi, mipela i go long wei bilong dei olgeta de; ol i tingim mipela olsem sip bilong kotim na kukim.
PSA 44:23 Papa, kam bek! Wai yus i stap slip? Kam daun! No rusim mipela foreva.
PSA 44:24 Olsem wanem yu kamautim pes bilong Yu, na lusim pain na presen bilong mipela?
PSA 44:25 Soul bilong yumi i go daun long das; bodi bilong yumi i holim gras bilong graun.
PSA 44:26 Kam daun na helpim mipela! Baim mipela bek long dios long stap wantaim yu.
PSA 45:1 Long ol bos bilong singsing. Long saund blong “Lilies”. Wanpela tok bilong pisin save na bilong descendants bilong Korah. Em i tok bilong lav. Hart bilong mi i kamap strong olsem from wanpela bikpela toksave, na mi tokim verses bilong mi long king; tengua bilong mi olsem pen bilong man bilong save gut long raitim.
PSA 45:2 Yu i man bilong finis tumas; graes i salim maus bilong yu, olsem God i givim yu bleksi oltaim.
PSA 45:3 Kisim i go na katim sword long sait bilong yu, o wariar bilong pawa; kamap strong na wailis long majesti na glori bilong yu.
PSA 45:4 Long glori, bai yu raisim win long wei bilong truth na humbug na jastis; hat bilong yu i mas showim wok bilong yu we i bikpela.
PSA 45:5 Bilong yu arao i kamapim skru long het bilong poit bilong king; ol nesen i pundaun aninit long lek bilong yu.
PSA 45:6 Tron bilong yu, O God, i stap oltaim na oltaim, na jastis em i skaipela bilong kingdom bilong yu.
PSA 45:7 Yu laikim gereftis na yu hatim ol wickedness; olsem na, God, bikpela bilong yu, i givim yu anointing long hed bilong yu, na yu stap hap tumas long ol narapela, wantaim oil bilong jubeli.
PSA 45:8 Ol klos bilong yu i swit moa long mir, alas, na kasía; long haus bilong ivory, hap i wokim yu hamamas.
