PSA 45:9 Dautis bilong king i kamap long meri i gat respek bilong yu; kwin i stap klostu long han rattel bilong yu, i dressim gut long gol bilong Ofira.
PSA 45:10 Harim, o meri! Tingim na kisim notis, lusim i go daun long han bilong yu: Forgetim ples bilong yu na haus bilong papa bilong yu.
PSA 45:11 King i laikim bikos yu swit moa, yu mas kisim hed i go daun long en, em i papa bilong yu.
PSA 45:12 Dota meri bilong Taire bai kam wantaim gip; ol man bilong bikpela moni bai lukim yu gut.
PSA 45:13 Prinses i glori yet, long rum bilong en, klos bilong en i wokim pinis long nedel wantaim gol.
PSA 45:14 Em i go long king, klos bilong kolormik i stap long en, na poro meri nogut yet ol i kam bung long yu.
PSA 45:15 Ol i kam insait wantaim hamamas na gladnes; ol i go insait long haus bilong king.
PSA 45:16 Ol pikinini bilong yu bai i go bek long ples bilong ol tata bilong yu, na yu bai makim ol prinis long graun.
PSA 45:17 Mi bai renim nem bilong yu long olgenarashen; olsem, ol nesen bai givim prais long yu long taim na long taim.
PSA 46:1 Long taim bilong mana meri i sing. Bilong pikinini belong Korah. Olsem Alamoth i tok, em i sang. God em i stap long husat i save harim na givim strong, em i helpim oltaim long taim bilong hevi.
PSA 46:2 Mipela no ken i bikim PEKI, maski graun em i kisim chanj long stap, maunten i kilap i go daun long bubu solwara.
PSA 46:3 Wara bilong ol i kirap na savlav, maunten i shake long taim bilong harikin. Selah
PSA 46:4 I gat wanpela riva we us streams em i amusem bikpela siti bilong God, hap gripepela ples we Most High i stap.
PSA 46:5 God i stap insait long en; em bai no inap rausim. God bai halivim em moning taitim em bung.
PSA 46:6 Ol nesen i stap strongim bel, ol kingdom i bagarap; gras na erat i tanim wen Em i kirapim vois.
PSA 46:7 Papa bilong ol ples i stap wantaim yumi; God bilong Yakob em i bikpela kot bilong yumi. Selah
PSA 46:8 Kam, lukim wok bilong LORD, hu i bringim bagarap long graun.
PSA 46:9 Em i stopim fais long graun; Em i brukim banara na i smasmolim spia; Em i burnim sikis long paia.
PSA 46:10 "Stap strong na save, i go ap, long ol nesen, Mi bai go ap long ol graun; Bikpela i stap strong."
PSA 46:11 Papa bilong ol solja i stap wantaim yumi; God bilong Jakob em i kanda bilong yumi. Selah
PSA 47:1 Long taim bilong skael bilong sang. Wan Psalm bilong pikinini bilong Korah. Ol pipol, klapim han bilong yu; singaut i go long God wantaim vose bilong winim.
PSA 47:2 Olipim bilong LORD Moa Bikpela, king bikpela we i gat pawa long olgeta graun, em i amamas!
PSA 47:3 Em i daunim ol nesen aninit long yumi, na ol pipel i stap daun aninit long lek bilong yumi.
PSA 47:4 Em i pikim inheritance bilong yumi, praid bilong Yakob, ol man we em i lavim. Selah
PSA 47:5 Bikpela i go ap long heven, LORD wantaim saun bilong trampet, ol i singaut i sambai long joi.
PSA 47:6 Singim sankam long God, singim sankam; singim sankam long King bilong yumi, singim sankam!
PSA 47:7 God em King bilong olgeta gras; singim prais bilong yu yet inap longpela long Em.
PSA 47:8 God i bos long ol nesen; God i sib sit daun long thrown bilong em, em i halu.
PSA 47:9 Ol bikpela man bilong ol narapela kantri i kam yuasim ol pisin bilong God bilong Abraham; bikos ol shiled bilong graun i bilong God, Em i go het long wel.
PSA 48:1 Wanpela sang. Wanpela Psalm bilong pikinini belong Korah. Bikpela i go long LORD, na em i bikpela long praisim insait long taun bilong God bilong yumi, maunten bilong halivim bilong em.
PSA 48:2 Winim long hevi i stap, jubeli bilong olgeta graun, olsem maunten Zafon, Maunten Sayon, taun bilong King bikpela.
PSA 48:3 God i stap insait long strongples bilong en; Em i shoim selem i kamap olsem banis.
PSA 48:4 Bihain em i go, ol kingly i kam olsem wan, na ol i go apo long wan wai.
PSA 48:5 Ol i lukim, ol i sori tru, na ol i ranawe long bikmus.
PSA 48:6 Ol i kisim fright, pain olsem meri i karim bebi.
PSA 48:7 Wantaim win blong east Yupela i bagarapim ship blong Tarshish.
PSA 48:8 Olsem yumupela harim, olsem yumupela lukim long taun bilong LORD bilong ol paitim meri, long taun bilong God bilong mipela: God bai plantim em i go oltaim. Selah
PSA 48:9 Long Haus Tavolo bilong yu, mipela i stap tingim gutpela kisim bilong yu.
PSA 48:10 Nem bilong yu, o God, olsem ol i givim prais long yu, i kamap long hap bilong graun; han rit bilong yu i fulap long jus.
PSA 48:11 Maunt Saion i amamas, pikinini meri bilong Yuda i hamamas long jusis bilong Yu.
PSA 48:12 Wokabaut long Sayan, kamautim em, kisim nabawan long haus bilong en.
PSA 48:13 Lukim barrier bilong em, go wokabaut long strongpela haus bilong em, na bai yu ken skulim genarashen bihain.
PSA 48:14 God em God bilong yumi longwe time olsem na longwe time olsem; Em bai i kam bek long givim direction long yumi, tasol death i kam.
PSA 49:1 Long ol bos bilong sang. Wanpela Psalm bilong pikinini bilong Korah. Harim dispela, all yufala ples; lisin, all manmeri husat i stap long graun,
PSA 49:2 Nambis na hap, ol ric na ol pua tasol.
PSA 49:3 Maus bilong me bai givim kaunsil, na tingting bilong het bilong me bai bringim save.
PSA 49:4 Mi go inarim tok bilong mi long wanpela tok bilong kastom; Mi go tokim piksa bilong mi wantaim gita:
PSA 49:5 Wai mi mas i gat fea long taim bilong trabel, wail ol raskol i kam autlong na sorim mi?
PSA 49:6 Ol putim trast long moni bilong ol, na ol brukim bikpela toksave long olgeta riki bilong ol.
PSA 49:7 No man i no ina pem save brata bilong en, o peim pris long God.
PSA 49:8 Long ripresen bilong spirit blong em i go long moni, nogat moni ina stap bai em kamap bekim.
PSA 49:9 Em i mas stap oltaim na no ken si dai.
PSA 49:10 Em i klia olsem, ol man wis i dai, na ol i no save na ol i no tingim samting istap dai tung, na ol lusim propati bilong ol long narapela.
PSA 49:11 Graun bilong ol i stap olsem haus bilong ol forever - ples bilong ol spirit, genarasyon i go inap long taim, tasol ol i kolim ples bilong ol olsem nem bilong ol yet.
PSA 49:12 Maski em i gat planti moni, em olsem kain animals we i dai, em no inap holim.
PSA 49:13 Em i bikos bilong ol sel brek na ol i foloim ol, ol i tok strong long tok bilong ol. Selah
PSA 49:14 Olsem ol pipel i kamapim sheep, ol i go daun long hel. Deat bai bilong ol, em i stap lokim ol olsem bosboi. Ol i gat save long moning bai ol i bosim ol, na bodi bilong ol i paul i go daun long hel, longwe ples bilong haus bilong heven.
PSA 49:15 Bog en God bai bosim laip bilong mi long hap graun, bilong em i go tok Lukim, em yet bai kisim mi i go wantaim em. Selah
PSA 49:16 No ken amaze long tingting bai yu, wanken em i kamap rich, na balusim house bilong en i go antap.
PSA 49:17 Wanpela dei em i dai, olgeta samting em i no ken kisim i go; planti bilong em i no inap folim em i daun.
PSA 49:18 Long long taim em i stap, em i givim berkat long spirit bilong en — na ol man i givim prais long yu taim yu kamap gut.
PSA 49:19 Em bai kamap genarason bilong papa na mama bilong em, olsem na em nogat lukim lait bilong de.
PSA 49:20 Man i gat planti samting, tasol i no save, em i olsem ol bek na i dai.
PSA 50:1 Sang bilong Asaf. Bikpela Wan, God bilong LORD, i tokstrong na i singautim erth long plaen sun i kamap na go daun.
PSA 50:2 Long Sayan, em i perfek long lapun bilong finis, Bikpela God i shain kamap.
PSA 50:3 God bilong mipela i kam bek, em no ken stap mama! Faia i kaikai olgeta i go bifor em, na ston weathers i harim gut long en.
PSA 50:4 Em i kirapim heven i go we, na gras na erth, bai em i jusim piple bilong em.
PSA 50:5 Kam na yumi stap wantaim, ol man i save long God olsem papa na mama bilong em, ol i mekim pinis kongres long God olsem long sakrifis.
PSA 50:6 Heven i tokautim righteousness bilong Em, long bikos God Em yet yu Jaj bilong ol. Selah
PSA 50:7 Harim, o pipo bilong mi, na mi bai tok, o Isrel, na mi bai givim witness gen long yu: Mi em i Bikpela, God bilong yu.
PSA 50:8 Mi no kritim yu long ol sakrifis bilong yu, na ol burnt ofring bilong yu i stap olsem bilong mi tasol.
PSA 50:9 Mi no gat nid long bulmakau longpela stua bilong yu o kikim goat long pen bilong yu.
PSA 50:10 Long olgeta binatang long bus i belong long me — olgeta bulmakau long tausenpela hil.
PSA 50:11 Mi save olgeta pisin long maunten, na olgeta krea i stap long gras, ol i bilong mi.
PSA 50:12 Sapos mi beli i dai pinis, mi no bin tokim yu, long wol em i bilong mi, na ol samting i got insait long en.
PSA 50:13 Ina bai mi kaikai klim bilong bulmakau, osa bai mi dringim blod bilong keng?
PSA 50:14 Ofaim saksem blong tankyu long God, na purmim promis bilong yu long God bilong Heven.
PSA 50:15 Kisim nau na krai long me long de ba yu gat trabel; Mi bai kam halivim yu, na yu bai givim respek long mi.
PSA 50:16 Bikpela God i tok long ol pipel i no gat laip, "Wanem na rit yu gat long karim bek covenant bilong me na ol tok bilong me i stap long maus bilong yu?"
PSA 50:17 Yumi no saves long instrksen bilong Mipela, na yumi kisim wods bilong Mipela i go bihain bai yumi.
PSA 50:18 Wanpela yu lukim man i stilim samting, yu kisim i go olsem brata, na yu putim tok bilong yu wantaim ol i gat as bilong bagarap.
PSA 50:19 Yu lusim maus bilong yu long olgeta samting nogut na katim rop bilong tang yu long bikpela ka.
PSA 50:20 Yumi sindaun na tok bisim brata bilong yumi; yumi birua gen klostu bilong pikinini bilong mama bilong yumi.
PSA 50:21 Yu mekim ol dispela, na mi stap quiet; yu ting olsem mi samting bilong yu. Nau mi strongim tok long yu, na mi kisim bek long yu, tokim yu long ai bilong yu.
PSA 50:22 Nau tingim dispela, husat i lusim bikim God, bai mi bairam yu brigata, na i no gat man i save yu.
PSA 50:23 Emas long givim ofing bung, em i givim respek long Mi, na olsem ol i wokim rot bilong en i stap straet, bai mi shom ol sep long God.
PSA 51:1 Long bilong mana meri i kam. Wan Psalm bilong David. Taim Nathan man bilong Got i go kam long em after em mekim sin wantaim Bathsheba, Givim mi mercy, o God, olsem yu gat lav; olsem yu gat karamapim, wipesim aut ol samting nogut bilong mi.
PSA 51:2 Wosim mi klim long iniwiti bilong mi, klinim mi long sin bilong mi.
PSA 51:3 Mi save long hevi bilong mi, na sin bilong mi i stap klostu long ai bilong mi.
PSA 51:4 Long yu, mi bin mekim sin, na mi bin wok ol samting nogut long ai bilong yu, ripot bilong yu bai i kamap rait wen yu toktok, na yu bai i stap nogat kan long yu wen yu givim desisen.
PSA 51:5 Mi kamap long hevi i go long nogut; mi bin i go long sin bilem momma bilong me i karim me.
PSA 51:6 Bikos Yu laikim trut long ka bombo; Yu tisim mi save long ples bilong hart.
PSA 51:7 Purifaim mi wantaim hyssop, na mi bai i kam klia; wesim mi, na mi bai i kam wait gen olsem sno.
PSA 51:8 Givim mi harim joy na gladness; ol bon bilong yu husat yu brikim, ol i mas rejois.
PSA 51:9 Kamautim face bilong yu long sin bilong mi na brisim olgeta iniquiti bilong mi.
PSA 51:10 Mekim mi yet kam bek long het bilong mi, na bringim bek gen spirit righteousness insait long mi.
PSA 51:11 No rausim mi long presens bilong yu; no biruaim Holy Spirit bilong yu long mi.
PSA 51:12 Bekim bekim gen joy bilong yu long me, na yu yet holim mi long spirit bilong mi i wankain, olsem salvishen bilong yu i kam bekim gen long me.
PSA 51:13 Na mi bai tisim ol sina long rotpela wei bilong Yu, na ol i stap long hevi bai kam bek gen long Yu.
PSA 51:14 Baim me bek long blod kol, O God, God bilong salvesen bilong mi, na tang bilong mi bai singautim stret bilong yu.
PSA 51:15 Papa bilong mipela, opim maus bilong mipela, na maus bilong mipela bai tokaut long stewardi bilong yu.
PSA 51:16 Yu no likim sakrifis, na mi bai bringim i kam; Yu no save long burnt ofring.
PSA 51:17 Sakrifis bilong God em i spirit bilong yu i bagarap; hati bilong yu i bagarap na i sabitim, o God, Yu no ken lakim.
PSA 51:18 Long tingting bilong yu i gut, mekim Zion i kamap strong; bildim ap banis bilong Jerusalem.
PSA 51:19 Na Yu bai kam ap long raitim sacrifice, long ol sacrifice we yu burn olgeta; na ol bulmakau bai i go antap long altiya bilong Yu.
PSA 52:1 Long ol bos bilong singaut. Wanpela tok bilong ples na bilong Daud. Bihaen long Doeg man bilong Edom i go kam kasaul long Saul na tolem em, “Daud i go kam long haus bilong Ahimelek.” Wai yu kisim praid long nogut, o man strongpela? Lovin bilong God i stap oldei.
PSA 52:2 Tunas bilong yu i malumalum long mekim bagarap olsem naip sharp, O man i wokim bikhet.
PSA 52:3 Yu lavim olgeta samting nogut more dan gutpela, na yu tok baihevi more dan tok trut. Selah
PSA 52:4 Yu laikim olgeta wod bilong kaikai ol, O tung yu bilong bikpela lip.
PSA 52:5 Bikpela bai kisim yu go daun long narok i go i stap oltaim; Em bai kisim yu ap na rausim yu i go long haus bilong kanu; Em bai rausim yu long graun bilong samting i gat laip. Selah
PSA 52:6 Ol righteous bai lukim na agrik; ol bai kilim man bilong hevi, ol i tok:
PSA 52:7 Lukeim i go long man, em i no mekim God bilong em yet long stap, tasol em i putim trast long planti moni bilong em, na em i strongim yet bilong em olsem na bai em i bagarap.
PSA 52:8 Mi olsem diwai oliv, mi stap strong long haus bilong God; mi putim trast long lavin kare bilong God long taim igo pinis na i go yet.
PSA 52:9 Bai mi singim prais long yu foreva, bikos yu mekim olgeta dispela. Bai mi w8 long nem bilong yu — em i gutpela — long hap bilong ol sant bilong yu.
PSA 53:1 Long ol bos bilong sing. Olsem Mahalath i tok. Wanpela Maskil bilong Davide. Man bilong nogut i tok long het bilong en, “God i no stap.” Ol i bagarap; wok bilong ol i birua. I no gat man i mekim gud.
PSA 53:2 Bikpela i blickim i kamdaun long heven upon ol man meri bilong wol for lukim if sampela i save, if sampela i lukim God.
PSA 53:3 Ol i go bek long wei narapela, ol i tu kaletha na stap long bikhet; i no gat man i nogut, we i mekim gud, maski wan tasol.
PSA 53:4 Wokman bilong hevi nogat larn yet, ol i kaikai ol pipol bilong me olsem bauned, na ol i no gat hap bilong kallisim God.
PSA 53:5 Ol i stap, kisim bikpela fea na kilim olgeta hap, long ples we ino gat fea samting. Bikos God i skaterolim bon bilong ol i kamap nogut long yu, na yu mekim ol i kisim shame, bikos God i no givim values long ol.
PSA 53:6 O, olgeta save bilong Israel i kam bek long Zion! Wanpela taim God i bringim bek pipo bilong en i bin holim i go, Jacob i mas hapim, Israel i mas amamas!
PSA 54:1 Long ol bikman bilong singsing. Wanpela stap long ensembla instrumens. Wanpela tok pikinini bilong Dauid. Taim Zifait pipol i go long Saul, ol i tok, "Dauid i kaibarim hus among us?" Savim mi, o God, bai yusupela nem, na givim mi jus, o God, bai yusupela strong!
PSA 54:2 Harim praer bilong mi, o Bikpela; lisen long tok bilong maus bilong mi.
PSA 54:3 Ol pisin man i kam bekim mipela, na ol man i no gat hati, oli sakim mipela—ol man oli no givim respek long God. Selah
PSA 54:4 Sapos Gott em i halivim mi tasol, na Dok i sapot long soul bilong mi.
PSA 54:5 Em bai givim bek long enemy bilong me olgeta samting nogut, na long tru bilong yu, brukim ol.
PSA 54:6 Bikos nating, bai mi sakrifais long yu; bai mi praisim nem bilong yu, o LORD, bikos em i gut.
PSA 54:7 Em i bin saveim me long olgeta trable, na mai pe i bin bihainim ol enemy bilong me.
PSA 55:1 Long olgeta man i save sing. Wantaim instrumens i gat string. Wanpela tokwis bilong David. Harim prea bilong mi, O God, no ken slipim bekim bilong mi.
PSA 55:2 Husaitim yu long harim tok bilong mi, givim mi ansa. Mi no inap stap strong long tok bilong protest, na mi birua.
PSA 55:3 Long tok bilong poi, long presa bilong ol i no gat laif, ol lusim bikim ol samting nogut i kam long me, na ol i kros na kisim me long rong bilong ol.
PSA 55:4 Haret bilong me i go tok-tok insait long me, na ogota bilong dai i kam bekim me.
PSA 55:5 Fear na shakim ol i kamap long me, na horror i winim mi.
PSA 55:6 Mi tok, "O, mipela i gat wing olsem dove, Na mi go flap wing na kisim pes, mipela i pundaun na kisim res."
PSA 55:7 Em i go longwe na mi bai lus! Bai mi save stap long bus. Selah
PSA 55:8 Mi bai harim pas long haus bilong mi, longwe na farapela nau long dispela biknem win.
PSA 55:9 Papa bilong mipela, ol i bagarapim na palim tok bilong ol, wantaim mi lukim vailens na pait long ples.
PSA 55:10 De besen na nait ol i kamautim banis, wail malis na trabel i stap insait.
PSA 55:11 Bagarap i kam insait, na puripuri na bikim skel i nogat lusim stret.
PSA 55:12 Em i no inim na mekim olsem long me; mi inap bekim. Em i no poi na kamap strong long me; long em mi inap harim.
PSA 55:13 Em yu, man olsem mi yet, poroman bilong mi na fren balus bilong mi.
PSA 55:14 Mipela i sharim switpela felosip torete; mipela i wok wantaim ol pipel i go insait long haus bilong God.
PSA 55:15 Mande i kam bekim ol longpela taim; ol i go daun long hel long life yet, wantaim nogut i stap long ol hus.
PSA 55:16 Mi singaut long God, na LORD i savevim mi.
PSA 55:17 Bikos tumora, bek na nait, mipela i singaut long trabel, na Em i harim toktok bilong mipela.
PSA 55:18 Em i saveman soul bilong me long peis, long taim bilong faet, ol i kisim faet gen me, planti man i kam bek gen me.
PSA 55:19 God bai harim na yu ina shamem ol — Em i God we i stap long thrown bilong taim — Selah — bikos ol i no senis na ol i no gat respek long God.
PSA 55:20 Pasin bilong me i go bekim narafren bilong em, em i bagarap long promis bilong en.
PSA 55:21 Tok bilong em i swit olsem bata, tasol digma igris i stap insait long het bilong em. Wods bilong em i soft olsem oil, yet ol i makim na kisim aip na katim olsem sip.
PSA 55:22 Kisim bek na rulim i go long Holi Spirit, na em bai holim yu; em no bin givim man i kamap strong long ples, tasol em i stap strong olsem, em no ken lusim.
PSA 55:23 Bikos Yu, o God, bai kisim ol i go daun long hole bilong bagarap; man bilong shedim blod na bikhet, ol no ken stap na halv bilong taim bilong ol yet. Bai mi putim trast long Yu.
PSA 56:1 Long ol bosim singsing, long saund blong 'Pijin long Dok na Farawe'. Wanpela Miktam tok bilong Davit we em i skrivim tasol Philistines i kam kisim em long Gath. Bikim meri long me, o God, ol man i go bekim bekim long me; olgeta de ol i warkim war long me.
PSA 56:2 Enemi bilong mi i go bekim mi long oldei, wantaim planti man i kamap strong na bagarapim mi.
PSA 56:3 Wanpela taim mi les, mi putim trast bilong mi long Yu.
PSA 56:4 Long God, wanem wod bilong em mi praisim — long God mi putim trast. Mi no bin fear. Wanem man i ken mekim long mi?
PSA 56:5 Ol dei ol dei, yu salim tok bilong me i go raun; olgeta tingting bilong ol i stap long me i dai pinis.
PSA 56:6 Ol i tok birua, ol i stap bek long bus, ol i waitsim stet bilong mi, ol i w8 long kilim laip bilong mi.
PSA 56:7 Nogat long sin bilong ol, bai ol i go frei? Long rausim bilong yu, Bikpela God, kasl bilong nesen i dai.
PSA 56:8 Yu kisim kaunt long ol ples we mi go wail. Yu putim taeka bilong mi insait long botol bilong yu—ol i no stap insait long buk bilong yu?
PSA 56:9 Tasol enemy bilong me bai ranawe long dei mi kisim hap i go long beten, na mipela bai save olsem Bikpela i stap wantaim mi.
PSA 56:10 Long God, wos em i tokim story long em, na mi hamamas long tok bilong en, long LORD, wos em i tokim story long em, na mi hamamas long tok bilong en.
PSA 56:11 Bikos mipela trast long God; mipela no ken kisim fea. Wanem samting ol man i ken mekim long mipela?
PSA 56:12 Olegu bilong yu i stap long me, o God; bai mi go wailisim ofa bilong tankyu long yu.
PSA 56:13 Bikos yu tokautim ol save bilong me long dai, mitim ol fut bilong me long pilim i go daun, na inap long wokabaut wantaim God long laip bilong laif.
PSA 57:1 Long ol man i save song, long saond blong 'Yu no ken kilim'. Wanpela tok bilong Daud, Miktam, taim em i ranawe long Saul go insait kaev. Pigim belas long mi, o God, pigim belas, wantaim soul bilong mi i go kisim hap long yu. Long shade blong wing bilong yu, bai mi go kisim skel, till danger i pas.
PSA 57:2 Mi singaut long Bikpela God, long God we i givim purpus bilong em long me.
PSA 57:3 Em i kam daun dari heven, na i saveim mi; em i krosim ol i pulim i go daun long mi. Selah. God i salim kot long en, givim kat nating long tingting bilong em, na tok tru bilong em.
PSA 57:4 Soul bilong me i stap longpela lions; mi lain daun wantaim ol beasts we i gat bikpela hap — ol man we i gat tith bihain ol spea na arao, na tang buk ol i gat olsem sords i gat sharp.
PSA 57:5 Kam longwe na kamap strong, O God, we long hap bilong heven; glori bilong yu ken kaevim long holim erth.
PSA 57:6 Ol i kisim nep bilong net na putim long lek bilong mi; spirits bilong mi em i go daun, mi les. Ol i digim hole bifo mi, tasol ol yet i bin slip long em! Selah
PSA 57:7 Bel bilong me em i stap strong, o God, bel bilong me em i stap strong. Bai mi singim song na wokim musik.
PSA 57:8 Kam bek, glori bilong mi! Kam bek, o harp na laip! Mi bai kam bekim dawn.
PSA 57:9 Mipela bai praisim Yu, Papa God, long olgeta nesen; mipela bai singim sang bilong Yu long olgeta pipel.
PSA 57:10 Lovink nem bilong yu go long heven, na Fethfulnes bilong yu go long klaut.
PSA 57:11 Bikpela, yu kam longwe na kamap strong long hap bilong heven; glori bilong yu ken kambek i go antap long holim graun.
PSA 58:1 Long bilong bikman. Long saund blong 'Yu No Ken DistrOi'. Wanpela tok bilong Davit we em i skraitim. Yupela i tok stret long hem, ol bikman? Yupela ol pikinini manmeri i givim desisen long wei bilong trut?
PSA 58:2 Nogat, long ol bilong yufala yumi tingim i no jus; wantaim han bilong yufala yumi kisim strongpela pasin i go long graun.
PSA 58:3 Ol i nogut i stap wain long bel, na ol i givim lie i go daun long rot bilong tumbuna.
PSA 58:4 Poison bilong ol i laik poison bilong sip, olsem cobra i pakim eria bilong en.
PSA 58:5 I no lissen long saut bilong man bilong singsing, em i mekim magik bilong en.
PSA 58:6 O God, brukim olgeta tit bilong ol insait long maus bilong ol; O LORD, kamautim olgeta fang bilong ol laion.
PSA 58:7 Ol i go daun olsem wara i ran i go; na wannem ol i kilim banis, naip ol i pundaun i no inap katim.
PSA 58:8 Olsem slug i go daun long slip blong en, olsem pikinini i kamat ai still long bel blong mama, bai ol i no lukim sun.
PSA 58:9 Bipo kukim pot bilong yu i kamap long ol pakpak, em i gat grinn na drai, Em bai kisim ol i go long we.
PSA 58:10 Ol raitim man bai amamas long taim ol i lukim ol i kamap strong, ol bai wasim lek bilong ol long blod bilong ol i no gat laif.
PSA 58:11 Ol man bai tok, “Tru, retaitim bilong ol righteous i kamap strong long loa! Bikpela God i givim sentens long graun, na tok bilong en i no bihainim hevi, em i stap long jastis.”
PSA 59:1 Long taim bilong song leader. Long saund blong 'Yu No Ken DistrOi'. Wanpela tok bilong Davit we em i skrivim, wanpela taim Saul salim ol man i go wachim house bilong Davit, oli laik kilim em. Bikim me fri long enemy bilong me, o God bilong mi; protekim mi long ol man i kam ap genston mi.
PSA 59:2 Baim yu save me long ol workman bilong nogut, na saveim mi long ol man bilong shedim blod.
PSA 59:3 Ol i stap bihain i go long me. Ol man pikinini i wok long tromoi long me, maski mi no bin mekim giaman o sin, O Papa bilong yumiyumi.
PSA 59:4 Long wei nau, mi no bin mekim dispela, ol i kam hariap long paitim mi. Kam daun na halivim mi, kisim notis.
PSA 59:5 O Lod Gaga bilong ol paitim, Goda bilong Israel, kam bek gen na paitim ol narapela nesen; no givim klosap long ol bikhet na traitors i no gat tru. Selah
PSA 59:6 Ol i kam bek long apinun, ol garm bilong ol mama dog, na ol wokabaut olgeta long siti.
PSA 59:7 Lukeim ol i kirapim long maus bilong ol - wods bilong pait bilong ol i kam long lip bilong ol: "Bilong husat ina i harim mipela?"
PSA 59:8 Bikpela, yu givim tok bis long ol; Yu kisim ol narapela kantri i go long hap.
PSA 59:9 Mipela bai waitim yu, o bikpela strong bilong mi, wantaim yu em i bikpela kota bilong mi, o God.
PSA 59:10 Bikpela God bilong mi, em i kam bikos em i gat lovwantaim long mi; God bai mekim mi lukim ol i no save long ol eni.
PSA 59:11 No ken kilim ol, piple bilong mi bai lusim. Windim ol i go long pawa bilong yu, na bringim ol i daun, O Lode, shield bilong yumi.
PSA 59:12 Long sin bilong maus bilong ol, na long tok bilong lip bilong ol, bai ol i go insait long praid bilong ol, long katarius na lies ol i tok, na ol i no inap kom out, bikos ol i mas bekim responsibol long tok bilong ol.
PSA 59:13 Kaikai ol i go long pisinis bilong rausim; kaikai ol til ol i no stap, olsem em i klia long olgeta hap bilong graun olsem God i bos bilong Yakob. Selah
PSA 59:14 Ol i kam bek long apinun, ol i guriguri olsem dog, na ol i wokabaut long siti.
PSA 59:15 Ol sahen long graun bilong kaikai, na ol givim rausim sori tok if tedei no inap.
PSA 59:16 Bai mipela singautim strong bilong yu, na tokautim gutpela laip bilong yu long moning, wantaim yu em i fortress bilong mi, na ples bilong mi long taim bilong trabel.
PSA 59:17 Long yu, o Bikpela kot bilong mi, mipela singim sang bilong preis, wantaim yu em i fortress bilong mi, o God, yu em i bikpela loviservis bilong mi.
PSA 60:1 Long bilong mana meri i save sing. Long saund blong “Lili blong Kovena”. Miktam blong Davide long ol lusi. Taim em i faet Aram-naharaim na Aram-zobah, na Joab i kam bek na i kilim 12,000 Edomait long Vali blong Sol. Yu rimsim mipela, O God; Yu bin brukim mipela; Yu bel kol; strongim mipela gen!
PSA 60:2 Yu shakim graun na yu pullum i op. Healim olgeta brukna pasal, bikos olsem graun i stap long tremble.
PSA 60:3 Yu bin mekim pikinini belong yu karim hevi, mipela i stap bek long wain yu givim mipela dring.
PSA 60:4 Yu go puti up em i go hap bilong flag long ol i bikpela bagarap na i save, olsem oli ken ranawe long banis. Selah
PSA 60:5 Givim tok na savim mipela wantaim han bilong yu, na ol manmeri yu stap laikim, ol i ken kamap strong.
PSA 60:6 God i tok from hause lotu: "Mi bai winim! Mi bai givim Sukem long ol pipol, na mi bai dividim Vali of Sukkot.
PSA 60:7 Gilead i bilong mi, na Manase i bilong mi; Efrayim em i het bilong mi, Judah em i szepta bilong mi.
PSA 60:8 Moab emi basin bilong mi; long Edom mi kisim sandal bilong mi na putim i go daun; long Philistia mi singautim win long hap.
PSA 60:9 Husat bai kisim mi go long siti i gat barik? Husat bai lidim mi go long Edom?
PSA 60:10 O God, yu no tromoiim mipela? Bai yu no go bek long ples bilong war wantaim ol soza bilong mipela?
PSA 60:11 Givim mipela hep long enemy, olgeta hap bilong man i no gat bek.
PSA 60:12 Wantaim Bikpela God bai yumi warkim wantaim bravi, na em bai krungim poitpinis bilong yumi.
PSA 61:1 Long taem bilong song leader. Wanpela taim yu usim instrument bilong string. Bilong Dauid. Harim tok bilong mi, O God; yu kam long na harim prea bilong mi.
PSA 61:2 Long wei na graun mipela i kolim Yu wanken oltaim hap bilong mipela i dai pinis. Lusim mipela i go long rok we i bigpela moa long mipela.
PSA 61:3 Long taim yu bin stap ples bilong hariap bilong mi, na yu stap strong olsem wanpela bau bilong strong against ol poisen.
PSA 61:4 Mipela i mas stap long haus bilong yu foreva na mipela i go bek long ples bilong scara bilong wing bilong yu. Selah
PSA 61:5 Yu harim tok bilong mi, o God; yu givim mi hamas long graun bilong ol i tekeda namel bilong Yu.
PSA 61:6 Kisim i go longpela taim bilong laif bilong Bikman, na yia bilong en i go long olsem genarashon olgeta.
PSA 61:7 Em i mas sit long throne bilong en long ples bilong God oltaim; apointim lok olgeta bilong yu na trast bilong yu i lukautim em.
PSA 61:8 Mi bai singim prais long nem bilong yu oltaim, na mi bai kamapim promis bilong mi dei bihain dei.
PSA 62:1 Long bikman bilong singaut. Ol i tok: Jedutun, wan man bilong Solomon taim. Wan Sang bilong Davit. Long God tasol, spirit bilong mi i stap kaikai; saveman bilong mi i kam bek long Hem.
PSA 62:2 Em i rok bilong mi tasol na saveman bilong mi; em i bai hap bilong mi, na mi no ken shake long taim olgeta.
PSA 62:3 Olamau bai yu pilim tok strong long man olsem wal ibin katim i go daun? Yupela olgeta bai pusim daun im olsem banis ibin kalap?
PSA 62:4 Ol i laikim tru long kisim daun im long ples bilong paowa o prestis; ol i amamas long tok pis; long maus bilong ol, ol i blesim, tasol long bel insait bilong ol, ol i karim kurse. Selah
PSA 62:5 Ki stap i go long God tasol, o spirits bilong me, wantaim hop bilong me i kam from Him.
PSA 62:6 Em i rok bilong me na salvesen bilong me; Em i fortress bilong me; mi no bai katim.
PSA 62:7 Salvesen bilong me na hanar bilong me i stap long God, em i rok strong bilong me; ples bilong mi hide em i God.
PSA 62:8 Putim traust long Em long taim olgeta, o piple; kamautim het bilong yu bifo Em. God em i stap refij long yumi. Selah
PSA 62:9 Man i kam long ples i go daun ol i nosave olsem smok, na ol i go hap long hevi em i dispela em i no tru. Taim ol i go we bilong skel, ol i go antap, tasol ol tu ol i go daun olsem smok.
PSA 62:10 No ken trust long moni i kam long bikim ol man i bagarap, o gat hope i no truth long samting ol i stilim. Sapos yu gat planti moni, no putim heart bilong yu long ol.
PSA 62:11 God i tok wanpela taim; Mi hia harim dispela tupela taim: strong i bilong God,
PSA 62:12 Na mipela i gat lav wantaim devosin long yu, o Papa bilong mipela, wantaim yu bai givim bek long ol man olsem wok bilong en tasol.
PSA 63:1 Sang bilong Dauid wankain taem em i stap long Wik Bus long Yuda. O God, yu em i bikpela bilong mi. Mi go long yu stret wantaim; soul bilong mi em i masalai long yu. Bodi bilong mi em i pilim strong long yu long kantri drai na i no gat wara.
PSA 63:2 Mi bin lukim Yu long ples namel na behim strongpela bilong yu na glori bilong yu.
PSA 63:3 Bikos Yu laikim olsem i gutpela long olgeta samting, maus bilong mi bai givim ples na han long yu.
PSA 63:4 Mi blesim Yu olsem long olsem mi stap; long nem bilong Yu mi lifim han bilong mi.
PSA 63:5 Soul bilong me i amamas olgeta long ka bilong gudepela kai; lip narakai bilong me, mouth bilong me bai singautim sang i praisim Yu.
PSA 63:6 Mi rimembirim Yu long bet bilong mi, na mi tink long Yu long waches bilong nait.
PSA 63:7 Yu yet yu helpim mi; mi bai singim song bilong jalos long saed bilong wing bilong Yu.
PSA 63:8 Soul bilong mi i klostu long yu; han rait bilong yu em i holim mi.
PSA 63:9 Bai ol i lukim laif bilong mi i mekim em i no stap, bai ol i go daun long hap graun.
PSA 63:10 Ol i pitim long powa bilong sward, na ol bai kamap ka long fox.
PSA 63:11 King bai amamas long God; olgeta hhu masalai long em i hap bilong en, bikos maus bilong ol bikman bai i stap kutim.
PSA 64:1 Long man i save dirigen ol sing. Psalm bilong Davit. Harim, o God, voys bilong me; saveman laif bilong me long tremol bilong eni.
PSA 64:2 Kamdai mipela i holim mi long tok bokis bilong ol wokman bilong hevi, long graun bilong ol wokman bilong hevi.
PSA 64:3 Ol i sapim toktok bilong ol olsem sord na ol i tanim tok harit bilong ol olsem banarrows,
PSA 64:4 Ol i ambushim ol narapela i no bin mekim rong long ples i stap isolet, na bai ol i paitim gunshot harimol, na ol i no bin gat fea.
PSA 64:5 Ol i holim strong long pikinini bilong ol i go long wei bilong nogut; ol i taktok long kaivim snares bilong ol. “Husat bai lukim ol?” ol i tok.
PSA 64:6 Ol i tokautim hevi bilong mekim kol, ol i tok, "Mipela imas perfektem wanpela plan i no moa klia long eni man." Bilong insait i go, na het bilong man i go, em i dai kisim save.
PSA 64:7 Bikos God i go kotim ol long banarang; nupela bai ol kisim suk.
PSA 64:8 Ol i pundaun, tung bilong ol yet i turnim gen long ol. Ol i lukim, na ol i kisim hed bilong ol i shakem.
PSA 64:9 Olgeta manmeri bai fearim, kukim tok bilong wok bilong God, na tingim strong long dispela ol samting em i mekim.
PSA 64:10 Ol i stap raite i mas laikim long Bikpela na yu mas go bek long Em; ol Getty long haret i mas laikim.
PSA 65:1 Long ol bos bilong singsing. Wanpela sang bilong Davit. Praiz i stap waitim Yu, o God, long Zion; ol promis bilong mipela bai kam true long yu.
PSA 65:2 Yu husat i harim bikpela prea, olgeta manmeri bai kam long yu.
PSA 65:3 Taim bilong hevi i kam ants long me, Yupela i kisim bek long sindaun bilong yumi.
PSA 65:4 Blesim i kam long wanpela yu pikinim, kisim na bringim klostu long stop olsem insait long haus kot bilong yu! Mipela i fulap long gutpela bilong haus bilong yu, holi bilong templa bilong yu.
PSA 65:5 Long wok bung long tromoi na jastis, Yu ansa mipela, o God bilong sevensesen blong mipela, hope blong olgeta hap bilong graun, na solwara i go daun olsem.
PSA 65:6 Yu bin mekim maunten long pawa, na yu bin katim strong long yu yet.
PSA 65:7 Yu stilim strongpela sai bilong solwara, kikim bilong waves ol i go, na gulpmol bilong ol narapela kantri.
PSA 65:8 Ol pipol we i stap farawe i fearim wonda bilong yu; Yu mekim moning na san i go daun singautim hap bilong en.
PSA 65:9 Yu kisim hevi long graun na givim wara long en; long planti yu givim ka bilong en. Wara bilong God i fulap long wara, bikos yu preparim ka bilong mipela long givim provisen long graun.
PSA 65:10 Yu wetim graun bilong en, yu flattenim hap bilong en; Yu mekim em soft olgeta wantaim ren, yu givim berekari long en i karim ka.
PSA 65:11 Yu kam bekim yia wantaim hamamas, na rod bilong yu i overflow long planti ka.
PSA 65:12 Graun bilong bus em i kamap strongim, ol maunten i kisim laip long hapines.
PSA 65:13 Graun i kamap na ol sok na bulmakau i kalapim, na ol vales i pulap wantaim ka. Ol i singautim lole na ol i singsing.
PSA 66:1 Wokim saut i kamap strong long Jehovah! Olgets long graun, wokim saut i kamap strong ki long God!
PSA 66:2 Singim glorim bilong nem bilong En; mekim praisim bilong En i glori.
PSA 66:3 Tokim long God, “Wanem samting yu mekim em i amamas! Yu gat bikpela strong, ol poisin i skulim long yu.”
PSA 66:4 Olgeta graun i go daun long yu; ol i singim sang bilong preis long yu; ol i singim sang bilong preis long nem bilong yu. Selah
PSA 66:5 Kam na lukim wok bilong God; ol samting em i mekim i amamas long ol manmeri.
PSA 66:6 Em i bin mekim solwara i kamap graun; ol i bin pas long wara, ol i go heneng long lek; long hap bilong en, yumi i amamas long en.
PSA 66:7 Em i bos bilong taim olgeta bai yu usim pawa; ai bilong en i lukim ol nesen. No ken letim ol pipol i bagarap i kamap strong. Selah
PSA 66:8 Blessim God bilong yumui, o ol pipel; saut bilong prize bilong em i kamap klia.
PSA 66:9 Em i save laif bilong yumi na em i stapim lek bilong yumi long slip.
PSA 66:10 Bikos yu, O God, yu traiim mipela; yu pilim mipela olsem silva.
PSA 66:11 Yu bringim mipela long net; Yu putim bikpela pe bilong yap bilong mipela long bek bilong mipela.
PSA 66:12 Yu lusim ol man i go antap long hed bilong yumi; yumi i go insait long faia na wara, tasol Yu bringim yumi i kam insait long plenti.
PSA 66:13 Mipela bai go insait long haus bilong yu wantaim ofa bilong bun; mipela bai kamapim bekim promis bilong mipela long yu.
PSA 66:14 Ol promis i go bek long maus bilong mi, na maus bilong mi i tokim ol dispela long taim bilong trabel bilong mi.
PSA 66:15 Mipela bai ofaim yu ol pikinini bilong ol bulmakau i stap gutpela olsem sakrament burn monop, wantaim smok bilong ram i kam strong; mipela bai ofa bulmakau na kengim goat. Selah
PSA 66:16 Kam na harim tok, yumi ol i gat respek long God, na mi bai tokim ol samting em i mekim long me.
PSA 66:17 Mi kisim aut i goap long Em wantaim maus bilong mi, na mi praisim Em wantaim tus bilong mi.
PSA 66:18 Mi go hap bilong mi long hevi, Papa God bai no harim tok bilong mi.
PSA 66:19 Bikpela God em i harim tok bilong mi, em i kam long herim saut bilong beten bilong mi.
PSA 66:20 Bikim tok blesim long God, em i no salim praer bilong me, na em i no holim bak luv laki bilong en!
PSA 67:1 Long ol i go manager bilong sing. Wanpela song long ol instrument bilong string. Wanpela sang bilong Psalm. Wanpela song. Mipela i hop Bikpela bai givim mipela graun na blesim mipela, na makim pes bilong em i shine uponus, Selah
PSA 67:2 Na ol i save long wei bilong yu long graun, ol saveman bilong yu ibelong ol narapela ples.
PSA 67:3 Ol pipol bai givim prais long yu, o God; olgeta pipol bai givim prais long yu.
PSA 67:4 Nesen i ambai hap hap na singim song bilong gladnes, long bikos Yu jijim pisinini ol pipol wei fare na yu lidim nesen ol long graun. Selah
PSA 67:5 Ol pipol bai givim prais long Yu, o God; olgeta pipol bai givim prais long Yu.
PSA 67:6 Gro na i givim ka; Bikpela, em i bikpela bilong yumi, em i givim blessing long yumi.
PSA 67:7 Gott i givim blessing long mipela, olgeta hap bilong wol i go ken kirap long Em.
PSA 68:1 Long tisa bilong sang. Psalm bilong Daud. Wanpela sang. Bikpela i kamap, na eni nemigo bilong em i sindaun, olsem man i no likim em i ranawe long ples bilong em.
PSA 68:2 Olsem smok i go daun, Yu bai driva ol i go; olsem waks i pen long paia, ol bikhet na ol i dai long wei bilong God.
PSA 68:3 Dai na stret bai hapim na singsing, ol i kisim part long celebreten na hamamas long ai bilong Bikpela.
PSA 68:4 Singim sang long God! Singim praisim long nem bilong Em. Liftim up Em i go antap long klau—nem bilong Em ol i kolim Bikpela—and amamas long em.
PSA 68:5 Papa bilong ol pikinini we i no gat papa, na wan man i save lukautim meri we husband i dai, em i God long ples bilong em we em i stap holy.
PSA 68:6 God i stap ikisim ol pipol we i stap wantaim nogat long pela famili; Em i laisim ol prisen long go long gutpela taim, tasol ol i no lissen i stap long kantri we san i katim.
PSA 68:7 O God, taim yu go bifor piple bilong yu, taim yu i go bek long ples nogut, Selah
PSA 68:8 Gras i shake, na heven i kisim rain i kam daun bifor God, Wan we i stap long Sainai, bifor God, God bilong Israel.
PSA 68:9 Yu, Bikpela, salim rains plenti, na yu givim bak streng long ol pipol bilong yu, olsem inheritance i go daun, we i bin tirid.
PSA 68:10 Ol pikinini bilong yu i stap olsem long hap; o God, long planti ka bilong yu, yu givim ka long ol pikinini nogut.
PSA 68:11 Papa God i givim tok; mipela meri olgeta i kirapim dispela tok.
PSA 68:12 Kings na ol solja bilong ol i ran i go hapkas; meri em i stap wait long haus i dipositim ol lo.
PSA 68:13 Maski yu lidau long haus kukim ol pipel, wing bilong piji i kamap gen silver, na plum bilong em i shine olsem gol.
PSA 68:14 Taim Bikpela God i skaterim ol kings long kantri, em i olsem snou i pundaun long Zalmon.
PSA 68:15 Maunten bilong God em i Maunten Basan; maunten i gat plenti pekis em i Maunten Basan.
PSA 68:16 Wai yusim kisim ai bilong jalim, o maunten i gat planti pek? Dispela maunten em i nau husat God i bikim em i stap, na Bikpela bai stap oltaim long hap.
PSA 68:17 Kar i God olsem ten thousand – thousand of thousand, Papa God i stap long tempele bilong en olsem em i bin stap long Maunten Sinai.
PSA 68:18 Yu go ap long hai; Yu pilim bek prisna na karim i go. Yu kisim gif olsem moni na samting bilong ol man, ol i no odomol, ol i birua, na Bikpela God, Pita bilong heaven, bai i stap hap there.
PSA 68:19 Praiz i go long Lod, hu i karim bel hevi bilong yumi long ol dei, God bilong saveman bilong yumi. Selah
PSA 68:20 Bikpela God bilong yusim mipela, Lod God em i save mipela long dai.
PSA 68:21 God bai bagarap ol hed bilong ol i no likim, ol krown bilong ol i gat gras bilong ol i stap long wok bilong gui.
PSA 68:22 Papa God i tok, "Mipela bai karim ol i go bek long Bashan, mipela bai kisim ol i kam bek long bubung bilong solwara."
PSA 68:23 Foot bilong yu bai go daun istap long bloo bilong enimi bilong yu – tongues bilong daks bilong yu tu, olsem.
PSA 68:24 Ol i lukim prosesions bilong yu, o God—march bilong God bilong mi na King go insait long templa.
PSA 68:25 Singers i go bifor, musishians i folo bihain, long ol meri i pilai tamburin.
PSA 68:26 Blessim God long bikpela assembli; blessim LORD long bun bilong Israel.
PSA 68:27 Benjamin i stap, em i nambawan pikinini, em i bosim ol, prins bilong Yuda ol i kam wantaim ol, prins bilong Zebulun na Naphtali.
PSA 68:28 Tokim Bikpela, kisim i go ketrang bilong yu; showim strong bilong yu, olsem yu usim long halivim mipela.
PSA 68:29 Bikos long Haus Lotu bilong yu long Jerusalem, king i bai bringim ofa na pagi ol i go long yu.
PSA 68:30 Krosim bek long beast long rip, grup bilong bulmakau long midst bilong liklik bulmakau bilong ol nesen, na i kam daun, kisim bar bilong silva i kam, until em i stap i go daun. Troweim ol nesen i amamas long war.
PSA 68:31 Misisi bai kam from Ejip; Kas bai stilim han bilong en long Bikpela.
PSA 68:32 Singim sang long God, o kingdom bilong graun; singim prais long Lod—Selah
PSA 68:33 Em i rais long heven hevi bilong taim bifo; behold, vosis bilong en i strong na i kom bek gen.
PSA 68:34 Givim powa long God, husat majesti i go long ol Israel, husat strong i kamap long heven.
PSA 68:35 O God, yu em i bikpela tru long haus lotu; God bilong Israel em yet i givim strong na pawa long ol pipol. Blessing i kam long God!
PSA 69:1 Long ol bos bilong sang. Long song bilong 'Lilim'. Bilong Dauid. Savesim mi, o God, bikos wata i go klosap long nek bilong mi.
PSA 69:2 Mi go daun long olgeta hap graun, ples bilong stan i no stap; mi husat i drift long solwara i depele, banis i kalapim mi.
PSA 69:3 Mi les long taitim; wanpela het bilong mi i drai pinis. Mai i dai, laiken bilong Bikpela.
PSA 69:4 Ol i hatim mi bai nogat risin, ol i bikpela olsem gras bilong hed bilong mi; ol i laik kilim mi, ol i birua long me nogat gutpela resin. Mi no stilim, tasol mi mas peim bek.
PSA 69:5 Yu save long olgeta olsem na gilt bilong mi i no hidim igo long Yu.
PSA 69:6 Ol pipol i hop tumas long Yu, bai mipela i no bilong kisim shame bikosim mi, O Lod God bilong ol ples; na ol pipol i go bek long Yu, bai mipela i no gat shame bikosim mi, O God bilong Israel.
PSA 69:7 Mi go i stap long ol kalangai long nem bilong Yu, na shem i go kambek long ples bilong mi.
PSA 69:8 Mi kamap man i no save long ol brata bilong mi, na man i stap long kantri i no bilong em, ol pikinini bilong mama bilong mi.
PSA 69:9 Kros long Haus bilong Yu em i bin katim mi, na ol pikinini toksave long ol pipel i no givim respek long Yu em i pinis kamdaun long mi.
PSA 69:10 Mi kisim sor na mi bikim kaikai nogut, tasol em i bringim shame long me.
PSA 69:11 Mi putim sakklot olsem klos bilong mi, na ol i laik long me.
PSA 69:12 Ol pipol i save sit long gait bilong ples, yu laik pilim shame long me, na mi stap song bilong ol dringol.
PSA 69:13 Mipela prai long yu, o Bikpela, em i kam long taim bilong graz. Long bikpela lavu bilong yu, o Bikpela, givim mipela ansa wantaim sevensesen bilong yu.
PSA 69:14 Bailim mi long marasin, no ken givim mi go daun; kisim mi long ol man i no laikim mi, na longpela wara i go daun.
PSA 69:15 No ken olgeta wata i kam daun long me, na graun i no katim me i go insait; Pit i no ken klosim maus bilong en long me.
PSA 69:16 Bikim tok long me, Papa God, bikos gupuna bilong yu em i gutpela; wokim faced bilong yu i kam long me olsem bikpela karem bilong yu.
PSA 69:17 Kamautim face bilong yu i no go long mi, nauspel bilong mi, bikos mi stap long tribulesen. Givim mi ansa bikos!
PSA 69:18 Kam klostu long sol bilong mi, ransomeim mi; peilim prais bilong mi, bekim ol iet long ol waitman bilong mi.
PSA 69:19 Yu save long me nau, olsem nem bilong me i go daun, meso, shame na bekimai bilong mi. Ol man i no likim mi, ol i stap bifo yu.
PSA 69:20 Ol kat kat i bin brukim bel bilong me, na mi stap long sutim hus. Mi go lukisim klostu, tasol mi no finaisim, mi painim ol i givim klostu, tasol mipela i no gat.
PSA 69:21 Ol i poinim ka ka bilong mi long gali, na ol i givim mi viniga ofa trink we.
PSA 69:22 Mipela hop tumora bilong ol i kamapim santing i givim pain long ol, na em i kamapim penati na pasis long ol.
PSA 69:23 Mai ai bilong ol i kamap strong na ol i no inap lukim, na baks bilong ol i kalap i go long taim.
PSA 69:24 Birua bilong yu, Kisim i go long ol, na pait imas bilong yu lusi tumas i kam behain long ol.
PSA 69:25 Ples bilong ol i mas stap klia; nogat man i ken stap insait long haus bilong ol.
PSA 69:26 Ol i persekutim man bilong yu, na tokim pait bilong ol iyu wundim.
PSA 69:27 Tingim bagarap long ol, na bai ol i no inap kisim ribat long righteousness bilong yu.
PSA 69:28 Ol i no inap long Buk Bilong Laip, na ol i no ken skruim namel long namel bilong ol righteous.
PSA 69:29 Mi stap i go insait pain na trouble; O God bilong mipela, bai saveman bilong yu, save mipela.
PSA 69:30 Mi bai singim sang bilong prais long Nem bilong God, na mi bai liftim em up wantaim tang yu.
PSA 69:31 Na dispela bai bringim moa gladi long tok bilong God, moa yet long olsem ak, moa yet long olsem bulmakau wantaim het na fut.
PSA 69:32 Ol semak i go senis na kilim hap. Yupela husat i sakim God, inap yu bel isi kam ap gen!
PSA 69:33 Bikpela i harim ol i nogat samting na i no kilim bin ol pipol i kisim long het bilong en.
PSA 69:34 Heven na graun bai givim prais long Em, solwara na olgeta samting i moa insait long ol.
PSA 69:35 God bai saveim Zion na bai rebuildim sities bilong Judah, olsem na ol bai stap dai na ol bai kisim.
PSA 69:36 Ol desendan bilong servan bilong Em bai ineritem klostu, na ol man meri i givim respek long nem bilong En bai stap insait long en.
PSA 70:1 Long ol bos bilong sang. Bilong Daubid. Bringim bek memori. Harim yu, o God, bai yu saveman me! Hariap, o Lod, bai yu halivim mi!
PSA 70:2 Ol husat i sakim laip bilong mi, bai ol i krosim na skulim; na ol husat i laik mekim olsem long mi, bai ol i tambuai na bagarap tru.
PSA 70:3 Ol i go tok, 'Aha, aha!' ina lusim bek long shem bilong ol.
PSA 70:4 Ol pipel we sakim Yu, bai hamamas na glat long Yu; na ol pipel we lovim salvishen bilong Yu, bai tok, 'GOD i go antap nogut!'
PSA 70:5 Mi bikpela i no gut, na mi i nidim; harim long kom bek long meik, o God. Yu yet em i halivim mi, na yu yet em i savim mi, o Bikpela, no ken slip.
PSA 71:1 Long yu, o Bikpela, mi go kam na kisim hap bilong mi; mi no inshem long taim bai.
PSA 71:2 Long stret bilong yu, sikim na saveman mi; kisim han bilong yu na harim tok bilong mi, saveman mi.
PSA 71:3 Kam na bem rock bilong refijim mi, we bilong mi inap go daunol. Givim tok bilong sev me, bikos yu em i rock bilong refijim mi, na fortres bilong difens bilong mi.
PSA 71:4 Baim yu save me, o God bilong mi, long han bilong ol raskol, long pinis bilong ol i no gat jastis na ol i bagarap.
PSA 71:5 Yu em i hope bilong mi, O Lod God, konfides bilong mi long taim bipo, statim bilong yut.
PSA 71:6 Mi go bek long yu sins mi born; Yu kam bekim mi long bel bilong mama bilong mi. Praise bilong mi i stap olsem long yu.
PSA 71:7 Mi kamap nau ol i save pem na tok long mi, tasol Yu yet ples bilong mi i go inap long yu.
PSA 71:8 Maus bilong me i fulap wantaim preis bilong yu, na wantaim glori bilong yu, long oldei.
PSA 71:9 No ken kukim mi long taim mi bilong ples olsem; no lusim mi long taim bodi mi i no inap wok gen.
PSA 71:10 Ol i tok birua long me, na ol i w8 long laif bilong me, ol i plan long kilim mi.
PSA 71:11 “God i lusim em; bihainim em na kisim em, long olgeta em i no gat narapela man i save helim em.”
PSA 71:12 O Bikpela bilong mi, no inap longwe nau. Olen i go hariap long helpim mi.
PSA 71:13 Ol i tok besig long spirit blong me, bai ol i kisim sham na katol long ol; na ol i laik mekim olsem long me, bai ol i kapul long sham na susa.
PSA 71:14 Mi bai hop yet long taim, na mi bai givim prais long yu i go yet moa.
PSA 71:15 Maus bilong me bai tokim jastis na sipios bilong yu long oldei, maski mi no inap save holimpas bilong ol.
PSA 71:16 Mi bai go insait long strong bilong Lod God; mi bai tokaut justis bilong yu — bilong yu tasol.
PSA 71:17 O Bikpela, yu laik traiim mi long taim bifo, taem bilong yut, na inap long dispela de, mi wail bekim Wok bilong yu, em i mak bilong admiral.
PSA 71:18 Na mi bai iatim na graun, yet, yu no ken lusim mi, O God, long wei na mi kamap tokautim pawa bilong yu long ol genarashen i go bek, stren bilong yu long ol i kam bihain.
PSA 71:19 Raitim bilong yu kamap long heven, o God, yu we i mekim wok bikpela. Hu, o God, i olsem yu?
PSA 71:20 Yu bin mekim mi lukim planti trabel na ogreta, tasol Yu yet bai bringim mi bek gen long laip. Yu bai kam bek gen long hap, yu yet bai bringim mi bek gen long laip, even long daunponda long graun.
PSA 71:21 Yu bai bringim mi go hap, strongim mi gen, na yu kam comfortim mi gen, na yu strongim gutpela nem bilong mi.
PSA 71:22 Mi bai givim sankam long Yu wantaim hap long féthfulnes bilong Yu, o God bilong mi; mi bai singim sang long Yu wantaim lai, o Wan Holide bilong Israel.
PSA 71:23 Mipela singim sang bembe long yu, lip bilong mipela bai karim bikmus jo, long naip bilong mipela, yu bin bekim.
PSA 71:24 Tang bilong mi bai toktru bikos yu rait, na ol i wokim ol samting nogut long mi, bai ol i skulim, na kros long ol samting, ol i go bek gen, jus bikos yu rait long ol dei.
PSA 72:1 Bilong Solomon. Givim kingpela i go long yumi na jusis bilong yu, na susa bilong king i go long yumi na righteousnes bilong yu.
PSA 72:2 Em i mas jugisim piple bilong yu long jastis, na ol pikinini bilong yu ol i siki, em i givim jastis long ol.
PSA 72:3 Maunten na hils ina bringim pis na jus long pipol.
PSA 72:4 Em i mas givim rait long ol i sufakai, savim pikinini bilong ol i no gat moni, na daurim ol bagarap.
PSA 72:5 Ol i mas savingim em long oltaim san i stap shain, long oltaim mun i stap, ribong long olgenereisen.
PSA 72:6 Em i laik ren, olsem ren bilong moning i kam wasim graun, em i laik ren bilong moning i wasim erth.
PSA 72:7 Ol rait i go strong long taim bilong em, planti gudpela samting i kamap, toksave long taim bai mun i no inap kam bek gen.
PSA 72:8 Em i mas bos long solwara na solwara, na long Eurates na go long ol ende bilong graun.
PSA 72:9 Ol pipol i go wail long bus bilong en i mas kisim daun bung long en, na enemi bilong en i mas pisin graun.
PSA 72:10 King bilong Tarshish na ol ples i stap farawe long solwara, bai ol i bringim pi; king bilong Sheba na Seba, bai ol i kisim samting bilong givim.
PSA 72:11 Ol kingly ol i go daun long en, na olgeta nesen i servim en.
PSA 72:12 Em bai savim narakain man i kisim aut na krai, na man i suffa igat no hap bilong en.
PSA 72:13 Em bai givim kompassion long ol i no gat samting na ol i nidim help, na em bai savim laip bilong ol i spasim.
PSA 72:14 Em bai pilim bek ol long taim bilong presen na Strong, wantaim blod bilong ol i stap strong long ai bilong em.
PSA 72:15 Em i mas long olsem! Mipi bilong Sheba, em bai givim i go long en olsem gift. Ol manmeri i mas beten bek long en; ol i mas givim bikpela tok long en olde long de.
PSA 72:16 Mai planti graun i kamap long kantri; bai em i skulim na stap antap long maunten. Bai plante bilong em, olsem ka bilong frut, i kamap strong olsem bus bilong Lebanon, na ol manmeri bilong em olsem gras bilong ples.
PSA 72:17 Na nem bilong en bai i stap oltaim, na nem bilong en bai i go oltaim olsem san bai i shine; long hem, ol nesen i ken blesim, ol i ken kisim em oli wantaim.
PSA 72:18 Papa God bilong Israel, em yet i mekim wok strongpela, i gat bikpela bikpela blessin.
PSA 72:19 Blessim bikos nem bilong em i glori, mipela hop olgeta graun i kamap fulap long gloribillong em. Amen na amen.
PSA 72:20 Na kamapim prea bilong Davide sambai bilong Iese.
PSA 73:1 Sang bilong Asaf. Siam, God i givim gutpela samting long Israel, long ol man meri husat klia bilong harim i stap.
PSA 73:2 Long me, feet bilong me i go daun nex, tasol; steppim bilong me i go slip, tasol.
PSA 73:3 Mi envious long ol pipel i gat bikhet tasol mi lukim strongpela laif blong ol pipel i no gat laif.
PSA 73:4 Ol i no inap harim tok long taim bilong ol i dai; bodi bilong ol i stap strong na gut.
PSA 73:5 Ol i fri long ol pekpek, na ol i no inap kisim bek long narapela manmeri.
PSA 73:6 Praida em i kol arapela bilong ol; klos bilong strongim em i kaparaunim ol.
PSA 73:7 Long moninga bilong ol i kam, toksave bilong hart bilong ol i go i go, bai ol i wok long hevi, long bikim ol samting nogut.
PSA 73:8 Ol i laifim na ol tok bilong nogut, wantaim ol i thraten long mekim bagarap na paitim het.
PSA 73:9 Ol i putim maus bilong ol iwe long heven, na toksave bilong ol i go stret long graun.
PSA 73:10 Ol pipol bilong ol i kam bek long dispela ples na dringim waesa long planti.
PSA 73:11 Ol bikhet ol tok, "God i gat save long wanem? Bikpela i gat save?"
PSA 73:12 Lukim, dispela ol yet i nogut – olsem taim ol i stap fri long tok, na ol i save planti moni.
PSA 73:13 Mipela kim bekim hart bilong mipela i klia, emas, na mipela wasim han bilong mipela long nogut pasim, tasol olgeta i go long ken.
PSA 73:14 Mi skul olde long taim, na ol i pilim mi long moning.
PSA 73:15 Mi bai tok olsem, den mi bai bagarapim pikinini bilong yu.
PSA 73:16 Taim mi laik saveman, em i bikim hevi long ai bilong mi
PSA 73:17 Na mi go insait long hause lotu bilong God, na mi kisim save long wok nakimol long ol.
PSA 73:18 Yu wail pilama ol long graun i slip; Yu pilim ol i daun long hap bilong bagarap.
PSA 73:19 Ol i bagarap pinis, ol i pusimapim na i go long terrors!
PSA 73:20 Olsem wan man i kam bek long stap bilong dreem, Papa bilong ol, yu kam bek na bagarapim skinpela bilip long bodi bilong ol.
PSA 73:21 Wanpela taim bel bilong me i sori, na mi go harim bek long insait,
PSA 73:22 Mi no save, mi olsem animal nogut bifo yu.
PSA 73:23 Mi stap olsem yu yet; Yu holim han ratt bilong mi.
PSA 73:24 Yu usim toktok bilong yu ledim mi, na bihain yu bekim mi long glori.
PSA 73:25 Mi gat haiwe nau long heven bek yu, na long graun mi nogat laikim wan man besides yu.
PSA 73:26 Bodimi na het bilong me inogat strong, tasol God em i stap long strengim het bilong me, na em i porson bilong me foreva.
PSA 73:27 Ol i go longwe na You, bai ol i dai klostu; you i bagarapim ol i no trusim yu.
PSA 73:28 Bareket, em i gutpela long mi long go klostu long God. Mi bin mekim Lord GOD bilong me olsem ples bilong birua, na mi ken announcim ol wok bilong yu.
PSA 74:1 Maskil bilong Asaf. Wai yusim ol i no laikim mipela foreva, o God? Wai bel hat bik na i stap yet long yu long ol pipol bilong yu husat i stap long graun bilong yu?
PSA 74:2 Rimembiri kongregesen bilong yu we yu bin baim ol long taim bifo, na yu bin bebaim ol olsem traib bilong inheritasen bilong yu - Maunt Sain, pati bilong Hebre long Isalel, we yu stap.
PSA 74:3 Wokim bek yu yet long stap long ol ruina i go daun na i no bin gat end yet, long ol samting insait Haus Lotu enimi ibin bagarapim.
PSA 74:4 Olega i goap long yu long ples bilong mipela i bin kat ol kot; ol i bin kisim banara bilong ol olsem singsing.
PSA 74:5 Olsem ol man wiles ol i usim aks long bus na ol gat planti trees
PSA 74:6 Na kilim olgeta kervings wantaim aks na piks.
PSA 74:7 Ol i bikim haus lotu bilong yu paia na i katim gut; ol i mekim ples bilong Nem bilong Yu em i no swit mo.
PSA 74:8 Ol tokim olsem long hevi bilong ol, "Mipela i kirapim ol tasol." Ol i barim daun hapkas ol ples we God i bin kam mitim mipela long graun.
PSA 74:9 Ina sain i no stap. Nogat propet i stap gen, na igat wanpela taim bai yumi harim tok. Ikanai yumi save olsem taim bilong dispela hevi i go long olsem.
PSA 74:10 Oli longwe, Bikpela, nem bilong enemy bai i laik katim yu olsem? Foe bai i kisim nem bilong yu na bagarapim oltaim?
PSA 74:11 Witdrawim han bilong yu we i strong? Stretim em olos long bagarapim ol!
PSA 74:12 Bikpela i tok bilong me long taim bipo, wokim siksave long graun.
PSA 74:13 Yu braimim solwara na yu pukim hed bilong draon ol i stap long solwara.
PSA 74:14 Yu krosim hed bilong Leviatan; Yu givim em i kaikai long ol krecha bilong desot.
PSA 74:15 Yu brokimm ples wea wata i kam aut, na yu draiim riva i no stap flow.
PSA 74:16 De bes long yu, na nait tu; Yu bin plantim mun na san.
PSA 74:17 Yu setim olgeta kauntim bilong graun; Yu mekim taim hot na taim kol bilong yia.
PSA 74:18 Rimembol olsem poisen ibin laifim Yu, Bikpela, olsem pikinini narapela kanaka ibin krungim nem bilong Yu.
PSA 74:19 No ken givim soul bilong pijin blong yu long ol binatang i kaikai; yu no ken lusim laip bilong manmeri husat i katim trabel, ol i stap katim trabel foreva.
PSA 74:20 Singsing long Kovenan bilong yu, wantaim ol ples we ol i kamap strong long violence i fulapim ol hap tumbuna bilong kantri.
PSA 74:21 No ken letim ol i katol long trabel i go bek long shame; ol pikinini na ol i no save long moni i singautim nem bilong yu.
PSA 74:22 Kam daun na kirap, o Bikpela, na defendim kaos bilong Yu! Yumi remember olsem ol man i no save i laifim ol tok pikinini long ol dei, mockim Yu.
PSA 74:23 No ken long bilipim olsem ol bikmaus bilong ol giaman i go ap gen gen long yu.
PSA 75:1 Long ol boss bilong sang, long saund bilong 'Yu no ken kilim'. Wan Psalm bilong Esaf. Yumi givim sankyu long yu, O God, yumi givim sankyu, long namel bilong yu i kamap klostu. Ol pipol talem wankain woks bilong yu i amaze.
PSA 75:2 Wanpela taim mi pilim, mi bai jijim stret.
PSA 75:3 Wanpela taim graun na ol pipol we i stap long en i shake, em mi yet yu holimapim pilia bilong en. Selah
PSA 75:4 Mi tokim ol proud, ‘Yu no ken boast,’ na long ol bikman, ‘Yu no ken strongim skul bilong yu.’
PSA 75:5 No ken tu lifimapim ap long horn bilong yu gen heven, na yu no ken tok autsait long nek bilong yu i stap stret.
PSA 75:6 Long givim bikpela i kam nogat long isi na nogat long wes, na nogat long bus.
PSA 75:7 Bareket, em i God husat i givim sentens; Em i kamdaun wanpela, na em i lifimapim anarapela.
PSA 75:8 Wap long kik na i stap long han bilong LORD, i fulap long wain i paul long spes olsem kina kina smel. Em i kilim bek long kik bilong Em, na olgeta man i no gat laif long graun i dring bek, dring olgeta, rausim wara paul.
PSA 75:9 Mi bai tokaut olgeta taim long em; mi bai singim sang bilong preis long God bilong Yakob.
PSA 75:10 Mi bai katim ol han bilong ol nogut, tasol han bilong ol drai bai go antap.
PSA 76:1 Long ol bos bilong singsing. Wanpela song long instrument bilong stri. Wanpela sang bilong Asaf. God i stap kukim nem bilong en i go long Judah; nem bilong en i bikpela long Isrel.
PSA 76:2 Haus bilong em i stap long Salem, ples bilong em i stap long Sion.
PSA 76:3 Em i brukim ol arua bilong faia, siporo na sord na wepam bilong fait. Selah
PSA 76:4 Yu kamap strongpela long lait, yu bikpela moa long ol maunten we i gat planti animal.
PSA 76:5 Ol birua i bin stilim na kisim, ol i slip long slip bilong ol. No geman bilong strong ipo ina lifim han.
PSA 76:6 Long ol i save, yu tokim, Bikpela God bilong Yakob, hos na ranita i go daun, ol i slip na klostu.
PSA 76:7 Yu alo wan yet long fearim. Wanpela Yu i cross, husat ina bai stap bifor Yu?
PSA 76:8 Long heven yu tokim desisan, na erth i save na i kam quiet.
PSA 76:9 Taim God i kamap strong na jujes, long saveman ol pipol i stap long graun, ol i no gat strep. Selah
PSA 76:10 Na ol man i gat bel kros, bai ol i praizim Yu; wantaim ol narapela i sapot long bel kros, yu bai kam ap long ol, olsem yu usim klos bilong yu.
PSA 76:11 Makim na kamapim promis bilong yu long LORD God bilong yu; ol kantri nabarap i bringim gif long Em, na ol i kukim respek long Em, bikos Em i Debe na tru.
PSA 76:12 Em i brukim spirit bilong prins; ol kwin bilong graun i fearim em.
PSA 77:1 Long taim bilong singsing mama, olsem Jeduthun i tok. Wanpela sang bilong Asaph. Mi kisim voice karim go long God, mi singaut i gohet long God bai em i harim mi.
PSA 77:2 Long de bilong trabel, mi go bekim God; ol nait, han bilong mi i op, i no bin pakim; spirit bilong mi i no inap long kamap strong na kisim komfort.
PSA 77:3 Mi rememberim Yu, o God, na mi kisim sori na mi bikmaol; Mi tingim, na spiriti bilong me i kamap dai. Selah
PSA 77:4 Yu kisim ai bilong me nau i no inap go daun; mi tasol i gat planti sor na mi no inap toktok.
PSA 77:5 Mi bin tingim taim bilong bifo, na mia i lukim ol yia i go bek long taim.
PSA 77:6 Nait time, mi rememba song bilong me, na long bel bilong me, mi tingim, na spirit bilong me i stap think.
PSA 77:7 Olsem, Papa God bai i amusim mipela foreva, na em bai i no showim kina helpim han bilong en agen?
PSA 77:8 Em i go pinis oltaim nau? Em i no gat promis gen long oltaim?
PSA 77:9 God i kamas long stap grasim? Iamas long paitim bilong en i stap daunim kompassion bilong en? Selah
PSA 77:10 Mi tok, "Mi bel isi long tingting, han rait bilong Bikpela i go bek."
PSA 77:11 Mi bai rimembim wok bilong LORD; yes, mi bai rimembim wondas bilong tumbuna.
PSA 77:12 Mi bai tok tuturul long olgeta samting yu mekim, na mi bai tokbai long ol bikpela wok yu mekim.
PSA 77:13 Rot bilong yu, o God, i holigren. Wanem kain god i gat bikpela olsem God bilong mipela?
PSA 77:14 Yu em God bilong wonda, yu mekim wonda long ol samting; yu showim strong bilong yu long ol ples.
PSA 77:15 Long pawa Yu bebaim ol pipol bilong Yu, olikanak bilong Yakob na Yusuf. Selah
PSA 77:16 Warai i lukim Yu, o God; warai i lukim Yu na i kirap kirap; ol geta hap bilong warai i rausim tu.
PSA 77:17 Klaud i kamdaun wara; skai i save harim thunder; Pilium yu bungim i go bek gen.
PSA 77:18 Thunder bilong yu i save bikim nogut long tornado; lait bilong lightning i kamapim wold; gras bilong earth i shake na i cut long.
PSA 77:19 Rod bilong yu i go daun long solwara, rot bilong yu i go insait long wara bikpela, tasol bris yu no inap findim prit bilong yu.
PSA 77:20 Yu bin lidim piple bilong yu olsem lok ol i go long han bilong Mosese na Aron.
PSA 78:1 Maskil bilong Asaph. Kisim han bilong yu, o pipo bilong mi, long tok save bilong mi; harim tok bilong maus bilong mi.
PSA 78:2 Mi bai opim maus bilong mi long wikim tok bilong Bibel, em i wanpela kain pasin bilong tisa; Mi bai tokim samting i klostu long taim bilong bipo.
PSA 78:3 Mipela i harim, mipela i save, na papa bilong mipela i tokim mipela.
PSA 78:4 Bai yumi no ken harim dispela stori long pikinini bilong yumi, bat bai tokim long genarason nambawan i go bek ole preis bilong LORD, strongpela wok bilong En, na wondas ol i mekim.
PSA 78:5 Em i makim wanpela tok bilong wol long Jakob, na em i givim laip long Israel, olsem na em i tokim papa bilong mipela long skulim pikinini bilong ol.
PSA 78:6 Jenarisen i kam, na ol i save long ol, ol pikinini i no yet bam, ol i kamap na tellem pikinini bilong ol.
PSA 78:7 Ol i mas putim trast bilong ol long God, no lusim wok bilong em, tasol i holim komandments bilong em.
PSA 78:8 Na bai ol i no olsem tumbuna bilong ol, jenarason wei i kulkul na ogogoto, husat blong en i no tru long en, spirut blong en i no stap wantaim Bikpela.
PSA 78:9 Man bilo bow na arow bilong Efraim bekim bek i go bak long de bilong pait.
PSA 78:10 Ol i no bin holim kovenaeat bilong God, na ol i no bin laik stap long lo bilong Em.
PSA 78:11 Ol lusim bek long memori ol samting em i mekim, wunders em i shoim ol.
PSA 78:12 Em i wokim wondas bifoa tumbuna ol long lan bilong Ijip, long hap bilong Zoan.
PSA 78:13 Em i kisim solwara i go ap, na em i bringim ol i kam; em i putim wara i stap olsem wanpela baeren.
PSA 78:14 Em i lidim ol wantaim klau long de na wantaim lait bilong faia long nait.
PSA 78:15 Em i katim ston long bus na em i givim ol draik olsem planti na solwara.
PSA 78:16 Em bringim wata i kam long ston, na em mekim wata i ran i daun olsem olgeta river.
PSA 78:17 Bikos ol i continue long sin, ol i bagarap long bus, ol i oraitim Bikpela I Tambu long ples bilong traim na painim.
PSA 78:18 Ol i testim God olsem wanem, ol i laik ka long kai na ol i kirapim.
PSA 78:19 Ol i tok strong long God, ol i bin tok, "God bai inap prepaem ka long bus, dispela hap ples we i no gat planti samting?"
PSA 78:20 Taim em i paitim ston, wara i kam aut na wara i harim bikpela. Baine em i givim bret tu, o bai em i supliesin piginini bilong em long mit?
PSA 78:21 Bikpela i harim, em i kamap strong nogut long het bilong en, aifaira i kuk long Jakob, na het bilong em i go antap long Isrel.
PSA 78:22 Bikos ol i no bilivim God yet, na ol i no putim trast long sovesen blong em.
PSA 78:23 Na em i givim komando long klauabu we i stap above, na em i opim dei bilong heven.
PSA 78:24 Emi rainim i kamautim manna bilong ol i kaikai; Emi givim ol grain long hap bilong heven.
PSA 78:25 Man i kaikai bret bilong enjel; Em i salim kaikai inap long ol.
PSA 78:26 Em i bringim win bilong east kutubuk long heven, na em i drivaun win bilong saut bilong pawa bilong En.
PSA 78:27 Em i pilim mit bilong ol olsem ausan, na pisin i gat wing olsem san bilong solwara.
PSA 78:28 Em i kilim ol long senta bilong kamp ol, long ol sait bilong haus ol.
PSA 78:29 Ol i kaikai na bel isi, wantaim Em i givim ol long tingting bilong ol i laik.
PSA 78:30 Bifoa ol i kamap strong long kisim wanem ol i laik, wantaim kaika i stap yet insait long maus bilong ol.
PSA 78:31 Anga bilong God i kirap, na ol i kilim ol papa strong bilong ol, na tu ol i daunim ol yangpela man bilong Isrel.
PSA 78:32 Bai olgeta samting i go hap, ol i stap yet i kontinu long susim; long stap long wondarim wok i mekim, ol i no bilip.
PSA 78:33 Em i stap pinis taim bilong ol long nating, na yia bilong ol i go daun long bikpela fear.
PSA 78:34 Taim em i kilim ol, ol i go bek long en; ol i sori na ol i sakim God.
PSA 78:35 Na ol i rememberim, God em i Roc bilong ol, na God we i gat autoriti win mos bilong ol em i Savio bilong ol.
PSA 78:36 Tupela i bikim samting long maus bilong ol, na tupela i givim lie long tengues bilong ol.
PSA 78:37 Ol hart bilong ol i no kamap strong long em, na ol i no bihainim treaty bilong en.
PSA 78:38 Na em yet, Em i stap klostu long ol, Em i lusim sori long ol long sin bilong ol, Em i no bin kilim ol. Em i bihainim bel hat bilong em, Em i no bin lusim wara bilong em i go olgeta.
PSA 78:39 Em i remember ol i stap yet ol narapela man, olsem win blong paip go na i no kam bek gen.
PSA 78:40 Ol i no obediim Em olgeta taim long bus, na mekim em sori long desert!
PSA 78:41 Olaseta gen ol traiim God na krosim Wan Holigan bilong Isrel.
PSA 78:42 Ol i no gat memor long pawa bilong Em, dei Em i bin ridim ol long enemy bilong ol.
PSA 78:43 Taim em mekim sahn em long kantri Egypt, na wundas bilong em long graun bilong Zoan.
PSA 78:44 Em i bringim blod long wara bilong ol, na ol i no inap drinkim wara bilong ol.
PSA 78:45 Em i sendim swom flai i kaikai ol, na ol frog i bagarapim ol.
PSA 78:46 Em i givim ka bilong ol (grashiopa) na frut bilong wok bilong ol long lokis.
PSA 78:47 Em i kilim vaine bilong ol wantaim ston bilong rein, na figi bilong sycamore bilong ol wantaim ais.
PSA 78:48 Em lusim ol bikman bilong ol long hail, na ol livestock bilong ol i go daun long larim bilong lait.
PSA 78:49 Em i kirapim pas bilong en, weri, bel kol, na bagarap - grup bilong enjel i kam daun na bagarapim.
PSA 78:50 Em i kisim wei long rausim hangre bilong En; em i no sparim ol long dai, tasol em i givim laip bilong ol i go long sik.
PSA 78:51 Em i kilim olgeta pikinini bilong Egypt, ol man i strong long hap bilong Ham.
PSA 78:52 Em i bringim olt long ol pipol bilong em olsem sip na em i lidim ol long olsem mama bos long bus.
PSA 78:53 Em i lidim ol saf long we, ol i no bin fear, na solwara i kam daun na kisim ol enemies bilong ol.
PSA 78:54 Em i bringim ol long hap graun bilong En, long maunten han rait bilong Em i winim.
PSA 78:55 Em i kirapim ol nesen long bikmus bilong ol, na em i givim lottol long ol; em i bringim ol trib long Isrel i go insait long tent bilong ol.
PSA 78:56 Tasol ol i trai na ol i no kamap strong long law bilong Bikpela God, wantaim ol i no holim pren long tok bilong En.
PSA 78:57 Ol i kam bek gen, ol i bikim olsem tumbuna ol bilong ol, nogat trast, ol i krungut olsem banbok i no inap shot.
PSA 78:58 Ol i kirapim Em wantaim ol ples hait, na ol i bringim bilong jelos bilong En wantaim idol ol i bin gat.
PSA 78:59 Long harim tok, God i masalai pinis na tromwe Israel hambak.
PSA 78:60 Em inim husat i lusim haus lotu bilong Shiloh, hen em i stap kaml long ol man.
PSA 78:61 Em i givim strong bilong em long klostu, na em i givim glori bilong em long han bilong poi.
PSA 78:62 Em i givim piple bilong em long sop bikos em i sori nogut tru long ol narapela bilong en.
PSA 78:63 Aibak i kaikim ol yangpela man bilong Em, na ol meri bilong ol i stap wantaim sorow, long tingting bilong song bilong marit ol i no harim.
PSA 78:64 Pris ol i punda long sop, na widow meri bilong ol i no inap krai.
PSA 78:65 Papa God kam bek olsem wanpela strongpela man bilong pait, win i go daun long en.
PSA 78:66 Em i kilim bek nau enemy bilong En; Em i givim sham long ol, sham i no pinis.
PSA 78:67 Em i bikim bek long han bilong Josep na em i no laikim trib bilong Efraim.
PSA 78:68 Bain i pikinim tribe bilong Yuda, Maunt Saion, we em i lavem.
PSA 78:69 Em i bikim Haus Lotu bilong En olsem hap graun, olsem graun Em i strongim i stap oltaim.
PSA 78:70 Em i pikim Dauid, wokman bilong En, na em i kam bek long hap bilong sip.
PSA 78:71 Long ol tending ol meri sheep, Em i bringim i go bekim pasinda long piple Jakob bilong Em, long Israel, ol inheritance bilong Em.
PSA 78:72 Na Davide i lukautim ol longwey wantaim het bilong trutru, na i kosim ol gen wantaim han bilong saveman.
PSA 79:1 Sang bilong Asafu. Ol nesen, o God, i go insait long brata bilong yu; ol bin mekim birua long temples bilong yu we em i halo na ol bin mekim Jiusalem i stap olsem gras.
PSA 79:2 Ol i givim bodi ded bilong wokman bilong yu long ol pisin bilong heven, na flesh bilong saint bilong yu long ol bekside bilong graun.
PSA 79:3 Ol i kirapim blod bilong ol olsem wara long olgeta hap bilong Jerusalem, na i no gat man i kam bikim poroman long ol dai.
PSA 79:4 Mipela kamapim lak na bekbek long ol arapela, ol i laik krosim na bilakim mipela long ol stap wantaim mipela.
PSA 79:5 Olong tam, O Lod, bai yu kros olsem longwe? Bai seliman bilong yu i save kaikaim olsem sait?
PSA 79:6 Kisim i go long ples bilong yu na kirapim yogost long ol narapela kantri, long ol kingdom ol i no save tokim nem bilong yu, ol i no laik kallisim nem bilong yu.
PSA 79:7 Ol i kaikai Jacob olgeta, na ol i bagarapim gras bilong en.
PSA 79:8 No ken holim bek sin bilong tumbuna long us; kisim kam compasson bilong yu kwiktaim, bikos yumui ol i go daun.
PSA 79:9 Bikpela God bilong save mipela, halivim mipela long namel bilong yu, na yu yet yu laik kamap strong; kisim mipela long hens i go, pai bak long hevi bilong sin bilong mipela, long namel bilong yu.
PSA 79:10 Ol nesen i askim, "De na God bilong ol i go we?" Long ai bilong mipela, me kim tok klia long ol nesen pipia bilong yu long paitim bek long bloDDi bilong wokman bilong yu.
PSA 79:11 Mipela i harim pasal sak nar ol i go long yu, na bai yu yet savesim ol dispela i kisim bek long enemies, long strong bilong arm bilong yu.
PSA 79:12 Bekim olsem, sevenfala nau ol i go bek long shamem insait long laplap bilong ples narapela, Papa God, long ol yumi husat i kisim shamem long yu.
PSA 79:13 Mipela pipol bilong Yu, ol sheep bilong pasija bilong Yu, bai givim sankyu long taim olgeta; mipela bai tokautim ples bilong Yu fraim genarashon go long genarashon.
PSA 80:1 Long bilong mana meri i save sing. Long saund blong 'Lili blong Kovena'. Wan Psalm blong Asaf. Harim mipela, o Shepherd blong Israel, hu i lidim Jozef olsem ol fok; Yu hu i savesit long trohn bitwen cherubim, kam ap na shain
PSA 80:2 Bifoa Ephraim, Benjamin, na Manase. Kam long bringim strongpela powa bilong yu, kam long saveim mipela.
PSA 80:3 Bikpela, bringim mipela bek gen, mekim pes bilong yu i lait-im stap long mipela, na mipela i ken savet.
PSA 80:4 O Bikpela God bilong ol ples i go het long ples bilong spirit, olgeta hamas long bikpela i bosim, em i stap olsem long taim gede, long dispela praer bilong pipol bilong yu?
PSA 80:5 Yu givim ol kaikai bilong taleo na yu givim ol mun bilong taleo ol i kamap.
PSA 80:6 Yumi i mekim nabarnami bilong yumi kisim faet wantaim ol, na enejimi bilong yumi i laifim yumi.
PSA 80:7 Bikpela God bilong ol birua, bungim bek yumui, wokim pes bilong yu i shain stap long mipela, na mipela i ken save.
PSA 80:8 Yu kisim vine na kamautim long Ejip; Yu drivaun ol nesen na planim vine gen.
PSA 80:9 Yu klia graun bilong en, na en kamap strong na stap, fulapim Graun.
PSA 80:10 Maunten i kamapim bek long shade bilong em, na cedar bikpela i strong tu long braches bilong en.
PSA 80:11 I salim olt branis bilong en long Solwara, na ol het bilong en i go bek long Wara.
PSA 80:12 Wanem yu bin brukim daun bilong en wal, na ol man i go pas long en, ol i pikim frut bilong en?
PSA 80:13 Pik bilong bus i bagarapim em, na ol kreaatura bilong graun i kaikai long em.
PSA 80:14 Kam bek, o God bilong ol ples i go! Lookim daun from heven na lukim! Jusim dispela vine—
PSA 80:15 Rot i han bilong yu yet yu plantim, pikinini iyu yet yu kisim long yu yet yu bringim i kam ap long yu.
PSA 80:16 Vain bilong yu i katim na kisim, em i burn; ol i dai long tokim strong bilong fac bilong yu.
PSA 80:17 Lukim han bilong yu i stap long rait han bilong yu, long Pikinini man yu bin katim olsem samting longpela taim bipo bilong yu.
PSA 80:18 Em bai yumi no lusim bek i go long Bikpela; givim laip nau long yumi, na yumi kolim nem bilong yu.
PSA 80:19 Bringim bek yumui, Papa God bilong ol ples, makim fase bilong yu i shain uponus, na mipela i ken saves.
PSA 81:1 Long ol bos bilong sing. Olsem Gittith i tok. Bilong Esaf. Singim song bilong bel hap i go long God stap bilong strong bilong mipela; mipela i mas mekim nais nois long God bilong Yakob.
PSA 81:2 Liftim ap song, paitim tamburin, pilaia hap bilong swit soun na lyre.
PSA 81:3 Kamelim trambol long horn bilong ram long mun nupela, na long taim mun i kamap ful long de bikosim Fest.
PSA 81:4 Dispela em i wanpela loa long ol Israel, na wanpela ka long God bilong Yakob.
PSA 81:5 Em i mekim olsem wanpela tok bilong witnes bilong Josep, wewan em i go raun long kantri bilong Ijip, we bilong mi harim tok bilong narapela hap.
PSA 81:6 Mi kisim bek long hed bilong en, na hen i kamap fri long basket.
PSA 81:7 Yu kisim trabel na yu singaut, na mi bekim yu fri; Mi givim tok bak long yu from klau dagan; Mi traiim yu long wara Meribah. Selah
PSA 81:8 Harim, o pipo bilong mi, na mi bai givim yu tok orait: O Isrel, sapos yu harim tok bilong mi tasol!
PSA 81:9 Inap no gat narapela kina god long yu, na yu no ken buk i go daun long god bilong narapela hap.
PSA 81:10 Mi bin LORD God bilong yu, we bilong me bringim yu kam bek long Egip. Opim maus bilong yu wel, na mi bai filimup i.
PSA 81:11 Pipol bilong mi i no lisin long mi, na Isrel i no obrim tok bilong mi.
PSA 81:12 Mi lusim ol long ol het bilong ol i stap strong, na ol i bihainim wei bilong ol yet.
PSA 81:13 Mi laik ol pipol bilong me harim tok bilong mi, na Israel i go long we bilong mi,
PSA 81:14 Olsem wanpela taim mi bai daunim ol eni a, na mi bai kisim han bilong mi go bek gen long ol poi na ol i no liklik.
PSA 81:15 Ol i no laik LORD, bai mekim tok bilong olegesen, na wari bilong ol bai i stap foreva.
PSA 81:16 Mipela bai givim yu kaikai namba wan; long hanu i kam long rok, mipela bai fulipim bel bilong yu.
PSA 82:1 Sang i go bek long Asaf. God i stap long ples bilong ol spirit, na em i givim desisan long ol samting we i mas kam bek gen:
PSA 82:2 Oli man, how long bai yu givim sentens long wrong na tok strong long ol pikinini i no gat laif? Selah, waraupim.
PSA 82:3 Defendiim kaos bilong ol wik na papa i no stap; statim na sapotim ol rait bilong ol i skulim na daunim.
PSA 82:4 Saveman i go long ol pipol i no inap na i needim help, na saveim ol dispela long han bilong ol i no gat laif.
PSA 82:5 Ol i no save or ol i no undastand; ol i wanda long tumbuna; olgeta fonksen bilong graun em i shakin.
PSA 82:6 Mi tok olsem, 'Yupela i stap ol god, yupela ol i stap san bilong God we i gat autoriti win mos.'
PSA 82:7 Bareka olsem ol man i dai, na olsem bikman i pundaun.”
PSA 82:8 Kam daun, o God, wokim bekim, jijim olgeta graun, bikos olgeta nesen i stap long han bilong yu, na yu inaitisman, yu mas katim bekim.
PSA 83:1 Wanpela sang. Wanpela Psalm bilong Asaph. O God, no ken siwit; no ken stap mumu; no ken stap klostu, o God.
PSA 83:2 Lukim ol enemi bilong yu i stap strong long paitim yu, ol fo bilong yu i kamap strong na kisim hed bilong ol.
PSA 83:3 Ol i usim trick na katim plan long ol pipol bilong yu, na ol i tok birua long ol dispela yu ilaikim.
PSA 83:4 Mipela i tok, “Kam, mipela imas savwe olsem narapela kantri; nem bilong Israel i no gat tok istori gen.”
PSA 83:5 Wantaim wan tingting ol i plan long tok, ol i joineim na mekim wanpela union agensim Yu —
PSA 83:6 Haus bilong Edom na ol Ishimelait, bilong Moab na ol Hagrait,
PSA 83:7 Long Gebal, Amon, na Amalek, long Filistia wantaim ol pipol bilong Taire.
PSA 83:8 Asiria i kam stap wantaim ol, i givim strong long pikanini bilong Lot. Selah
PSA 83:9 Mekim olsem yu mekim long Midian, olsem Sisera na Jabin long Kishon River,
PSA 83:10 Ol i bin dai pinis long Endor na ol i kamap olsem makai long graun.
PSA 83:11 Mekim ol i dai bikpela man bilong ol olsem Oreb na Zeeb, na mekim ol i dai bikpela man bilong ol olsem Zebah na Zalmunna.
PSA 83:12 Husat tok, “Mipela i ken kaikai graun bilong God.”
PSA 83:13 Mekim olsem wanbel, O God bilong mi, olsem hus bifo win.
PSA 83:14 Olsem faia i kaikaim ol savan, olsem flamen i karim maunten long narapela,
PSA 83:15 Bekim ol long tomata, na givim ol iet long ston bilong yu.
PSA 83:16 Kisim shem na kova bek long ol, na ol i go lusim nem bilong yu, o LORD.
PSA 83:17 Oli masi i stap long sham, na oli save poret long fear; oli ken i go daun long sham, na oli peris long digos.
PSA 83:18 Ol i save, Bikpela, yu alone, nem bilong yu Bikpela, yu i bikpela win long olgeta graun.
PSA 84:1 Long bilong man i save lidim singsing. Olsem Gittith i tok. Wanpela sang bilong pikinini belong Korah. Hao nais ples bilong yu stap, Papa God bilong olgeta ples, em i swit moa!
PSA 84:2 Soul bilong me i laik kam bek long stap, i kamap nogut, i dai pinis long husat ol i go long ples bilong LORD; harte bilong me na bodi bilong me i singaut long God i alive.
PSA 84:3 Sparoa i stap long ples, na swalo i kisim ples bilong en na i mekim haus kukuk, besaida wailis bilong yu, O Papa bilong olgeta, King bilong mi na God bilong mi, i stap long ples bilong yu, na pikinini bilong en i putim besaida altas bilong yu.
PSA 84:4 Ol pipel we istap long haus bilong yu, ol berkat! Ol i stap givim prais long yu olgeta. I stap, yumit tok
PSA 84:5 Ol i blesim ol wei streng bilong ol i kam long Yu, na ol hart bilong ol i stap long piligrim.
PSA 84:6 Ol i pasim nao long Vale Baka, ol wokim i kamap ol ples bilong wara; na ren bung bilong seson kol moni i kova em ol geta.
PSA 84:7 Ol i go ap long streng, ol i go long streng, na raitim ol i kam bek long God long Sayan.
PSA 84:8 O Bikpela bilong ol ples we i gat armi, harim praer bilong mi; kisim han bilong yumi, o God bilong Yakob. Selah
PSA 84:9 Kisim notis long skild bilong mipela, o God, na bekim gut long face bilong anointet bilong yu.
PSA 84:10 Wanpela de in kot hus bilong Yu i gutu olsem tausend long hap ples. Mi laikim bai daor kiapa long haus bilong God bilong mi, na mi no likim stap long salim bilong ol i no gat laif.
PSA 84:11 Bikpela God em i laip na sheld; LORD i givim gras na glori, na em i no holim bek i go long ol good samting long ol manmeri i wokabaut wantaim save na strepela.
PSA 84:12 O Lo long ol ples i go, hamamas i stap long man hu i putim bilip long Yu!
PSA 85:1 Long taim bilong song leader bilong God. Wanpela sang bilong pikinini belong Korah. Yu, Bikpela, givim gutpela toktok long graun bilong yu; Yu bringim bek Jakob, pikinini bilong Isak, long hap bilong em.
PSA 85:2 Yu kisim bek long olgeta nogut pasin bilong ol; Yu kisim bek i go long olgeta sin bilong ol. Stap.
PSA 85:3 Yu holim bek olgeta firis bilong Yu; Yu tanim bek long hotpela iri bilong Yu.
PSA 85:4 Bikpela God bilong sevensesan bilong mipela, bringim bikim yumupela i kam bek gen, na kisim wei displisd tumas bilong yu long mipela.
PSA 85:5 Bai yu kros long mipela foreva? Bai yu stretim kros bilong yu long ol genarashun ol?
PSA 85:6 Inap yu givim bak laip long yumi gen, na ol pipol bilong yu ken harim gutpela sindaun long yu?
PSA 85:7 Bikpela, baim yu kam showim mipela long stap gutpela, na givim mipela sofware long saveman.
PSA 85:8 Mi bai harim tok bilong God Jehovah; bikos em bai tok pis i go long ol pipol na ol sent bilong en, na em no go lukim ol i go bek long hevi.
PSA 85:9 Sévensesen bilong em i kam klostu long ol i gat tromoi long em, na glori bai i stap long kantri bilong yumi.
PSA 85:10 Lovin bilong God i stap wantaim faitful, na jastis na pis i pisin, ol i kamap long wankain.
PSA 85:11 Fideliti i kam long graun, na Jastis i luk i daun long heven.
PSA 85:12 Papa God i go inap long providim gutpela, na kantry bilong yumi bai bringim planti ka.
