PSA 85:13 Jastis bai i go bifor em long prepare rot bilong fut bilong en.
PSA 86:1 Wanpela prea bilong David. Papa God, kusim yumi long tok, harim tok bilong mi, givim ansa long mi, wantaim ol pikinini i no gat samting, ol i nidim help.
PSA 86:2 Savesim sol bilong me, bikos mi em i man bilong God. Yu em i God bilong me; saveim servan bilong yu we i trast long yu.
PSA 86:3 Sindim belas olsem na long me, Papa bilong mipela, bikos mi singaut i go long yu olgeta dei.
PSA 86:4 Bringim bel isi long servant bilong Yu, Papa bilong olgeta, na mi lifimup spirit bilong me long Yu.
PSA 86:5 Papa, yu kiind na givim pardon, yu ric long tok bilong lav long ol pipol we mipela karim nem bilong Yu.
PSA 86:6 Harim tok ples bilong mi, GOD, lusim ai bilong yu long hap bilong mi, inap givim meri long mi.
PSA 86:7 Long taim bilong trabel bilong mi, mi karim kol long Yu, na Yu harim tok bilong mi.
PSA 86:8 O Pita, i no gat narapela olsem yu long ol geta spirit, na wok olsem yu i no gat.
PSA 86:9 Olgeta nesen ol i mekim bai kam na katim het bilong yu, Papa bilong mipela, na bai givim glori long nem bilong yu.
PSA 86:10 Bikos yu gret na yu wokim wondas; Yu alone em i God.
PSA 86:11 Skulim mi long wei bilong yu, Bikpela, naso mi ken wokabaut long troth bilong yu. Givim mi hat bilong wan pais, naso mi ken iofiam nem bilong yu.
PSA 86:12 Mi bai praisim Yu, O Lod God bilong mi, wantaim ol het bilong mi; Mi bai givim glori long nem bilong Yu oltaim.
PSA 86:13 Bikpela nau i stap long yu, yu givim mi laip, yu birua mi long hap graun bilong Sheol.
PSA 86:14 Ol pikinini i gat bikpela hed, ol i go antap long me, O God; grup bilong ol man i no gat hati i kam bekim laip bilong mi, na ol i no bin givim respek long yu.
PSA 86:15 Bai yu, O Lohadi, yu i god namel long stap na i givim planti grace, i no quick long bungim bel, na yu i stap strong long givim lav na i stap strong long truth.
PSA 86:16 Wokim face long me, givim mi meri; givim strong long wokman bilong yu, saveim pikinini bilong hap meri.
PSA 86:17 Yu showim mi sak na gutpela bilong yu, na eni enemy bilong mi bai si na bai shame; long yu, PAPA, yu halivim mi na givim mi gutpela harti.
