PSA 88:1 Wanpela sang. Wanpela Psalm bilong Pikinini belong Korah. Olsem choirmaster i mas. Long Mahalath Leannoth. Wanpela Maskil bilong Heman Ezrahite. O LORD, God bilong salvishon bilong mi, dei na nait, mi krai aut i go long yu.
PSA 88:2 Prer bilong mi i kam bifo yu; inklina han bilong yu long hap cry bilong mi.
PSA 88:3 Soul bilong me i fulap long hevi, na laip bilong me i kam klostu long Sheol.
PSA 88:4 Mi kam daun long ol pipel i go daun long hole bilong ded, na mi olsem man we i no ina streng.
PSA 88:5 Mi lus pinis long ol dai, olsem ol i paitim pinis i go daun long grave, ol i no stap long mami bilong yu, na ol i kat bek long han bilong yu.
PSA 88:6 Yu pilai mi long botol bung na dai, long dei bilong olgeta depte.
PSA 88:7 Wara bilong yu i kam strong long me; ol geta bilong yu i kalim mi. Selah
PSA 88:8 Yu rimsaitim ol fren bilong me long me; Yu mekim ol i nogat laik long me, na mi stap klost, na mi no inap go long ples.
PSA 88:9 Mai bel isi i kamap dim olgeta long sorow. Mi singaut i go long yu, LORD, oldei; mi waisim upim han bilong mi long yu.
PSA 88:10 Yu wokim mirakol long ol dai finis? Spirits i go daun kam bek gen, na oli prakisisim Yu? Selah
PSA 88:11 Inap long tokim olgeta long stori bilong yu yet, olegu na stap long lav, long ples bilong ded? Yu yet i gat faitfulness long Abadon?
PSA 88:12 Bai ol samting namba wan bilong yu i go kamap long wei bilong dekis, o raitim bilong yu long graun bilong forget?
PSA 88:13 Bilong yu, Papa bilong olgeta, mi kisim hap bilong help; long moning, prai bilong mi i kam bifo yu.
PSA 88:14 O Papa bilong olgeta, lusim wei long me? Kamiakim pes bilong yu long me?
PSA 88:15 Long tumbuna pikinini bai mi kisim sori, na mi klosap long dai. Mipela i kisim olgeta wikim fear na shaken long yu; mipela i lus tingting.
PSA 88:16 Pasal bilong God i birua, tevoro bilong yu i bin kilim mi.
PSA 88:17 Olde long dispela dei ol i kam bek long me olsem warara, na ol i klosim me long olgeta sait.
PSA 88:18 Yu kilim poroman bilong mi, na friend bilong mi; dak i stap wantaim mi olsem wan i stap wantaim olgeta.
PSA 89:1 Man bilong skul bilong Ethan man bilong Ezra. Mi bai sing long lovingsik bilong Papa God foreva; mouth bilong me bai tokaut strongpela trast bilong Em i go long olgenarashon.
PSA 89:2 Mi tok pinis, “Vinari i kamap strong oltaim; Yu plantim trast long heven.”
PSA 89:3 Yu tokim, “Mi mekim akord wantaim Pikinini i saves bilong Mi, mi promis long Daud wokman bilong Mi:”
PSA 89:4 “Mi bai plantim of na pikinini bilong yu foreva, na mi bai kamapim trohn bilong yu yet long olgenarashen.” Selah
PSA 89:5 Heven i givim prais long wonder bilong yu, LORD—na faithfulness bilong yu tu—long hap assembli bilong ol sanctified.
PSA 89:6 Hu inap kamap bikos long LORD long skai? Hu ibin spirit bilong heaven i stil olsem LORD?
PSA 89:7 Long kaunsil bilong ol saint, God i gat respek bikpela, na em i bikpela nao long olgeta we i kamapim em.
PSA 89:8 O Lip Go Bikpela, hu i laik yumi? O Bikpela Lip, fetfulness bilong yu i go raun long yu.
PSA 89:9 Yu bosim dispela solwara i go harom; wän dispela waws bilong en i kam antap, Yu stilim ol.
PSA 89:10 Yu kraim Rahab olsem kai i dai; Yu spredim ol enimi bilong yu na yu usim arm strongpela bilong yu.
PSA 89:11 Heven i belong yumui, na graun na em i gat olgeta samting yu bin mekim. Yu bin mekim graun na olgeta samting i stap long en.
PSA 89:12 Not na Saus Yu mekim; Tabo na Hermon i singautim rejois long Nem bilong Yu.
PSA 89:13 Strongpela i stap long arm bilong yu; hand bilong yu i strong. Rait han bilong yu em i go antap.
PSA 89:14 Raitim na Jastis i stap astern long tron bilong Yu; lovingseli na bilev i go bifo Yu.
PSA 89:15 Ol i blesim olsem ol i save gut long soun bilong jubeli, ol i warka long lait bilong presens bilong Bikpela.
PSA 89:16 Ol i amamas long nem bilong yu long oldei, na ol i kirap strong long raiteus bilong yu.
PSA 89:17 Yu stap bilong glori bilong strongpela bodi bilong ol, na long pinga bilong yu, tupela horn bilong mipela i go antap.
PSA 89:18 Skid bilong yumi i go long LORD, na king bilong yumi i go long Wan Holi bilong Israel.
PSA 89:19 Bipo yumi tok olsem long wanpela sios; long ol man bilong God yumi tok olsem, “Mi givim strong long wanpela man bilong pait; mi lifim up em i go we bilong mipela, em i pikinini long ol pipol.”
PSA 89:20 Mi finim servat David bilong Mi; wantaim oil bilong hevi bilong Mi, mi anointim em.
PSA 89:21 Han bilong mi bai stap i go long en, na arm bilong mi bai givim strong long em.
PSA 89:22 Nogat eni enemy bai kam kot long en, nogat man i no gat laif bai bagarapim em.
PSA 89:23 Mipela bai bagarap ol i no likim em na mipela bai kilim ol i birua long em.
PSA 89:24 Faithfulness na lovingkindness bilong mi bai i stap wantaim em, na long namel bilong mi, horn bilong en bai i go antap, em bai i kamap strong.
PSA 89:25 Bai mi putim han bilong en long solwara, na ran han bilong en long sangpela river.
PSA 89:26 Em bai singautim Me, 'Yu Papa bilong me, Yu God bilong me, Rupele bilong sevensesen bilong me.'
PSA 89:27 Mi bai appointim em olsem Pikinini Namba Wan bilong Mi, na em i gat autoriti win mosong long ol kingly bilong graun.
PSA 89:28 Mi bai kispim fo ever mi laik tru long en, na mipela akornd olsem bikpela promis, em i stap strong.
PSA 89:29 Mipela bai plantim lain bilong en, tron bilong en oltaim tasol longpela heven i stap.
PSA 89:30 Sapos pikinini bilong em lusim lo bilong mi, na no wok long jusmen bilong mi,
PSA 89:31 Sapos ol i braukim statits bilong Mipela na ol i no holim strong komanda bilong Mipela,
PSA 89:32 Mi bai kisim kaer long sindaun bilong ol wantaim rod bilong paitim, na mi bai givim ol pain long hevi bilong ol.
PSA 89:33 Bai mi no lusim lovting bilong mi long em, na mi no bin betreim Fethfulness bilong mi.
PSA 89:34 Mi no bai rausim kovenan bilong Mi, na mi no bai changim tok bilong maus bilong Mi.
PSA 89:35 Wanpela taim tasol mi go hed long haliness bilong Mi—mi no ken slip long Davide—
PSA 89:36 Ol pikinini bilong em bai i stap oltaim, na tron bilong em bifor Mi olsem san.
PSA 89:37 Olsem mun, em i stap strong long taim, wanes man i givim testimonio long heven. Selah
PSA 89:38 Nau, tasol, Yu kilim aut na tokim em i no gud; Yu bel kol olsem na i sori long pikinini yu i bikim.
PSA 89:39 Yu rimsait long agrikman bilong yu wantaim hausboi, na yu daunim krown bilong en long dus.
PSA 89:40 Yu bin kilim daun olgeta wal bilong en, na yu bin mekim olgeta strangples bilong en i go daun long graun.
PSA 89:41 Ol pipel i go na pasim em, ol i stilim samting bilong em, na em i kamap shame long ol narapela bilong en.
PSA 89:42 Yu go het upim han bilong rait bilong ol poi na enemi, Yu mekim ol i kamap bilong glad.
PSA 89:43 Yu bin kilim sharptem bilong sward bilong em, na yu no givim strong long em long taim bilong faet.
PSA 89:44 Yu bin finishim splenda bilong en, na yu bin kasim trohn bilong en i go daun long graun.
PSA 89:45 Yu kat shortim dei bilong yut na em, yu kisim sham long en. Selah
PSA 89:46 Olam bai, O Ladi, yu bai kaivim yu et longwe? Bai pasal bilong yu i go antap strong olsem ai?
PSA 89:47 Rimembiri lapun bilong taim ples bilong mi! Olsem wanem ken i go long ol man we yu kreaetim?
PSA 89:48 Husat man i stap na mai sioptim lukim die? Em ina pata long kisim soul bilong em long pawa bilong Sheol? Selah
PSA 89:49 Bikpela, nambis i go long yu we bilong ples bilong yu stap long wanem, wanpela yu tok tru long taim bifo, na yu tok tru long Daved?
PSA 89:50 Rimemba, Pita bilong yu, wail bilong ol i servist na yu we mi yet kam insait long het bilong mi long planti manmeri.
PSA 89:51 Ol i laik katolim, LORD, na ol i laik bagarap strongim pasal bilong man yu i bin anointim!
PSA 89:52 Blessim LORD foreva! Amen na amen.
PSA 90:1 Wanpela prea bilong Moisi man bilong God. Papa, yu bin stap long ples bilong mipela long olgenarashon.
PSA 90:2 Bifoa maunten i kamap o Yu birua erth na graun na wol, long taim bifo na long taim i go bek, yu em i God.
PSA 90:3 Yu bringim man i go bek long ausan, ol tok, "Kam bek, o sobs bilong ol man i dai."
PSA 90:4 Long ol bilong yu, tausend yia i kamap narapela dei tasol, olsem dei i go pinis tasol, o wach bilong nait.
PSA 90:5 Yu kisim ol i go bek long slaep bilong ol; ol i semak long graas nupela bilong moning —
PSA 90:6 Long moning em i kamap nova, tasol long apinun em i lus na em i mati.
PSA 90:7 Mipela i kamapim olgeta long Anga bilong Yu, na mipela i dae long rausim bilong Yu.
PSA 90:8 Yu bin putim ol hevi bilong yumi long fron bilong yu, na ol sin bilong yumi husat yumi bin hidim, ol i kamap long lait bilong prezens bilong yu.
PSA 90:9 Olgeta dei bilong yumi i kamdaun long kros bilong yu, na yumi kambekim yia bilong yumi wantaim sos.
PSA 90:10 Namba bilong yia na de bilong mipela em seventy yia, o eiti yia sapos mipela i strong, tasol praid bilong ol i warka tasol na sori, bikos ol i go pinis bikos ol i no stap longtaim, na mipela i flaiawe.
PSA 90:11 Husait i save ka pamuk long pait bilong yu? Pait bilong yu i kamap olsem frik bilong yu mas respektem.
PSA 90:12 Tisim mipela long kauntim dae mipela, na mipela inap bringim het bilong waisdom.
PSA 90:13 Kam bek, Pita! Olsem wanem taim bai yumi stap? Sindim bel hart long servants bilong yu.
PSA 90:14 Givim mipela kaikai long moning wantaim yumi lavin kindness, na mipela i ken sing wantaim glad, na mipela i glad olsem olgeta de.
PSA 90:15 Mekim gutpela hap blong yumi olsem long taim olsem yumi bin kisim trabel, olsem long yia olsem yumi bin lukim ol samting nogut.
PSA 90:16 Wok bilong yu i mas kamap long servantomu bilong yu, na gutpela splenda bilong yu i go long ol pikinini bilong ol.
PSA 90:17 Mipela i mas husat bikpela manna bilong Bikpela bilong mipela i kam daun long mipela; em i strongim wok bilong han bilong mipela—em i strongim wok bilong han bilong mipela!
PSA 91:1 Em i stap insait long ples namel bilong God bilong hevil, bai i stap i go long shade bilong Pawa gret.
PSA 91:2 Bai mi tokim long LORD, "Yupela i stap long ples bilong birua na kamp bilong strongim bilong mi, God bilong mi, we mi putim trast long em."
PSA 91:3 Em bai saveman yu long stretem bilong man i kam bekim pisin, na long sik long kilim olgeta.
PSA 91:4 Em bai kova yu gen long pluma bilong En; long anua bilong En yu ken finim ples bilong hidim; finis bilong En em i stap olsem skild na barik.
PSA 91:5 Yu no ken iafraid long toksik bilong nait, na arao i go antap long de.
PSA 91:6 Na nogat sik bilong dai i go wakabaut long tumbuna, na nogat disasta i kam na bagarapim ol samting long awa belo.
PSA 91:7 Tausen i mas pinis dai klostu long sait bilong yu, na ten tausen i mas pinis dai long han bilong rait bilong yu, no ken hurim bai kam klostu long yu.
PSA 91:8 Bai yu lukim ol long ai bilong yu na witunesim dispela painim bilong ol i no gat laif.
PSA 91:9 Bikos yu bin mekim LORD ol husat yu bai stap, ripot bilong mi, Most High —
PSA 91:10 Nogat ol kino bai kam long yu, nogat ol sik bai kam klostu long haus bilong yu.
PSA 91:11 Em bai givim tok long einjes ol i go lukautim yu long olgeta wei yu wokabaut.
PSA 91:12 Ol bai kisim yu go hap, na bai ol poto yu, so yu no ken kakai lek long stoan.
PSA 91:13 Yu bai tromot long lain na kabara; yu bai daunim liklik lain na snek.
PSA 91:14 Bikos em i lakim Me, Mi bai savim em; bikos em i save nem bilong Mi, Mi bai kisim ka long en.
PSA 91:15 Wanpela em i singautim long mi, mi bai givim ansa long em; mi bai stap wantaim em long taim bilong trabel. Mi bai skulim em, na mi bai givim em respek.
PSA 91:16 Laip longpela bai mi plesim em, na mi bai showim em Sevensesen bilong mi.
PSA 92:1 Wanpela Sang. Wanpela sang long dei Sabbath. Em i gutpela prisim LORD, na singim singsing long nem bilong yu, o Moa Hai,
PSA 92:2 Long tokautim lav bilong yu long moning, na long bilip long save bilong yu long nait.
PSA 92:3 Wantaim hap stinging bilong ten na singsing bilong lira.
PSA 92:4 Bikpela, yu gimme hamamas long wok yu mekim; mi singautim song bilong joi long wok bilong han bilong yu.
PSA 92:5 Wok bilong yu, o Bikpela, hamamas olgeta, tingting bilong yu longpela na dipela!
PSA 92:6 Man i go long olsem, em i no save, na man bilong bagarap, em i no inap undastan.
PSA 92:7 Maski ol pikinini i kamap strong olsem gras, na ol i stap strong na ol i kamap bikpela, ol bai i bagarap olgeta.
PSA 92:8 Bai yu, o Papa bilong mipela, yu kamap strong olsem forever!
PSA 92:9 Nambis, Bikpela, nambis, enemy bilong yu, ol i karim bel, ol yogua yet, ol i pas long wol; ol i wark long hevi, ol i dispela i go daun.
PSA 92:10 Bikos yu lilifimap horn bilong mi olsem horn bilong bulmakau bus; na mi get anointing wantaim oil bilong stap gutpela.
PSA 92:11 Mai ai i lukim pundaun bilong ol enimis, mai ka i harim kol kol bilong ol i no gat laif enimis.
PSA 92:12 Dai na rait bai kamap strong olsem palmti, na bai gro strong olsem seda long Lebanon.
PSA 92:13 Plantim long haus bilong Lod, ol bai kamap strong long kot bilong God bilong yumi.
PSA 92:14 Long taim ol i go dae, ol i ken planti givim frut yet, na ol i strong na stap gren yet.
PSA 92:15 Bilong prekem, “LORD em i stap straigt; Em i Roc bilong mi, na long em igat no samting i no stret.”
PSA 93:1 LORD i bos bilong ol! Em i kovara na kamap strong; LORD em i putim skirt bilong pawa na em i armim em yet long strong. Wanpela wara em i stap strong, ina bai no inap rausim.
PSA 93:2 Tron bilong yu em i stap long taim bipo; Yu kam long taim bilong bipo i go inap long taim i kam.
PSA 93:3 Wara i go antap, Papa God; Rivabiri i kirapim voisis; Solwara i liftimup waves bilong en.
PSA 93:4 Long sangpela wara i go antap – bikpela breakas bilong solwara – LORD ibin stap long hevi, em i gat bikpela pes.
PSA 93:5 Testemoni bilong yu em i stap strong olsem; holines i kamapim haus bilong Bikpela, long ol dei i kam.
PSA 94:1 O Bikpela, God bilong pait, O God bilong pait, kamap strong na shine forth.
PSA 94:2 Kam daun na sakim, O Jaj bilong graun; givim bi-long long ol proud long het.
PSA 94:3 O Bikpela, Olsem ol i stap olsem, ol nogat gutpela i amamas long tok bilong en?
PSA 94:4 Ol i kirapim tok bilong olsem bigman; ol i wokim ol samting nogut, na ol i tok brigina.
PSA 94:5 Ol i kirapim piple bilong yu, Bikpela; ol i bagarapim inheritance bilong yu.
PSA 94:6 Ol i kilim meri husban i dai na man i kam bilong narapela hap; ol i murim pikinini i no stap papa.
PSA 94:7 Ol i tok, “LORD i no save lukim; God bilong Yakob i no givim bel hevi.”
PSA 94:8 Kisim notis, O ol i no save long ol pipel! O ol buk, wanem taim yumi kam wis?
PSA 94:9 Em i go pasim ip long han, ina bai em i no harim? Em i go wokim ai, ina bai em i no lukim?
PSA 94:10 Em i givim toktok long ol narion, em i no gat skul bilong disciplin? Em i tisa man, em i no save gut?
PSA 94:11 Papa God i save tingting bilong man, ol i no ken givim meanin.
PSA 94:12 Man i hapim, o Bikpela, yu disciplinim, na yu tisim em long loa bilong yu.
PSA 94:13 I givim em relif long dei bilong trabel, na taim ol i dikim hol long ol birua.
PSA 94:14 Papa God bai no lusim ol pipol bilong em; Em bai no lakem brata na susa bilong em go nas.
PSA 94:15 Detsin bai kamap rait gen, na olgeta man i gat het bel isi bai bihainim.
PSA 94:16 Husait bai kamap strong gen long me agensim ol pipol i wark long hevi? Husait bai stap strong long me agensim warkmen bilong hevi?
PSA 94:17 Bikos LORD, Pita bilong yumi, i no helpim mi, bai mi go kam long ples bilong deat na stil.
PSA 94:18 Mi tok, "Leq bilong mi i go daun," Lovingselo bilong yu, o Bikpela, em i sapotim mi.
PSA 94:19 Wen wari i kamautim mi, konsolasiun bilong yu i switim soul bilong mi.
PSA 94:20 Inap long thon i birua bai yu halivim mi, em i wokim ol samting nogut long tok save?
PSA 94:21 Ol i joi tasol olsem wan long hap against ol righteous na katen ol innocent i go long dai.
PSA 94:22 Bikpela i stap strong long me, na God bilong me em i rock bilong ples bilong bai mi go kisim skul.
PSA 94:23 Em bai kisim bek long ol, salim ol i go long ol yet, na distroyim ol long ol nogut pasin. LORD God bilong yumi bai distroyim ol.
PSA 95:1 Kam, yumit yet long sing aut o hap long Papa God; yumit yet kisim bikpela voice long Rok bilong sevensesen i save yumit!
PSA 95:2 Mipela i go insait long em presence wantaim toksave gut; mipela i wokim saut long hariap longen song.
PSA 95:3 Bikos LORD em i bikpela God, em i bikpela King antap long ol kina god.
PSA 95:4 Long han bilong Em i stap long bun botol bilong graun, na talabun bilong maunten i go long em.
PSA 95:5 Solwara em i bilong En, nau em i mekim, na han bilong En i bin mekim kantri drai.
PSA 95:6 Kam, mipela i go worhipim na taitim hed; mipela i mas gidim kni bifo LORD olsem Meka bilong yumi.
PSA 95:7 Em i God bilong yumi, na yumi ol i pipol bilong ples gras bilong Em, ol sheep i stap aninit long han bilong Em. Tude, sapos yu harim voys bilong Em,
PSA 95:8 No ken harim bek long het bilong yu olsem yu mekim long Meriba, long de bihain long Masaha long bus.
PSA 95:9 Long ples we ol tumbuna bilong yumi bin tokim na triimim Mipela, ol i gat save long wok mipela bin mekim.
PSA 95:10 Long forti yia, mi bel kolim long olgenarason ya, na mi tok, "Ol i narapela ples we ol het bilong ol i go daun long rot, na ol i no save lukim we bilong mi."
PSA 95:11 Mi kam ap long othes long rausim bel hat, oli no inap go insait ripos bilong Mi.
PSA 96:1 Singim nupela sang long Lod; olgeta erth singim long Lod.
PSA 96:2 Singim sang long olgeta LORD, blessim nem bilong em; tokautim savesen bilong em dei bihain dei.
PSA 96:3 Tokim gut long ol manmeri em i gat bikpela namel long ol narapela kantri, ol wok bilong em i amamas long ol pipol oli stap.
PSA 96:4 Bikpela i go longwe LORD, em i mas praise longlong; em i mas saves antap long ol debes.
PSA 96:5 Olgeta god bilong ol narapela kantri i masalai, tasol LORD em i papa bilong heven.
PSA 96:6 Glory na powa i stap bifo Em; strong na gutpela i fillim hap Haus Lotu bilong En.
PSA 96:7 Givim Glory na Strong long LORD, o papa na mama bilong ol nesen, givim Glory na Strong long LORD.
PSA 96:8 Givim glori long LORD, bikos nem bilong Em i stret; kisim ofing na kam, na go insait long haus lotu bilong Em.
PSA 96:9 Praesim LORD long glori bilong halinasis; olgets long erth, krikim i go bel hevi long em.
PSA 96:10 Kirapim bek long ol narawan pesen: “LORD i bos bilong yumi!” Warld i stap strong; em i no inap sift; Em bai jujim ol ples ia na givim sentens long wei bilong jus.
PSA 96:11 Heven i amamas, na graun i hap hap; solwara i singaut, na olgeta samting i stap insait long em.
PSA 96:12 Gras bilong ples i kamap strong, na ol samting i stap insait long em. Ol diwai bilong bus orait i singaut wantaim glad.
PSA 96:13 Bifoa LORD, wantaim Em i kam - Em i kam bek long jijim erth. Em bai jijim wol long raitnes na ol pipal long fidilies bilong em.
PSA 97:1 Pipia i bos, olgeta kantri i amamas; na olgeta ai hap bilong solwara i glat.
PSA 97:2 Klaud na dakis i kam raitim Em; jastis na righteousness i stap olsem fondepela bilong tron blong En.
PSA 97:3 Faia i go bifor Em, na i kaikai ol eni bilong Em long ol sait.
PSA 97:4 Laitnin bilong em i lakim wel olgeta wold; graun i lukim na i bel.
PSA 97:5 Maunten i rais olsem waks long wei bilong prensens bilong LORD, bifor Lord bilong ol graun.
PSA 97:6 Heven i tokautim justis bilong Em; ol ples i lukim glori bilong Em.
PSA 97:7 Ol i stap i go long ples gras, ol manmeri i worshipim skulpta, na ol i pai long idol. Worshipim God, all yufela spirits!
PSA 97:8 Sayan i harim na katol, na taun bilong Yuda i amamas long ol senis bilong yu, Papa God.
PSA 97:9 Long tok bilong wan God tasol, Bikpela, yu em i bikpela long olgeta graun; yu longwe na yu bikpela, winim ol spirit no gut.
PSA 97:10 Bagarapim olgeta samting nogut, yupela i lumulua long LORD! Em i save ol alma bilong ol sant bilong em, na em i birua ol long han bilong ol nogut.
PSA 97:11 Lait i shain long ol i fait long lo bilong God, gladnes i kamap long ol i straigt long hart.
PSA 97:12 Amende long ol i go hed long Lod, yu masalai ol i go, singautim nem bilong em we hem i haliv.
PSA 98:1 Saum. Singim nupela sang long Lod, em i mekim wonda; hemin rait han na holii arm bilong em i winim victory.
PSA 98:2 Papa God i tokaut saveman bilong en, na i shoim rop bilong en long ol narapela kantri.
PSA 98:3 Em i memba lov na trustum bilong en long haus bilong Israel; olgeta hap bilong wol i lukim saveman bilong God.
PSA 98:4 Wokim saut long singsing long Bikpela, olgeta graun; kamap strong na go pinis—lusim tok bilong yu i go longwe, na singim sang bilong preis!
PSA 98:5 Singim sang in tok bilong LORD wantaim gita bilong tumbuna, long singsing switmoa wantaim piana bilong singsing.
PSA 98:6 Wantaim trompet na saun bilong horn bilong rambok, singautim rejois long ples bilong LORD, King.
PSA 98:7 Solwara igo i singsing, na olgeta samting i stap insait long em, graun, na olgeta manmeri i stap long en.
PSA 98:8 Wara i go pasim han bilong en, maunten i sing wantaim long joi.
PSA 98:9 Bipo long ai bilong Jehovah, em i kam long jedijim erth. Em bai jedijim wol long jastis na ol piple long ekuiti.
PSA 99:1 Lord i bos long throne; nesen i save harim na tetebil! Em i save sit long hap bilong kerubim; grand long graun i pairap!
PSA 99:2 Bikpela i go long olgeta long Sion; em i go hevi yet long olgeta ples.
PSA 99:3 Ol i givim prais long nem bilong yu bikpela na wei tumas—Em i holihol!
PSA 99:4 King bilong pawa i lavem jusis. Yu bilong plantim ripot; yu mekim jusis na righteousness long Jakob.
PSA 99:5 Liftim up olsem Bikpela God bilong yumi, wosip long pati bilong en; Em i holihol!
PSA 99:6 Moses na Aaron i stap long ol praist bilong Em; Samuel i stap long ol man we i kolim nem bilong Em. Ol i kolim i go long LORD, na Em i ansa ol.
PSA 99:7 Em i tokim ol long bus bilong klod; ol i holim kaeren bilong en, na statuts ol i givim ol.
PSA 99:8 LORD God bilong yumi, yu ansa ol. Yu i stap nau na yu givim forgiven long ol, tasol yu i kam bek long ol long pasin bilong ol.
PSA 99:9 Liftim up na pisinim olgetting long Lod i God bilong yumi, wosip long maunten bilong em we i stap halo, wantaim Lod i God bilong yumi em i man halo tru.
PSA 100:1 Wanpela Sang bilong tenkyu. Me kim tok harim gut long Jehova, olgeta graun.
PSA 100:2 Servim Lord wantaim belis; kam insait long em na sindaun wantaim sang bilong joy.
PSA 100:3 I gat save long ol tok bilong Jehovah. Em i God. Em i mekim mipela, na mipela i bilong em; mipela i pikinini bilong em, na ol sheep bilong em i stap long graun bilong en.
PSA 100:4 Go insait long gate bilong Em wantaim sankyu, na go insait long kot bilong Em wantaim preis; givim sankyu long Em, na blessim nem bilong Em.
PSA 100:5 Bikpela i gutpela, na lovinqi blong em i stap oltaim; fethfulness blong em i go daun long ol genarashon.
PSA 101:1 Sang bilong Dauid. Mipela bai singaut long stori bilong Diospla ren baluma na jastis; long yu, o Bikpela, mipela bai singim sang bilong pleseda.
PSA 101:2 Mi bai tingim gutpela rot — wanem taim yu kam long me? Mi bai wark long haus bilong mi wantaim het i stap katol.
PSA 101:3 Mai no ken go long olgeta samting nogut i kamap long ai bilong mi. Mi hamamas long wok bilong ol man i birua; em bai no stick long mi.
PSA 101:4 Hati i no orait bai lusim me; mi no save long hevi.
PSA 101:5 Husat i birua olsem long narapela man i stap mute, mi bai i stap mute; na husat ai bilong em i go het na haret bilong em i strong, mi no inap lakim em.
PSA 101:6 Mai bel isi i bikpela long ol gutpela man meri bilong kantri, ol ken stap wantaim mi; hu i go long rot bilong strepela sindaun em bai sarveim mi.
PSA 101:7 Nogat man i makol olsem pasal bai stap long haus bilong mi; nogat man i tok bagarap bai sanap long wei bilong mi.
PSA 101:8 Bikos long ta, mi bai kirap, inap mi katim ol man i warkim ol samting nogut i go, long siti bilong Papa.
PSA 102:1 Wanpela prea bilong wanpela i kamap strong i go daun, taim em i go daun na em i kirapim narapela kisim bek long en. Harim prea bilong mi, O Bikpela; laitim ror bilong mi i go long yu.
PSA 102:2 No ken haitim pes bilong Yu long dei bilong trabel bilong mi. Lusim han bilong Yu i go daun, na harim tok bilong mi; givim ansa quicklong long mi taim mi kisim tok.
PSA 102:3 Dei bilong mi i go daun olsem smok, na ol banis bilong mi i tan olsem emba i hot.
PSA 102:4 Hart bilong me i sakse, olsem gras i drai na stap; mi lusim kaikai bret, nogat tok.
PSA 102:5 Long olsem nau na mi singaut i go daun, bodimi bilong mi i kam antap long ol banis bilong mi.
PSA 102:6 Mi olsem kakaruk bilong bus, olsem kakaruk long puspus.
PSA 102:7 Mi stap awaken; mi olsem pisin wanpela long rooftop bilong haus.
PSA 102:8 Olgeta dei, enimis bilong me ol iuskim me, ol i laughterim me, na ol i kurseim me.
PSA 102:9 Mi kaikai ash olsem bret, na mi yet mixim dring bilong mi wantaim tia.
PSA 102:10 Bilong bikpela i stap long rausim na popo, yu pilim mi ap long han bilong yu, na yu kisim mi nau putim mi daun.
PSA 102:11 Dei bilong mi ol i go daun olsem shado longpela, na mi birua olsem gras.
PSA 102:12 Bikpela, yu sindaun long trohn oltaim; Nem bilong yu i go inap long olgenarasyon.
PSA 102:13 Yu kamap bek na givim bel hevi long Sion, wantaim taim we i orait nau – em i taim bilong givim em gupela bikpela hariap.
PSA 102:14 Ol i ambai long stoan bilong em, na yu mamafaka long dus bilong em.
PSA 102:15 Ol nesen bai pored long nem bilong GOD, na ol kings bilong graun olgeta bai pored long gutpela glori bilong yu.
PSA 102:16 Papa God bai mekim gen Sion; Em i kamap nau long glori bilong em.
PSA 102:17 Em bai go bek gen long prereman bilong ol destitute, em no birua prereman bilong ol.
PSA 102:18 Writim i go long buk, long genarason i kam bihain, na olsem narapela ples we i no yet katim tok, bai ol i givim prais long LORD.
PSA 102:19 Em i luk i daun long heit bilong haus lotu bilong En; LORD i wachim ol i go long heven i kamdaun long gras.
PSA 102:20 Long harim tok bilong prisona i kisim pain, lusiim ol man we i stap long dekisoin bilong dai.
PSA 102:21 Ol i autim nem bilong LORD long Sain na ol i givim prais long em long Jerusalem,
PSA 102:22 Wewan na kantri ol kam tanim servim LORD.
PSA 102:23 Em i bin brukim strong bilong me long rot, na em i katim dei bilong me.
PSA 102:24 Mi tok: "O Bikpela bilong mi, no bringim mi long halftaim bilong yia na dei bilong mi! Yia bilong yu i go we long olgenarasin.
PSA 102:25 Long taim bifo, yu bin mekim bikim graun, na heven i stap, em i wok bilong han bilong yu.
PSA 102:26 Ol bai i go daun, Yu yet yu stap; olgeta bai ol i bagarap olsem klambut. Olsem klambut Yu bai Yu chanjim ol, na ol bai ol i pas long.
PSA 102:27 Bareman Yu i stap olsem yet, na yia bilong yu bai i no ken finis.
PSA 102:28 Pikinini bilong servants bilong God bai I stap longpela na sindaun gut, na olegita bilong ol i kamap strong long ples bilong Yu.
PSA 103:1 Bilong Davit. Blessim LORD, o spirit bilong mi; olgeta samting i stap inside long mi, blessim nem holy bilong em.
PSA 103:2 Blessim LORD, o nalail soul bilong mi, no forgetim olgeta gupela wok bilong em —
PSA 103:3 Em i givim pardon long ol ogasta bilong yu, na em i holim ol sickness bilong yu.
PSA 103:4 Em i savim laip bilong yu long Maus Ol I Go Daun, na em i kisim krone long lov strong na karim, na givim i go long yu.
PSA 103:5 Em i givim yu gutpela samting olgeta, na klostu bilong yu i kamap gen olsem bilak.
PSA 103:6 Bikpela i mekim stret na justis long ol i katol.
PSA 103:7 Em i mekim bekim pasis bilong em long Moses, wok bilong en i go long ol pipol bilong Israel.
PSA 103:8 Papa God i stap klostu long paitim na i gat bel isi, em i nomoilong kas long rausim bel, na em i plenti long givim lav.
PSA 103:9 Em i no ken akusim mipela olsem oltaim, na em i no ken kepm long tok pisin bilong em yol.
PSA 103:10 Em i no bin givim pekela long yumi olsem yumi bin mekim samting nogut, na em i no bekim peki long yumi olsem olgeta samting nogut i kam.
PSA 103:11 Olgeta heven i go hap long graun, olsem nau bikpela lavu tru bilong em i stap long ol dispela i fearim em.
PSA 103:12 Olsem far i go long bihain bilong sun long mun bikpela, na olsem far tu em i kirapim sin bilong mipela long mipela.
PSA 103:13 Olsem papa i givim kros long pikinini, olsem na LORD i givim kros long ol manmeri husat i tremba long em.
PSA 103:14 Em i save long bodi bilong yumi; em i gat save olsem yumi ol i dust.
PSA 103:15 Long ol man, dei bilong em olsem gras—em i kamap strong olsem flawa bilong bus;
PSA 103:16 Wen wind i go pasim, em i bagarap nau, na ples bilong em i no gat memori long em gen.
PSA 103:17 Bai longlong taim bipo na longlong taim i kam, lovingselo bilong LORD i go long ol manmeri olsem ol i save fearim Em, na jastis bilong En i go long pikinini bilong ol pikinini.
PSA 103:18 Olsem na long ol manmeri husat i stap haitim kot bilong En, na husat i givim agrikal long tingim ol presep bilong En.
PSA 103:19 Papa God i stap long heven na em i makim trohn bilong en, na kingdom bilong em i bosim olgeta.
PSA 103:20 Blessim Lord, olgeta enjel bilong em i strong nogut ol i mekim wok bilong em, ol i harim tok bilong komanda bilong em.
PSA 103:21 Blessim Lord, olgeta paitim bilong em, yupela sarvim bilong en i mekim wil bilong em.
PSA 103:22 Blessim LORD, olgeta wok bilong em long ol ples we em i gat autoriti. Blessim LORD, O soul bilong mi!
PSA 104:1 Blessim LORD, o nalail spirit bilong mi! O LORD, God bilong mi, yu bikpela i tru; yu i kisim kas bilong glori na majesti.
PSA 104:2 Em i kapim lait olsem skarft bilong en; Em i stretim ot heven olsem haus bilong ples nakam,
PSA 104:3 Em i laiim timba bilong rum blong En long wara i go antap, em i mekim klau olsem kar bilong en, em i wokabaut long wing blong win.
PSA 104:4 Em i mekim win bilong en messenja, flaem bilong faia ol i servant bilong en.
PSA 104:5 Em i stapim erat long graun bilong en, nogat bai i mof i go.
PSA 104:6 Yu kisim i go ken olsem klos bilong yu; wara i stap antap long maunten.
PSA 104:7 Long yu tokim strongim ol, wara i ranawe i go; long saund bilong thunder yu, ol i harim go long wei—
PSA 104:8 Maunten i go ap, na vali i sindaun long ples yu givim ol i stap —
PSA 104:9 Yu wokim bek bilong ol, ol i no inap pas, na ol i no ken kam bek gen na kova olgeta graun.
PSA 104:10 Em i kirapim wata i kam long bus na vali; ol i ran i go insait long maunten.
PSA 104:11 Ol i givim draik long ol beast bilong bus; donki wil moa i kisim thairst blong ol i go daun.
PSA 104:12 Pipia i go stap besait long wara i kam ananit; ol i singaut wantaim long branis.
PSA 104:13 Em i givim wara long maunten from rumblong ples bilong en; erth i amamas long olgeta samting em i mekim, na ol wok bilong en i bringim mani benefis.
PSA 104:14 Em i mekim gras i gro long animpal, em i givim ka long ol man ol i wokim, na bringim kaikai i kam long graun.
PSA 104:15 Wain i mekim bel isi, ol i mekim pes bilong en i shine, na bret i save bel bilong en.
PSA 104:16 Diwai bilong LORD i kamap strong, diwai cedar bilong Lebanan em we Him planim,
PSA 104:17 we bilong pisin i mekim haus bilong ol long hap, na stok i mekim haus bilong em long diwai sipres.
PSA 104:18 Maunten hai i go long ol goat bilong bus, kalangal em i ples birua long ol rokrok.
PSA 104:19 Em mekim mun long givim taim bilong yia; san i save long go daun.
PSA 104:20 Yu bringim daknes, na em i kamap nait, na olgeta binatang bilong bus i wakabaut.
PSA 104:21 Ol yongpela lion i singaut long ol ka bilong ol, na oli saikim ka i kam bek long God.
PSA 104:22 Sana i kamap, na ol i go bek; ol i slip long ples bilong ol.
PSA 104:23 Man i go bek long wok bilong en na i wok harim long hap bilong en na i kamap long apinun.
PSA 104:24 Hamas olgeta wok bilong yu, Papa bilong olgeta! Yu mekim olgeta dispela long save nau; gras bilong earth i fulap long krea cha bilong yu.
PSA 104:25 Hia i stap solwara, bikpela na walap, i gat plenti animol olsem nogat nem, gutpela samting na liklik samting ol i stap long en.
PSA 104:26 Olap long hap, sip ol i pas, na Leviatan, we yu mekim bilong pley long hap.
PSA 104:27 Ol krea i lukim Yu, bai Yu givim ol kaikai bilong ol long taem we i kam.
PSA 104:28 Wanpela taim yu givim ol i go long ol, ol i kisim i go; wanka taim yu opim han bilong yu, ol i bel isi long gutpela samting.
PSA 104:29 Wanpela taim yu kaibrukim bek yu yet, ol i stap pret long fear; wanpela taim yu kirapim win blong ol, ol i dai na go bek long graun.
PSA 104:30 Wanpela taim yu salim Spirit bilong yu, ol i kamap nau, yu mekim gan agen pes bilong graun.
PSA 104:31 Glori bilong LORD i stap oltaim; LORD i amamas long wok bilong En.
PSA 104:32 Em i lukim long graun, na graun i skelim; Em i tachim maunten, na ol maunten i kukum.
PSA 104:33 Mi bai singim sang long Jehovah long ol lif blong mi; mi bai singim prais long God bilong mi long ol taim we mi stap.
PSA 104:34 Toksave bilong mi i mas lukim gut long en, wantaim mi amamas long Jehovah.
PSA 104:35 Ol sinna i dai pinis long graun, ol nogut i no stap gen. Blessim LORD, o sowl bilong mi. Haleluya!
PSA 105:1 Givim sanksem long LORD, kisim nem bilong Em i go; tusim ol samting em i mekim long ol narapela kantri.
PSA 105:2 Singim sang long Em, singim prais long Em; tokim ol samting namba wan we Em i mekim, ol wunders bilong En.
PSA 105:3 Givim prais long nem bilong em we i holip; harten bilong ol man i kamap strong long lukim LORD, bai oli amamas.
PSA 105:4 Sukim olsem i go long LORD na strong bilong em; olsem yu mas sukim pes bilong em oltaim.
PSA 105:5 Rimembiri ol samting bikpela na tokstrong em i bin mekim, ol samting namba wan i bin mekim, na ol tokstrong em i bin givim.
PSA 105:6 O pikinini bilong servant belong Him Abraham, O sussa bilong Jacob, ol pipol we Him i pikim.
PSA 105:7 Em i Bikpela God bilong yumi; Judgment bilong em i go ol abaot long graun.
PSA 105:8 Em i memorim agrirement bilong Em oltaim, wod em i tok bai i stap long thousand generashon —
PSA 105:9 Ilip pinisim Covenant bilong em long Abraham, na oath we em i tok long Isaac.
PSA 105:10 Em konfirmim olsem long Jacob olsem wanpela laen, long Israel olsem wanpela kovenan we no gat ende.
PSA 105:11 Mi bai givim yu lan bilong Kanaan olsem hap bilong inhiritans bilong yu.
PSA 105:12 Taim ol i liklik tasol, i few in namba, na ol i man i stap long kantri, em i no ples bilong ol, ol i stranger long hap.
PSA 105:13 Ol i go wail long nasyon, na ol i go long wan kingdom na go long narapela kingdom.
PSA 105:14 Em i no lusim man i bagarapim ol; em i strongim tok long king bilong ol long hap bilong ol.
PSA 105:15 Yu no ken tetchim ol man meri we mi bin anointim! Yu no ken wariharim ol profet bilong mi!
PSA 105:16 Em i kisim i kam famin long kantri na katim gras bilong ol, na ol i no inap kaikai.
PSA 105:17 Em i salim Josph long bifor ol, na ol i salim em olsem wanpela slave.
PSA 105:18 Ol i kurim pasim lek bilong em wantaim barak, na ol i putim nek bilong em insait long ain.
PSA 105:19 Na go long tingting bilong en i kam tru na tok bilong LORD i strongim em.
PSA 105:20 King i sendim em na lusim em; bikman bilong ol pipol i givim em fri.
PSA 105:21 Em i bikpela long en, em i bos bilong olgeta samting bilong en.
PSA 105:22 I instruktim prinis bilong en olsem hem laik, na tisim bikpela man bilong en long save.
PSA 105:23 Na Isrel i go insait long Egip; Jakob i stap long kantri bilong Ham.
PSA 105:24 Na Bikpela i mekim pipol bilong em i kamap planti, ol i kalap long nemigo bilong ol.
PSA 105:25 Husat hart bilong ol i hamarim long hate, ol i toktok long mekim plan agensim servit bilong En, na ol i hatim piple bilong En.
PSA 105:26 Em bingim Mosis haus boi, na Aron, wampela em i pikinim.
PSA 105:27 Ol i mekim singsing bilong em we i amaze olgeta long ol, na wonders long lan bilong Ham.
PSA 105:28 Em i kirapim dak i kam, na dak i kamap — yet ol i no lissen tok bilong Em.
PSA 105:29 Em i bringim blod long wara bilong ol, na ol fis bilong ol i dai.
PSA 105:30 Kantri bilong ol i pulap long rop, na ol i go long hap bilong king bilong ol.
PSA 105:31 Em i tok, na ol kunai i kamapim olgeta wail – ol buk na ol kunai i stap long olgeta hap bilong kantri.
PSA 105:32 Em i givim ol hail bilong ren, wantaim lait long olgeta graun bilong ol.
PSA 105:33 Em i kilim vin blong ol, figi, na i brokim diwai bilong kantri blong ol.
PSA 105:34 Em i tok, na lokis yangpela i kam, ol i go long olgeta, i no gat nakamal.
PSA 105:35 Ol i kaikai olgeta kala na ol i lamakim produis bilong graun bilong ol.
PSA 105:36 Em i kilim olgeta pikinini bilong papa long kantri bilong ol, ol bikpela samting bilong strong bilong ol.
PSA 105:37 Em i kam bek long Israel wantaim sila na gol, na i no gat wanpela long tribe bilong en i slip.
PSA 105:38 Ejip i amenas long taim ol Israel i go pinis, bikos wikim fear blong ol Israel i kam stap long ol.
PSA 105:39 Em i skelim kunai olsem samting bilong kovara, na em i givim faia bilong luminaim nait.
PSA 105:40 Ol i askim, na Em i kam bringim pisin quail, na em i suf monim olgeta wantaim bret bilong heaven.
PSA 105:41 Em i opim ston, na wara i kamaut strong; ol i flow olsem wanpela river long bus.
PSA 105:42 Em i remember pomis bilong em we em i halvahim long Abraham, servant bilong em.
PSA 105:43 Em i kirapim pipo bilong En long hap blong hamamas, na ol pipo em i bikim bilong En wantaim ol singsing bilong jubel.
PSA 105:44 Em i givim olgeta lain bilong narapela kantri, olsem oli ken kisim birua bilong wok bilong arapela man.
PSA 105:45 Ol i holim statut blong Em, na ol i obeyim loa blong Em. Aleluya!
PSA 106:1 Haleluya! Givim tankyu long LORD, bikos Em i gutpela; Lovin bilong en i stap oltaim.
PSA 106:2 Hu ina ken toksave ol samting bikpela we Bikpela i mekim, o kisim bek na tok stret long halepim praiz bilong En?
PSA 106:3 Ol i blesim ol mana, ol i halivim jusis, ol i wokim derek long ol taim.
PSA 106:4 Rimem long mi, Papa God, long moning yu yet long ol pipol bilong yu; kam bek gen long mi wantaim sevensesen bilong yu.
PSA 106:5 Mipela bai lukim prospariti bilong pipol we yu pikinini, hamamas long gladnes bilong nesen bilong yu, na givim glorii long inekens bilong yu.
PSA 106:6 Mipela i go hevi olsem tumbuna bilong mipela; mipela i mekim rong, na mipela i warkim ol samting nogut.
PSA 106:7 Papa bilong yumi long Egip ol i no save longing kamapim wonda bilong Yu, na yumi yet mas remember gutpela kain bilong Yu; tasol ol i bagarap long solwara, long Red Solwara.
PSA 106:8 Em i save ol long nem bilong Em, olsem Em i ken showim pawa bilong Em.
PSA 106:9 Em i tokim strong long Solwara Red, na em i drai pinis; Em i bringim ol long underside olsem long ples kanaka.
PSA 106:10 Em i save ol long han bilong poisen, na em i bekim ol long han bilong enemy.
PSA 106:11 Warais i kamapim ol eni; maski wanpela tasol i no stap.
PSA 106:12 Ol bilivim promis bilong En, na ol singim sang bilong en, preis bilong En.
PSA 106:13 Bai ol i lusim bekim快 long wok bilong Em, na ol i no bihain wail kaunsil bilong Em.
PSA 106:14 Ol i gat bikpela laik longlong long kantry kolddown, na ol i traim God long bus.
PSA 106:15 Em i givim tok bilong ol, tasol em i salim sik bilong bagarap i go long ol.
PSA 106:16 Long ples, ol i sikim Mosese, na Aron tu, man bilong Bikpela we i holy.
PSA 106:17 Gras i go op na kulkim Dathan, na i kivim assembli bilong Abiram.
PSA 106:18 Na faia i kukim ol long kompani bilong ol, flaem i kaikai ol nogut.
PSA 106:19 Long Horeb, ol i mekim bulmakau na ol i servisim imij bilong molten.
PSA 106:20 Ol i switim Glori bilong ol long piksa bilong bulmakau i kaikai gras.
PSA 106:21 Ol i lusim Bikpela Papa bilong ol, Jehovah bilong ol, we mekim bikpela wok long Egip.
PSA 106:22 Wok bilong God i amaze long kantri bilong Ham, na wok bilong God i tru strong long sait bilong Red Si.
PSA 106:23 Em i tok olsem em bai bagarapim ol – tasol Mususi, pikinini choisen bilong en, i stap bifoa em long hap blo pait, olsem em inap pasim bel hat bilong en long bagarapim ol.
PSA 106:24 Ol i lakisim kantri paisa; ol i no bilivim promis bilong en.
PSA 106:25 Ol i bikim sori long hap bilong ol, na ol i no harim voys bilong LORD.
PSA 106:26 Em i lifim han bilong en, em i kamakim tok long kasim ol i daun long bus.
PSA 106:27 Ol i skulim ol pikinini bilong ol long ol nesen, na ol i kirapim ol long olgeta hap graun.
PSA 106:28 Ol i joineim ol yet long Baal bilong Peor na ol i kaikai sakrisis ol i ofrim long dag na debil.
PSA 106:29 Ol i mekim wok nasal, na ol i kisim bel hevi long LORD, na sik bubu i kamap long ol.
PSA 106:30 Finehas i stap na em kam bekim wok, na pes bilong dei i stop pinis.
PSA 106:31 Em i kamapim righteousness long en olsem justice na streit long olgenarason i go i go.
PSA 106:32 Long wanpela wara Meribah, ol i kirapim LORD, na trable i kam long Moses bikos ol.
PSA 106:33 Ol i bagarap long Spirit bilong Em, na Mosis i tok harim long maus bilong en.
PSA 106:34 Oli no bin bagarapim pilipil igcen olsem Jehovah i tokim ol.
PSA 106:35 Bai ol i miksim wantaim ol nesen na ol i kisim kastom bilong ol.
PSA 106:36 Ol i wosipim idol bilong ol, na ol i kamapim trap long ol.
PSA 106:37 Ol i pilai pikinini man na pikinini meri long demon.
PSA 106:38 Ol i kilim blod bilong man we no bin mekim rong – blod bilong ol pikinini na ol meri, olsem ol i bikim sacrifice long figur bilong spirit bilong Kanana, na gras bilong kantri i punda long blod.
PSA 106:39 Ol i birua yet olsem long wok ol i mekim, na ol i sakim yet olsem long kaman ol i wokim.
PSA 106:40 Pasen bilong Jehovah i las long kantri na pipol bilong en, na em i pikimpek long inheritance bilong en.
PSA 106:41 Em i givim ol i go long hap bilong ol nesen, na ol i bilong dispela taim i bin hatim ol, na ol i bin bosim ol.
PSA 106:42 Enimig i winim ol, mekim ol i daun long han bilong ol.
PSA 106:43 Em i skulim ol long taim olgeta, tasol ol i birua long wari na sindaun i go daun long olgeta nogut pasin bilong ol.
PSA 106:44 Na em i harim bek bek bilong ol, em i save long sorimi bilong ol.
PSA 106:45 Na Em i rememberim covenant bilong Em wantaim ol, na em i kam bek gen long plenti bilong lovingseli bilong en.
PSA 106:46 Em i mekim olsem samting bilong pite long ol husat i holim ol long hap.
PSA 106:47 Bikpela, LORD God bilong mipela, seyvem mipela, kisim mipela long ol narion, na mipela inap givim sankyu long nem halow bilong yu, na mipela ken proud long preis bilong yu.
PSA 106:48 Papa God bilong Israel em i blesim long taim bipo na long taim i kam. Ol pipol olsem wan tok, "Amen!" Haleluya!
PSA 107:1 Givim sanksem long LORD, bikos em i gutpela; Lovin kare ba em i stap oltaim.
PSA 107:2 Ol i savemon long LORD mas tok olsem, ol i we LORD im bin bebem bek long han bilong poi.
PSA 107:3 Na ol i kam bek long ol kantri, long east na west, long not na saut.
PSA 107:4 Ol i go wail long ples nogat diwai, ol i no finisim rod long go long tanin hus, we em bai ol i stap.
PSA 107:5 Ol i bel kol na ol i thirsty; spirit bilong ol i kamakim long insait bilong ol.
PSA 107:6 Tisa ol i kirap strong long LORDE long taim ol i stap in trabel, na Em i savum ol long sik mama.
PSA 107:7 Em i lidim ol long stret na pas go long ples bilong taun wahan ol i ken stap.
PSA 107:8 Oli tok tumbuna long han bilong Jehovah long nupela pasin bilong en, na long wondia bilong en long ol pikinini man.
PSA 107:9 Em i pasim ol thausti na i kaikai i go long ol hungri na mekim ol i kamap strong long samting gudi.
PSA 107:10 Ol i sindaun long dek na long saed blong ded, ol prisenis long trabel na kais.
PSA 107:11 Bilong ol i bagarap long tok bilong God, na ol i kisim olgeta kaikai long toktok bilong Bikpela.
PSA 107:12 Em i bringim bel bilong ol i daun long taim bilong warkim strong, na ol i birua, na i no gat man i halivim.
PSA 107:13 Ol i kirap strong long LORD long taim ol i stap long trabel, na Em i save ol, painim ol long narapela hevi.
PSA 107:14 Em i kamautim ol long dak na shedow bilong dei, na ol i brukim chain bilong ol.
PSA 107:15 Ol i mas givim sanksem long LORD from hap bilong en, long lovting bilong en, na ol wonda i mekim long pikinini man.
PSA 107:16 Em i brukim daun geta bilong bronzu, na em i kat thromu bar bilong aian.
PSA 107:17 Ol i no save, long olgets we bilong ol, ol i kirapim, na ol i kamapim bikos long olgets we nogut, ol i kisim sik.
PSA 107:18 Ol i bikhat long ol ka, na ol i go klostu long gate bilong ded.
PSA 107:19 Ol i kirap strong long LORD long taim ol i stap in trabel, na Em i save ol.
PSA 107:20 Em i sendim wod bilong En na em i helem ol; Em i savem ol long hap bilong deat.
PSA 107:21 Ol i givim tankyu long LORD fromwe bilong en i kamap strong na wondar bilong en i mekim long ol pikinini man.
PSA 107:22 Ol i mas givim sakrifis bilong tankyu na tokim wok bilong Em wantaim bel hap.
PSA 107:23 Ol i go long solwara insait long sip, na ol i wokim bismis long wara bikpela.
PSA 107:24 Ol i lukim wok bilong LORD, na ailos bilong en long hap bilong solwara.
PSA 107:25 Em i tok na kamapim win blong storms, na em i liftim wav na wata blong solwara.
PSA 107:26 Ol i go aplde long heven, na ol i sindaun long bubu; gutpela bilong ol i brukim long sori tru bilong ol.
PSA 107:27 Ol i go bek, ol i stilim olsem ol i dring strong, na olgeta save bilong ol i no moa wankain.
PSA 107:28 Ol i singaut long LORDE long taim ol i stap na kasem sori na hevi, na Em i kam bekim ol, na i bringim ol i kukim  long hap bilong sori na hevi.
PSA 107:29 Em i stilim strong win kaikai long tok pkinpkin, na wels bilong solwara i no gat sais.
PSA 107:30 Ol i amamas long tait, na em i bringim ol long ka long hapot i tambuonai ol.
PSA 107:31 Ol i mas givim sanksem long LORD from hap bilong het i go long en, na ol samting nais i mekim long pikinini man.
PSA 107:32 Oli givim bikim em i go hap long assembli bilong ol pipol, na oli preisim em long kaunsil bilong ol bikpela man.
PSA 107:33 Em i bringim river na mekim desot, spring water i kamap graun i dai long wara.
PSA 107:34 Na graun i stap planti ka i kamapim felis blong solwara, bilong olgeta nogut pasin blong ol pipol i stap.
PSA 107:35 Em i bringim desert long olgeta wara, na graun i dai long olgeta spring.
PSA 107:36 Em i mekim ol hungri i kam na sindaun, oli stap long ples na mekim taun long en, long ples ia ol i ken stap.
PSA 107:37 Ol i planim graun na plantim vineya, na ol i kamap na givim kupla ful harves.
PSA 107:38 Em i givim blessing long ol, na ol i multiplai planti; em i no lifim olgeta animals bilong ol i lak.
PSA 107:39 Wanpela taim ol i kamdaun, ol i wari long sikisipen, hevi, na sori,
PSA 107:40 Em i kirapim disrespek long ol biceman meri, na em i mekim ol i go long ples i no gat trek, dasol.
PSA 107:41 Bikpela i kirapim ol i no gat samting long trouble na sorere, na em i multiplicim ol famili bilong ol olsem ol animol bilong ol.
PSA 107:42 Ol i gat save i lukim na kamap hap hap, na ol geta samting nogut i stap maut.
PSA 107:43 Em wei igat save, em kisim notis long dispela samting na tingim gutpela lavin bilong Papa God.
PSA 108:1 Wanpela sang. Wanpela psalm bilong Daud. Hart bilong me em i stap strong, o God; bai mi singim na miki musik wantaim olgeta insait bilong me.
PSA 108:2 Kam bek, o hap na laip! Mi bai kam bekim moning.
PSA 108:3 Mi bai givim prais long yu, o Bikpela, long olgeta nesen; mi bai singim sang bilong yu long olgeta pipol.
PSA 108:4 Yu kilim olgeta na stap i go longwe na pas Bai yu trai istap i go longlong klau.
PSA 108:5 O God, kam longwe na i go ap, we long olgeta heven; glori bilong yu ken kisim long olgeta graun.
PSA 108:6 Givim tok na savim mipela long han rait bilong yu, na ol manmeri yu gat laik long ol bai kamap strong.
PSA 108:7 God i tok from hause lotu: "Mi bai winim! Mi bai givim Sukem long ol pipol, na mi bai dividim Vali of Sukkot.
PSA 108:8 Gilead i bilong mi, na Manase i bilong mi; Efraim em i het bilong mi, Judah em i szepta bilong mi.
PSA 108:9 Moab em i basin bilong mi; long Edom mi kisim sandal bilong mi na tromoi i go; long Philistia mi singautim win.
PSA 108:10 Husat bai kisim mi go long siti i gat barikeli? Husat bai lidim mi go long Edom?
PSA 108:11 O God, yupela i no tromoi mipela? Bai yupela i no kam daun gen wantaim ol solja bilong mipela?
PSA 108:12 Givim mipela hap long enemy, wantaim olgeta halivim bilong man i no gat bek.
PSA 108:13 Wantaim Bikpela God, yumi wokim bravely, na em bai krungim ol enemy bilong yumi.
PSA 109:1 Long taim bilong singsing masis. Wanpela sang bilong Davit. O God bilong priezim mi, no ken siwit.
PSA 109:2 Ol i nogut na ol i giaman, maus ol i bikim olsem, na toktok i go long mi; ol i toktok long mi wantaim tok bokis.
PSA 109:3 Ol i kam aut long mi wantaim tok bilong het, na ol i katim mi long nogat rison.
PSA 109:4 Long toktok bilong mi yet, ol i tok bes against mi, tasol mi man bilong beten.
PSA 109:5 Ol i givim mi nogut long hap blong gutpela, na hatred long love blong mi.
PSA 109:6 Putim man bilong hevi i go apo long em; letim wanpela man i kam kasem i stap long han rait bilong em.
PSA 109:7 Wanpela em i kam kas, em i stap long hevi, na praya bilong em bai i kamap long sind.
PSA 109:8 Dei bilong em i no long; narapela man i ken kam bihainim posisen bilong em.
PSA 109:9 Ol pikinini bilong em i no gat papa, na meri bilong em i bikim widou.
PSA 109:10 Ol pikinini bilong em bai go walalang olsem ol i bekim moni, ol i lukim ka longwe farawe long husat ol i bagarap.
PSA 109:11 Mipela i harim ol man bilong ples bai kaikaim, na ol narapela man i stap long ples bai kisim i go ol samting em i warkim.
PSA 109:12 Igat nokis man i ken givim kaekae long em, na igat nokis man i ken stap wantaim ol pikinini we i no gat papa bilong en.
PSA 109:13 Ol descent bilong en bai katim ol, na nem bilong ol bai rausim i go long jenaration nambaut.
PSA 109:14 Hevi bilong tumbuna i go long ol bifor Bikpela, na nogat wanpela sin bilong mama bai i stap klost long buk.
PSA 109:15 Sin bilong ol i mas stap oltaim bifor ai bilong LORD, na Hem i mas katim of ol memori long graun.
PSA 109:16 Em i no tingim showim gutpela sindaun, tasol em i go bek long ol pikinini, ol i no gat samting, na ol brukhert, oleta go long wei bilong dai.
PSA 109:17 Ol kakai we em i lovim, em i kam daun long en; ol blesin we em i no laik bilivim, em i go longwe liklik long en.
PSA 109:18 Kisim kros olsem kot i bin kisim, bai em i go daun insait long bodi bilong en olsem wara, na long bun bilong en olsem oil.
PSA 109:19 Em i mas olsem skat wapis long en, olsem belt i taitim foreva namel long en.
PSA 109:20 Mipela hop ripot bilong LORD i go long ol pipel i tok bisman long me.
PSA 109:21 Bikpela Papa bilong heaven, yu helpim mi gut long namel bilong yu; savesim mi long gutpela lovinkind bilong yu.
PSA 109:22 Mi bikpela i no gat, na mi i masalai tu; haret bilong mi i katikati wounded.
PSA 109:23 Mi go daun olsem shado i go long; mi pusim i go olsem bikpela kunai.
PSA 109:24 Kni bilong me i stap sik olsem nau long taim bilong kaikai nogat, na bodi bilong me em i kamap narapela na klostu.
PSA 109:25 Mi bel bilong kokomo long ol i krungim mi; wanpela ol i lukim mi, ol i kisim hed bilong ol i shake.
PSA 109:26 PAPA bilong mi Bikpela, halivim mi; savim mi long stap insait iet bilong yu.
PSA 109:27 Ol i save, em i han bilong yu, yu, Bikpela, yu mekim dispela.
PSA 109:28 Ol i kilim tok baksait, bai yu givim bikpela blessing. Wanpela taim ol i kamap, ol bai kisim shame na sori, be yu servent bai amamas.
PSA 109:29 Ol i mas i kisim klos blong sham; ol i mas i wapim shame bilong ol olsem klip.
PSA 109:30 Long maus bilong me bai mi givim sankyu long LORDE i go olsem; bai mi praisim Em i go long ples bilong olgeta.
PSA 109:31 Em i stap long hap right han bilong man i no gat kala, long salvim em from ol i save kondem spirits bilong em.
PSA 110:1 Sang bilong Dauid. Bikpela i tokim Long bilong mi: “Si dung banis long han bilong mi long taem we bai mi mekim ol eni bilong yu ol i stap long graun olsem fotstul bilong yu.”
PSA 110:2 Papa God i stap stretim bikpela szepta bilong yu long Sayan: "Yu bos long mekim desisen insait long ol aibam."
PSA 110:3 Ol pipol bilong yu bai i kam volente long de bilong yu we yu go fight. Ol i dressap long wei bilong halivim splenda, from bel bilong moning, na dew bilong yut bilong yu em belong yu.
PSA 110:4 LORD i makim olegis na no inap binim mai: "Yu stap priest foreva long rope bilong Melkisetek."
PSA 110:5 Papa God i stap long rait han bilong yu; Em bai bagarap ol kings long de bilong em i popo.
PSA 110:6 Em bai jijim nem bilong ol narapela kantri, bagarapim ol bikman long wei na long wei, na ol dai pinis i stap kisim tupela na tripela.
PSA 110:7 Em bai dringim wara long craik long rot; olsem na Em bai lifim op hed bilong En.
PSA 111:1 Haleluya! Mi bai givim sanksem long Papa bilong ol, wantaim olgeta hatis bilong mi, long kaunsil bilong ol i stap raits na long miting bilong ol.
PSA 111:2 Wok bilong Bikpela i gret; ol i mas tingim olgeta long tin na lukim strong.
PSA 111:3 Wok bilong em i gutpela tru, na gat bikpela pes; justis bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 111:4 Em i mekim ol samting nais i kam long memori bilong yumi; LORD em i gat hatwok long stap na em i amamas.
PSA 111:5 Em i givim ka long ol i wetem respek long Em; Em i remember tupela i makim pinis foreva.
PSA 111:6 Em i mekim bekim ol pipol bilong em long strongpela wok bilong em, na em i givim ol inheritance long ol narawan pes.
PSA 111:7 Wok bilong han bilong Em i stap long tru na jastis; ol ples save long Em i kamap strong tru.
PSA 111:8 Ol i stap strong longwe longwe, na olgeta samting i kamap long truth na jus.
PSA 111:9 Em i salim bekim ripresen bilong pisin long ol pikinini bilong En; Em i wanpela tok bilong en long ol Pikinini bilong En, em i stap foreva; holi na gat bigpela respek i stap long Nem bilong En.
PSA 111:10 Respek long Jehovah em i stap long wisdom; ol manmeri i folow ripot bilong Em i gat save nau long undestanding. Prais bilong Em i stap lasting eternali!
PSA 112:1 Haliluya! Man i blesim, em i gat respek long LORD, na em i amamas tumas long komandyasyon bilong Em.
PSA 112:2 Ol desenden bilong em bai i stap strong long graun; genarason bilong ol man i stap raite bai i kamap blessed.
PSA 112:3 Moni na gupla i stap long haus bilong em, na raitim bilong en i stap oltaim.
PSA 112:4 Lait i kamap long dokis long ol man i stap straigt – ol i gat bel isi, karem yumi, na ol i stap raits.
PSA 112:5 Olsem gut long man husat i go long stret na givim planti, lenden fri, na husat i wokim bilong en i stap insait long jusis.
PSA 112:6 Em i no bai katolong oltaim; man righteous bai stap long memorika forever.
PSA 112:7 Em i no afred long tok bilong hevi; haret bilong em i strong, na em i putim trast long LORD.
PSA 112:8 Haten bilong en em strong, em i no afraid, na em laik winim ol enemy bilong en.
PSA 112:9 Em i kirapim gutpela samting long ol pipol i no gat, raitim bilong em i stap oltaim; korn bilong en i go antap long bikpela respek.
PSA 112:10 Man bilong evil i go see na bai i sori; bai em i kirapim tooth na i stap nating; laikim bilong man bilong evil bai i dai pinis.
PSA 113:1 Halaleya! Givim prais, o wokmanmeri bilong LORD; praisim nem bilong LORD.
PSA 113:2 Blesim na stap long nem bilong Bikpela, long taim bai i go i go.
PSA 113:3 Long pla bilong san i go ap long pla bilong san i go daun, nem bilong LORD i tanim.
PSA 113:4 LORD i go hap long olgeta nesen, glory bilong em i go hap long heven.
PSA 113:5 Hus i olsem LORD God bilong yumi, em i sindaun long hevi?
PSA 113:6 Em i kam daun yet long lukim heven na graun.
PSA 113:7 Em i kirapim ol pikinini long gras na i liftim up ol i no gat samting long kamp bilong rabis.
PSA 113:8 Givim ol i sit wantaim bikpela manmeri, wantaim prins bilong piple God.
PSA 113:9 Em i stap laik mami bilong pkinini olsem mami i amamas long pikinini, long haus bilong em, olsem mami i amamas long ol pikinini bilong em. Haliliuya!
PSA 114:1 Wanpela taim Isrel i go bek long Egip, haus bilong Yakob i kamap long ol pipol we i usim tok ples narapela.
PSA 114:2 Juda i kamap ples bilong Halivim bilong God, na Isrel em i ples bilong pawa bilong En.
PSA 114:3 Solwara i lukim na i ranawe; Jodan i tanim bek;
PSA 114:4 Maunten igo i skip olsem ram, hil igo i skip olsem lem.
PSA 114:5 Olsem wanem, O solwara, yu ranawe, O Jordan, yu turnim bek?
PSA 114:6 O maunten, bai yumu skipim olsem ram, O hil, bai yumi skipim olsem lamb?
PSA 114:7 Poro, o erth, long wei bilong presens bilong Lod, long wei bilong presens bilong God bilong Yakob.
PSA 114:8 hu i kamapim ston na bilong wara, na flint i go bekim fountain bilong wara!
PSA 115:1 Nogat long yumi, Papa God, nogat long yumi, ba tasol long nem bilong yu, gitori i go long yu, bikos yu gat olgeta ren na toktok, bikos yu gat olgeta wailis na strongpela hap.
PSA 115:2 Ol nesen i tok, "God blong ol i stap we?"
PSA 115:3 God bilong yumi i stap long heven; Em i mekim ol samting we em i laik.
PSA 115:4 Idol ol bilong ol, silva na gol, em i wokim ol long han bilong man.
PSA 115:5 Ol i gat maus, tasol ol i no inap tok; ol i gat ai, tasol ol i no inap luk
PSA 115:6 Ol i gat yut, bas ol i no inap harim; ol i gat nus, bas ol i no inap smel
PSA 115:7 Ol i gat han, tasol ol i no inap feelim; ol i gat leg, tasol ol i no inap wokabaut; ol i no inap tok birua yet long naraka bilong ol.
PSA 115:8 Ol i mekim ol, bikim olsem ol, na olgeta i putim bilip long ol.
PSA 115:9 O Isrel, putim traust long LORD! Em i help na shiled bilong ol.
PSA 115:10 O hus bilong Aron, putim trast long Lod! Em i holimapim na em i skil bilong ol.
PSA 115:11 Yupela i go bikpela long Jehova, yupela i trast long Jehova! Em i heli bilong ol, na em i skil bilong ol.
PSA 115:12 Papa God i save gut long yumi; Em bai givim bikpela blessing long yumi. Em bai givim bikpela blessing long aus Israel; Em bai givim bikpela blessing long aus Aalon.
PSA 115:13 Em bai givim blessing long ol man i fear long Papa God — liklik na bikpela olsem.
PSA 115:14 Mipela i laik LORD i givim yu na ol pikinini bilong yu planti.
PSA 115:15 Yu ken blesim long han bilong GOD, Meka bilong heven na graun.
PSA 115:16 Heven ili i belongim long LORD, tasol erth em i givim long ol man.
PSA 115:17 Ol dai i no inap givim prais long Lod, na ol samting we i go daun long ples silent.
PSA 115:18 Yumi ol i blesim LORD long taim nau na moa. Aleluya!
PSA 116:1 Mi lavim LORD, wantaim em i harim tok bilong mi, plaem bilong mi long meri.
PSA 116:2 Bikos em i kisim ear bilong en na lusim i go daun long me, bai mi karim tok bilong mi go long em olpela taim bilong mi yet.
PSA 116:3 Ropis bilong dei i kam bekim mi; sori bilong Sheol i winim mi; trouble na sori i kam astan long mi.
PSA 116:4 Mi karim nem bilong Jehovah: "O Jehovah, kisim na save soul bilong me!"
PSA 116:5 Lord i stap graun na ret; God bilong yumi i fulup long kros.
PSA 116:6 Papa God i lukautim ol pipel i nogut saving long tok; mi no inap harim, na em i savim mi.
PSA 116:7 Go bek long ples bilong yu yet, o spirits bilong me, wantaim LORD i bin givim yu gutpela samting.
PSA 116:8 Long yu bin save laip bilong me from dei, ai bilong me from tia, lek bilong me from pundaun.
PSA 116:9 Mi bai wok bifor Bikpela long graun bilong ol samting i gat laip.
PSA 116:10 Mi bilip, olesem na mi tokim, "Mi i katik tru, mi savesek long sufoka"
PSA 116:11 Long taim mi bel isi, mi tok, "Ol man i gat bikpela laip!"
PSA 116:12 Mipela i gat wei wanpela long bekim tok bilong Jehovah ol geta gutpela samting we em mekim long mipela?
PSA 116:13 Mipela bai kisim kap salvesen na mipela bai kolim nem bilong LORD.
PSA 116:14 Mi bai potoim ol promis bilong me long LORD long as bilong ol pipel ol i stap.
PSA 116:15 Narakain long luk bilong Bikpela na mipela man i go dae olsem na saint bilong em.
PSA 116:16 Olsem tru, Papa God, mi servat bilong Yu; mi servat, pikinini bilong hap meri bilong Yu; Yu bromim bel hevi bilong mi.
PSA 116:17 Mi bai givim sakrifis bilong tenkyu long yu na mi bai kolim nem bilong LORD.
PSA 116:18 Mi bai mekim pinis pren long hap bilong LORD long ol pipol.
PSA 116:19 Long kot bilong haus bilong LORD, long mit bilong yu, O Jerusalem. Haleluya!
PSA 117:1 Praizim LORD, olegita nesen! Mekim bikpela tok bilong Em, olegita pipol!
PSA 117:2 Rausim olgeta lavin blong hem long mipela i bikpela, na faithfulness bilong LORD em i stap oltaim. Haliluya!
PSA 118:1 Givim tankyu long LORD, em i gutpela; Lovin karai bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 118:2 Oli tok long Israel, “Lovin tingim Em i save stap oltaim.”
PSA 118:3 Haus bilong Aron i tok, “Lovin kindness bilong em i stap oltaim.”
PSA 118:4 Ol i save tasol long Jehovah i tok, “Lovin kare ba hem i stap oltaim.”
PSA 118:5 Long taim bilong sori na trabel, mi singaut long Bikpela, na em i ankam na em i givim mi fri.
PSA 118:6 Papa God i stap nambis na sai; mi no bin kirapim fear. Wanem man i ken mekim long mi?
PSA 118:7 LORD i stap nabaut long me; Em i holide bilong me. Olegeda, mi go lukim winim ol i hatim mie.
PSA 118:8 I gudepela long kisim rifuj long LORD nau long trast long man.
PSA 118:9 I gat betta long kisim kaivakaba long LORD na nogat long putim bilip long prins.
PSA 118:10 Olgeta nesen i kam ronim mi, tasol long namel bilong LORD, mi kilim ol.
PSA 118:11 Ol i kam raunim mi long olgeta sait, tasol long namel bilong Papa bilong mipela, mi kisim ol i go.
PSA 118:12 Ol i kam antap long me olsem bi, tasol ol i mati pinis olsem ponki i bun; long nem bilong LORD mi kisim ol i go.
PSA 118:13 Ol i pusim mi strong, na mi i go daun, tasol Bikpela i halivim mi.
PSA 118:14 Papa God em i stap long me long strong, na em i stap long me long sang, na Em i kamap saveman bilong me.
PSA 118:15 Kraisim bilong joi na selvishen i go daun long haus bilong ol righteous: “Han ratt bilong Bikpela i wok strongpela, ol i kamap gutpela!”
PSA 118:16 Han rait bilong LORD i go hap! Han rait bilong LORD i wok strong na gut!
PSA 118:17 Mi no ken dai, bain mi bai livim na tokim ol samting we LORD i mekim.
PSA 118:18 Papa God i skulim mi strong long taim, tasol em i no givim mi long dei.
PSA 118:19 Openim gate bilong righteousness long me, na mi bai go insait na givim sankyu long LORD.
PSA 118:20 Em i gate bilong LORD; ol righteous bai go insait long em.
PSA 118:21 Bai mi givim sankyu long yu, Yus hariap long tok bilong mi, na Yu kam bekim saveman bilong mi.
PSA 118:22 Ston i wokman i rausim em i kamap na kornerston.
PSA 118:23 Em i kam long han bilong LORD, na em i wari long ai bilong mipela.
PSA 118:24 Em i dei we Papa God i mekim; yumi bai hamamas na katol long em.
PSA 118:25 Papa God, savim mipela. Mipela i bikim bek long yu, Papa God, wokim mipela i kamap strong!
PSA 118:26 Blesim i kam long nem bilong LORD. Long haus bilong LORD mipela blesim yu.
PSA 118:27 LORD em i God; Em i makim lait bilong em i shine long mipela. Inap long bindings ol sacrifis bilong ples bilong wail long horns bilong alta.
PSA 118:28 Yu em God bilong me, na mipela bai givim sankyu long yu. Yu em God bilong me, na mipela bai lifim yu up.
PSA 118:29 Givim tanis long Lod, wantaim em i gutpela; Lovin kare ba em i stap oltaim.
PSA 119:1 Ol i blesim olsem wos em i go long wei i krai nogat, ol i warka long Lotu bilong Jehovah.
PSA 119:2 Ol i blesim olsem wanem i holim tok bilong En na ol i serchim Em long olgeta haret bilong ol.
PSA 119:3 Ol i no mekim pikinini; ol i wok long wei bilong Em.
PSA 119:4 Yu bin ordaim tok save, olsem yumi mas kipim ol long hart.
PSA 119:5 O, mipela i laikim ol sem bilong mi i kamap long halivim statut bilong yu!
PSA 119:6 Na mi no bai i kamap shame wen mi tinkim ol komandan bilong yu.
PSA 119:7 Mi bai givim prais long yu wantaim hare bilong mi i stap straet wane mi lernim jusis bilong yu olsem.
PSA 119:8 Mi bai i stap long stret lay bilong yu; no ken lukim mi na lusim mi tasol.
PSA 119:9 Oli man yangpela i ken bekim wei bilong en i klia,LONG tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:10 Long olgeta harte bilong me, mi go lusim na mi painim Yu; no givim mi lus long stap long komanda bilong Yu.
PSA 119:11 Mi kisim wod bilong yu, na yu i go insait long bel bilong mi, bilong me no ken sin agensim yu.
PSA 119:12 Yu bikosim, Papa; tisim mi long tok save bilong yu.
PSA 119:13 Long maus bilong me, mi tokim ol jedjment bilong mupela.
PSA 119:14 Mi amamas long wei bilong tok bilong yu olsem olgeta long samting bilong bai yumi kisim.
PSA 119:15 Mi bai tok tok long hap long precepts bilong yu, na mi bai lukim wei bilong yu.
PSA 119:16 Mi kam amaze long statut bilong yu; mi no ken foryet wod bilong yu.
PSA 119:17 Sindaun gutpela long servant bilong yu, na mi ken i stap na holim tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:18 Opim ai bilong me na mi bai sikim samting narakai na bikpela long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:19 Mi stap strainge long gras, no ken harim komandin bilong yu long mi.
PSA 119:20 Soul bilong me i go daun long olsem ya long tingim lapun tok bilong yu long olgeta taim.
PSA 119:21 Yu bosim ol pipol bilong praide, ol i go nogut, ol i lusim komanda bilong Yu.
PSA 119:22 Kisim wei bilong miksim na sham long mi, bikos mi bin holim testimonies bilong yu.
PSA 119:23 Ol birua sindaun na tok bisor long mi, tasol wokman bilong yu stap tingim statut bilong yu.
PSA 119:24 Testimoni bilong yu em i kam na hamamasim me; ol i stap na givim me toktok.
PSA 119:25 Soul bilong me i kam antap long graun; wokim mi i kam bek gen olgeta according long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:26 Mi tok aut long ol pasin bilong mi, na Yu ansa mipela; teachim mi long ol laen bilong Yu.
PSA 119:27 Mekim klar long me rot bilong tok save long yu, na bai mi yet long wondana klostu bilong yu.
PSA 119:28 Soul bilong me i kumakim long sori; strongim mi akordng long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:29 Kisim me longwe na rausim me long rot bilong bilip masalai, na givim mi laip long loa bilong yu.
PSA 119:30 Mi go longwe tru; mi putim ol loa bilong yu bifoa mi.
PSA 119:31 Mi holim strong long tok bilong yu, Papa God; no ken givim me sham.
PSA 119:32 Mi ran i go long rot bilong yu komanda, olsem yu bai givim mipela haret i kirap.
PSA 119:33 Skulim mi, PAPA, rot bilong statut bilong yu, na bai mi holim ol go long las.
PSA 119:34 Givim mi save, bihaenim loa bilong yu, na bai mi follem i go olsem, wantaim holetpela het bilong mi.
PSA 119:35 Lusim mi i go long rot bilong tok orait bilong Yu, long hap bilong em, mi hamamas, wantaim na mi finis liklik.
PSA 119:36 Wokim bel bilong me long stori tru bilong yu, na nogat long biknem moni.
PSA 119:37 Wokim ai bilong me i go we long samting nogut; givim mi laip longpela word bilong yu.
PSA 119:38 Stapim wod bilong yu long servent bilong yu, olsem ol i save fearim yu.
PSA 119:39 Waipeotim shame bilong mipela, na mipela i pilim fear, wantaim yu yet i gat gutpela jus.
PSA 119:40 Mi laikim tok bilong Jehovah, bilong mi yet long! Wakim mi gen long jastis bilong Jehovah.
PSA 119:41 Bikpela, yu kam na helpim mi, olsem yu promis, na saveman bilong yu i kam ap long mi.
PSA 119:42 Na bai mi ken bekim wanem i laik tok strong long mi, bilong mi putim fidia long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:43 Nogat, kisim tok bilong trut i go long maus bilong mi, wantaim mi hop long jusis bilong yu.
PSA 119:44 Mi bai i kam daun long lo bilong yu, long taim, na long taim gen.
PSA 119:45 Na mi bai wakabung wantaim fri dom, bikos mi bin lukim presep bilong yu.
PSA 119:46 Mi bai tokim olsem long tok bilong witnesses bilong yu, na mi no bin shame long ol king.
PSA 119:47 Mi amamas long komandyu bilong yu, bilong em mi lamuwim ol.
PSA 119:48 Mi liftim up han bilong mi long komanda bilong yu, olsem na mi lamulai, na mi tingim strong long statit bilong yu.
PSA 119:49 Rimembiri tok bilong Yu long servant bilong Yu, we bilong yu givim mi hope.
PSA 119:50 Em i kamfort bilong mi long taim bilong trabel, olsem promis bilong yu i bringim bek gen laip bilong mi.
PSA 119:51 Ol pikinini ilaikim mi yet, tasol mi no lusim lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:52 Mi rimembirim jounejimpas bilong tumbuna bilong yu, o LORD, na mi finisbek long ol dispela.
PSA 119:53 Asua i kam long me bikos long ol wicked man ol i no givim respek long Tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:54 Statut bilong yu ol i sindaun na sang bilong mi long haus bilong mi stap bilong warkim pilgrimage.
PSA 119:55 Long nait, Papa bilong olgeta, mi rememba nem bilong yu, bikos mi mas holim laip bilong yu.
PSA 119:56 Em i praktis bilong mi, na mi bihainim presep bilong yu.
PSA 119:57 Bikpela i tok bilong me; Mi promis long kispim wod bilong yu.
PSA 119:58 Mi go lukim pes bilong yu wetaim haret bilong mi; givim gratia long mi olsem yu promis.
PSA 119:59 Mi bin tingim pas bilong mi na mi bin wendim foootprints bilong mi long testemoni bilong yu.
PSA 119:60 Mi go haritim bipo long wanpela sekond, na mi holim komandmen bilong yu.
PSA 119:61 Maski ol rop bilong ol i kamapim mi, mi no lusim tok save bilong yu.
PSA 119:62 Long midnait mi kamap strong na mekim tenkyu long yu long raitim jusis bilong yu.
PSA 119:63 Mi wanpela poro bilong olgeta i gat respek long yu, na mipela i holim presep bilong yu.
PSA 119:64 Erth i fulap long lov bilong kam na klostu, Papa; teinim mi long lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:65 Yu i gud long servant bilong yu, o Bikpela, olsem yu tok.
PSA 119:66 Tisim mi gutpela nambis na save, wantaim mi bilivim long komando yupela.
PSA 119:67 Bipo long taim bilong siking, mi go daun long rot bilong bagarap; nau mi holim wod bilong yu.
PSA 119:68 Yu i gutpela, na Yu mekim ol samting i gutpela; tisim mi long tok save bilong Yu.
PSA 119:69 Masalai ol i go long pisin storiman long me, mi holim presep bilong yu wetim hap bilong het bilong me.
PSA 119:70 Haten bilong ol i harim na klostu, tasol mi amamas long Lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:71 Em i gut long me ol i katim long me, na mi inap lern Statut bilong yu.
PSA 119:72 Lo bilong yu husat i kam long maus bilong yu i prezis moa long mi olsem tanim thousand peis bilong gol na silva.
PSA 119:73 Han bilong yu i wokim na i mekim miepela; givim mi save long mi lernim komandmen bilong yu.
PSA 119:74 Ol i save fearim Yu, bai ol i lukim mi na rejois, bikos mi bin hope long tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:75 Mi save, o Bikpela, Rul na desisan bilong yu i stap gutpela, na long trusoi yu mekim mi sufia.
PSA 119:76 Mipela pray nau, bai yu yet kam na givim mipela heti long yu, olsem yu promis long servants bilong yu.
PSA 119:77 Kamapim compassion bilong Bikpela long mi, na mi ken i stap, olsem laip bilong yu em i sweit tru long mi.
PSA 119:78 Ol i sem tumas i dai paitim bikos ol biruaim mi wantaim ka; mi bai tingim gut long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:79 Ol i gat fea long Yu, bai ol i turnim bek long mi, ol i save gut tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:80 Hart bilong mi i mas igat strepela wari long lo bilong ol lwa, na mi no ken kisim shame.
PSA 119:81 Soul bilong me i paua long salvation bilong yu; mi stap wait long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:82 Mai bel isi pinis, wating long long bilong promis bilong yu; mi askim, “Wen bai yu kam givim mi kaikai bilong het?”
PSA 119:83 Mi olsem sak bilong wain i drai nau long smok, mi no forgetim statut bilong yu.
PSA 119:84 Hamas dei bai wan servist bilong yu wait? Wanem taim bai yu wokim jusis long ol i save me?
PSA 119:85 Ol proud i kisim hole long graun bilong me long agensim Lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:86 Ol komandmen bilong yu olgeta i stap tru; mipela i persekutim mi nogat ripek long en—helpim mi!
PSA 119:87 Ol casi i wipim mi long graun, tasol mi no lusim ripot bilong yu.
PSA 119:88 Wokim mi i kam bek gen olgeta long tok bilong yu husat i stap strong na i kirapim, na mi bai harim tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:89 Wod bilong yu, Papa bilong olgeta, em i stap oltaim; em i stap strong long heven.
PSA 119:90 Fethean bilong yu i go on long olgenarashun ol; Yu bin mekim graun, na em i stap yet.
PSA 119:91 Ol loa bilong yu i stap long tude, bikos ol samting i wok servismet long yu.
PSA 119:92 Sapos lo bilong yu i no bin kamap long hap blong mi, nambis na mi olsem kilim olgeta long taim bilong sorimi.
PSA 119:93 Mi longwe time tru na no ken forge ol lak bilong Yu, wantaim ol lak ya i bringim mi bek gen.
PSA 119:94 Mi bilong Yu; savesim mi, nau Mi go lukim kamau tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:95 Ol pikinini i w8 long bagarapim mi, tasol mi bai tingim stret long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:96 Mi lukim wanpela hap long olgeta samting i kamap strong, tasol komanda bilong yu em i go long long, i no gat hap.
PSA 119:97 O, mi lavem loa bilong yu! Em i tok save long mi long oldei.
PSA 119:98 Tok bilong loa gim mekim mi save pla meri long ol poi na, wantaim ol i stap wantaim mi.
PSA 119:99 Mi save moa yet long ol tisa bilong mi, bikos tok bilong God em i tok bilong mi long tingim.
PSA 119:100 Mi save tok klia mo dan ol big man, long bikos mi bihain kaan long tok saves long yu.
PSA 119:101 Mi go het long lek bilong mi long olgeta wei i no gut, bai mi inap kepepim tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:102 Mi no go we long law lo bilong yu, nau Yu yet yu trainim mi.
PSA 119:103 Ol tok bilong yu i swit long mit bilong mi—i swit moa long maus bilong mi olsem han bilong bi!
PSA 119:104 Mi kam save long wei bilong precepts Yu, na mi hatim ol wei fals.
PSA 119:105 Tok bilong yu em i lait long lek bilong mi, na em i lait long rot bilong mi.
PSA 119:106 Mi go hed long tok na konfirmim olsem, bai mi holim strongim tok bilong righteous.
PSA 119:107 Mi bruk bilong mi i kamap strong, GOD olgeta, revivim mi gen long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:108 Akseptim ofering bilong volken blong maus bilong mi, o LORDE, na tisim mi long jusis bilong yu.
PSA 119:109 Mi kamap long tok olsem, mi putim laip bilong mi long han bilong mi yet, na mi no forget lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:110 Ol i mekim narapela trap long mi, tasol mi no lusim tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:111 Stori tru bilong yu em i inheritance bilong me foreva, wantaim ol i kamapim hamamas long het bilong me.
PSA 119:112 Mi go bekim het bilong mi olsem na mi ken kisim strong imas long mekim ol loa bilong yu, na stap olsem go long las.
PSA 119:113 Mi les long ol i go bikpela two-mind, tasol mi lavem yu lagiu.
PSA 119:114 Yu stap long ples we yu hariim mi, na Yu stap olsem skild bilong mi; Mi putim bel bilong mi long tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:115 Lusim me, yumi ol i wok olsem bikhet, na mi ken i kamap strong long bihainim ol loa bilong Bikpela.
PSA 119:116 Yu yet mas sustainim mi olsem yu promis, na mi ken i stap; no skulim long hope bilong mi.
PSA 119:117 Kisim bek long me, na bai mi save, na inap long taim olgeta yumusim pikinini long stret bilong yu.
PSA 119:118 Yu trowewe ol i go daun long we long Statut blong Yu, wantaim ol i giaman i no got pekela.
PSA 119:119 Olgeta ol raskol long graun yu pikinautim ol olsem skrap metal; mipela lavem stori bilong yu.
PSA 119:120 Bodimi bilong me i tutu long respek bilong Yu; Mi stap long fear long judgmen bilong Yu.
PSA 119:121 Mi wokim ol samting we i stret na rait; no lusim mi long ol man i bagarapim mi.
PSA 119:122 Luhekim gutpela sindaun bilong servant bilong yu; no ken larim ol pipol bilong praide i bagarapim mi.
PSA 119:123 Mai bel isi pinis, waitpin long saveman bilong yu, na long pamoa bilong yu we i stap insait long jus.
PSA 119:124 Jagos long servant bilong yu olsem lav bilong yu, na teachim mi lo bilong statut bilong yu.
PSA 119:125 Mi servat bilong yu, givim mi save, na mipela i ken knowim testimonies bilong yu.
PSA 119:126 Em i tim nau long Bikpela i kam akt, long ol i braikim lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:127 Mi lavim komanda bilong yu moa yet long gol nambawan klia.
PSA 119:128 Bikos long dispela, mi admirim olgeta kaontri bilong Yu, na mi hatim ol narapela rot bilong dae.
PSA 119:129 Stori tru bilong yu em i wondarful; olsem na mi bihainim ol.
PSA 119:130 Olsem wanem na tok bilong yu i kamapim, em i givim lait, na em i skulim ol simpel.
PSA 119:131 Mai opim maus bilong me na mi kirap na hap, bilong yu, mi laik long tok save bilong yu.
PSA 119:132 Wokim bek long me, givim mi merci, olsem yu du long ol mana i lakim nem bilong yu.
PSA 119:133 Dirim pas bilong me long tok bilong yu; nogat sindaun i go het long me.
PSA 119:134 Baim me bek long hap bilong man, na mi ken i go het long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:135 Mekpela pes bilong yu shain long servants bilong yu, na tisa mi long tok save bilong yu.
PSA 119:136 Mai bel isi kamautim olsem ren water long wei loa bilong yu i no givim respek.
PSA 119:137 Papa bilong yupela, yupela i stap raitepela, na desisipn bilong yupela i stap straait.
PSA 119:138 Tok bilong Yu i dai, na i strong tru long olgeta samting.
PSA 119:139 Pasen bilong mi i go daun olgeta bikos ol i no likim yu, ol i lusi saves long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:140 Pomis bilong yu em i kol kilim, olsem na servent bilong yu i lakim.
PSA 119:141 Mi nogat bikpela, mi i amamas, tasol mi no forgetim precepts bilong yu.
PSA 119:142 Raitim bilong yu em i stap oltaim, na Lo bilong yu em i truth.
PSA 119:143 Hevi na sori i kam long mi, tasol tok save bilong yu em i sweit bilong mi.
PSA 119:144 Testimoni bilong yu em i stap rait fastaem. Givim mi save, na bai mi ken i stap.
PSA 119:145 Mi kisim wantaim olgeta harte bilong me, bai yu hariapim mi, O LORDE! Mi bai bihainim statuts bilong yu.
PSA 119:146 Mipela i karim Yu, savesim mipela, na mipela inap kisim testemoni bilong Yu.
PSA 119:147 Mi kamap bifo moning i kom na mi singaut long hap; long tok bilong yu mi putim hop bilong mi.
PSA 119:148 Mai bel isi wanpela tok long waches bilong nait, na mi bai tingim gut long Tok bilong Yu.
PSA 119:149 Harim tok bilong mi, O PAPA bilong olgeta, olsem lovikselo bilong yu; givim mi laip olsem jastis bilong yu.
PSA 119:150 Ol i bihainim nogut i kam klostu, na ol i longwe nau long Lo bilong yu.
PSA 119:151 Papa bilong mipela, yu klos besen, na ol tok bilong yu olgeta i tro.
PSA 119:152 Taim bipo mi lusim long ol tok bilong yu, na yu tetem ol long taim i go kam, oltaim.
PSA 119:153 Kisim lok long trabel bilong mi, bekim mi, wantaim Mi no forget loa bilong Yu.
PSA 119:154 Defendim kaos bilong mi, baimbekim mi; wokim mi i kam bek gen olsem Wod bilong Yu.
PSA 119:155 Sivikेशन i go longwe na ol pipol i no gat laif, wantaim ol i no lak bilong sikiim statut bilong yu.
PSA 119:156 Gutpela i mas bilong yu, o Bikpela; wakim mi gen olgeta long kanon bilong yu.
PSA 119:157 Maski ol i go hevi na bagarapim mi plenti, mi no lusim tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:158 Mi lukim wantaim bilak ol i nogat fe, long ol i no holim tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:159 Tingim husat ol i lamusim tok save bilong yu, Papa bilong yumiyumi; givim mi laip according long dio long stap wantaim yumi.
PSA 119:160 Olgeta samting we Yu tok em i tru, na ol raitim jusges bilong Yu i stap oltaim.
PSA 119:161 Ol bikman bilong gavman na lotu i go hetim mi longwe na mipela no mekim samting, tasol haret bilong mi i bikim trausim nasal long tok bilong yu tasol.
PSA 119:162 Mi amamas long promis bilong yu olsem man i faidim kago bilong wara.
PSA 119:163 Mi hatred na ronim long tok bokis, tasol loa bilong yu mi lanem.
PSA 119:164 Seben taim long dei, mi praisim Yu long raitim jusis bilong Yu.
PSA 119:165 Plenti pis i kam long olgeta i lakim loa bilong yu; nogat samting ina bringim wonem tasol bai ol i slip.
PSA 119:166 Mi waitim salvation bilong yu, Papa bilong mipela, na mi warkim ol komando bilong yu.
PSA 119:167 Mi harkim tok save na mi lovim ol longlong.
PSA 119:168 Mi bilip strong long ol tok bilong yu, na ol story bilong yu, wantaim em i tok truth, ol rot bilong mi em ol i stap bifo yu.
PSA 119:169 Krai bilong me i kam bifo yu, o Papa bilong olgeta; givim mi save long tok bilong yu.
PSA 119:170 Mipela i mas askim Yu, kam bek long yu; Yu yet yu helpim mipela long promis bilong Yu.
PSA 119:171 Maus bilong me i kirapim prais, wantaim yu i skulim mi long ol stapela bilong yu.
PSA 119:172 Tang mi singaut long tok bilong yu, wantaim ol komando bilong yu em i stap righteous.
PSA 119:173 Han bilong yu i mas kam ap long helpim mi, nau mi bin chusim presep bilong yu.
PSA 119:174 Mi laik kam bek long saveman bilong yu, Papa God, na Lo bilong yu em i plesa blong mi.
PSA 119:175 Lai mi stap na praisim Yu; na jusis bilong Yu i save helpim me.
PSA 119:176 Mi go bek long wei olsem sip bilong pik we i las; suk finisim servant bilong yu, for mi no forget toksave bilong God.
