PSA 120:2 Lod, saviourim soul bilong me long lip na toktok i no kamap na long tang na toktok i giaman.
PSA 120:3 Wanem em bai mekim long yu, na wanem bai kamap long yu, O tang mai bilong bikim birua?
PSA 120:4 Alewa bilong pkin i kam long warrior, wantaim kol bilong faia husat i karim long diwai bilong brom!
PSA 120:5 Weo long mi, mipela stap long Mesek, na yu yet, mi save waka i go long han bilong Kedar!
PSA 120:6 Taim long mi stap long ol pipel i no likim pis.
PSA 120:7 Mi kamap strong long peis; tasol wanpela taim mi tok, ol i laik war.
PSA 121:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Mai kamautim ai na lukim maunten. Bilong wanem halivim mai kam?
PSA 121:2 Help bilong me i kam from LORD, Meka bilong heven na graun.
PSA 121:3 Em i no go let fut bilong yu pilai; Protecta bilong yu i no go slip.
PSA 121:4 Susu i go, Bikman bilong Isrel em i no ken slip na em i no ken surik.
PSA 121:5 Papa God i stap lukim yu; Papa God i stap olsem san bilong yu long sait rgba.
PSA 121:6 Sana no ken go kilim yu na mon i no ken kilim yu long nait.
PSA 121:7 Papa God bai lukautim yu long olgeta ken; Em bai save stapim spirit bilong yu.
PSA 121:8 LORDE i lukautim yu yet long taim yu i go na taim yu i kam, nau na foreva moa.
PSA 122:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Bilong Dauid. Mi hamamas long taim ol i tokim mi, "Mipela i go long haus bilong LORD."
PSA 122:2 Fut bilong mipela i stap long gate bilong yu, O Jerusalem.
PSA 122:3 Jerusalem i kamap strong olsem wanpela taun, yumi i stap wantaim.
PSA 122:4 We bilong triabus i go ap, triabus bilong LORD, olsem wan testimony long Israel, long givim sankyu long nem bilong LORD.
PSA 122:5 Long hap bilong ples bilong jijman, bilongaus bilong haus bilong Daivid i stap.
PSA 122:6 Pri ol i praikim long peis bilong Yerusalem: "Ol i lavim yu, ol i kamap strong na moningi."
PSA 122:7 Mipela i laikim peace kamap long insait bilong yu, na prosperiti i stap insait long strongpela ples bilong yu.
PSA 122:8 Long ol bilong brata na pren, mi bai tok, "Pis i kam insait long yu."
PSA 122:9 Long wei bilong haus bilong Lod God bilong mipela, mi bai go lukautim prosperi bilong yu.
PSA 123:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Mai kam luk long yu, yu we i sitten long heven.
PSA 123:2 Ai bilong servan i lukim han bilong ol bos, ai bilong hap meri i lukim han bilong meri bos, nogat, ai bilong yumi yet ol i luk long han bilong Bikpela LORD God bilong yumi, nau ol i soim mipela meri.
PSA 123:3 Papa bilong yu, givim mipela merisi, givim mipela merisi, long bikos mipela kisim planti kukim olsem.
PSA 123:4 Mipela bin i stap na karim planti sikar long ol pipol we i amamas, planti dispela laif i no gut long ol pipol we i gat bikpela hed.
PSA 124:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Bilong Davit. Igo GOD i no stap wantaim yumi—Nau Isrel i mas tok—
PSA 124:2 If Bikpela i no stap wantaim yumi wen man i kam bekim yumi,
PSA 124:3 Wewan em i birua, na bai ol i kaikaim mipela hail.
PSA 124:4 Na bai ol flod i kirapim mipela, na bai ol wata i kamautim mipela,
PSA 124:5 Na bai wara i birua i go daunim mipela.
PSA 124:6 Praiz i go long LORD, bilong hem i no givim mipela long ka bilong ol.
PSA 124:7 Mipela i kamaut na saveman olsem pisin i rausim long trap bilong man i kam huntim pisin; net bilong en i hol holeu, na mipela i slip aut.
PSA 124:8 Help bilong yumi i stap long nem bilong GOD, Meker bilong heven na graun.
PSA 125:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Ol man i givim bel nau long LORD, ol i olsem Maunten Sion, em ina pundaun, em i stap oltaim.
PSA 125:2 Ol maunten i kam rait rundim Jerusalem, olsem nau Lod i kam rait rundim pipel bilong em, na nau na long taim bai i stap.
PSA 125:3 Skeptā bilong ol i gohet no ken stap long graun ol i gat shar long raitim man, na bai ol raitim man i no kamap long mekim ol samting nogut.
PSA 125:4 GOD, wokim gud long ol pipel i gat harte gutpela, na long ol pipel i stap straigt long harte.
PSA 125:5 Na ol i wokim pasi i go long rot bilong bagarap, LORD bai driva ol longwe longol ol i wokim ol samting nogut. Pis i kamap long Israel.
PSA 126:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Taim Papa God i bringim baksaida ol prisna bilong Sion, mipela i kamap olsem ol man meri i stap insait long driman.
PSA 126:2 Na maus bilong yumi i kamap fulap long lapun, tengues bilong yumi i kamap fulap long sang. Ol i tok olsem long ol narawan ples, “Bikpela i mekim bikpela samting long ol.”
PSA 126:3 Papa God i mekim woks bilong em i gat bikpela, na yumupela i amamas long hap.
PSA 126:4 Bringim bek iet long ol prisner bilong mipela, o Bikpela, olsem ren na wara i kamap long Negev.
PSA 126:5 Ol i planti long taires bai kaikai wantaim lusi bilong joi.
PSA 126:6 Em i go na wailis, karim bek i go wantaim pikinini kumu, em bai kam bek gen na singautim loa, karim bek i go wantaim buk bilong graun.
PSA 127:1 Wanpela sang bilong go apo. Bilong Solomen. Sapos LORDE i no mekim haus, ol man i mekim haus wok long nogut, wei nogat senis; sapos LORDE i no lukautim taun, ol man i wachim i stap wach long nogut, wei nogat senis.
PSA 127:2 Bai yu kamap namel long moningtaim na i stap tilim long nait, wok harde long ka, bikos em i givim slip long ol man i larim.
PSA 127:3 Ol pikinini em i inheritans bilong GOD, na frut bilong bel em i givim bek long GOD olsem reward.
PSA 127:4 Olsem banarang long han bilong warrior, olsem nau pikinini i kamap long taim yu yet.
PSA 127:5 Man i bereket long em, wanpela bek bilong en i fulap long ol. Em no bai kisim shame wampela taim em go kamautim enemy long gate.
PSA 128:1 Wanpela sang bilong go ap. Ol man i gat bikpela blessing olsem na oli saving tok long LORD, ol i warka long wei bilong em!
PSA 128:2 Long taim yu kaikai bilong ka yu warkim, blessings na prosperiti bai i kam long yu.
PSA 128:3 Meri bilong yu bai i kamap olsem wanpela vaine we i karim planti fruit, stap strong na growe insait long haus bilong yu, na ol pikinini bilong yu olsem olpela pkin bilong olive we i save siddown arondim tepul bilong yu.
PSA 128:4 Olsem na blesing i kam long man husat i fearim LORD.

PSA 129:3 Ol man i wokim bus long baksait bilong mi, ol i mekim gro bilong ol longpela.

PSA 129:8 Maski ol i go pas, ol no ken tok, "Blessing bilong Bikpela i stap long yu; mipela blesim yu long nem bilong LORD."

PSA 131:1 Wanpela sang blo go apo. Long David. Hart bilong me i no gat bikpela tinking, ai bilong me i no luk strong. Mi no laikim bikpela samting, na mi no save kamot long ol samting we i go longwe tru long me.

PSA 132:1 Wanpela sang bilong go apo. O PAPA, tingim long namel bilong Davide olgeta hatis we em bin kisim,

PSA 132:3 Mi no go insait long haus bilong mi, na mi no kam daun na go insait long bet bilong mi.

PSA 135:11 Sihon king bilong Amorites, Og king bilong Bashan, na olgeta king bilong Canaan.

PSA 136:1 Givim sanksem long Lod, em i gutpela. Lovin kare long em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:2 Givim sankyu long God bilong ol god. Lovin kare ba em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:3 Givim sanksem long Lod bilong ol lod. Lovin ting bung long em i stap foreva.
PSA 136:4 Em i mekim wonda bikpela, lveng long em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:5 Long wanpela najing bilong Em, Em mekim heven. Em i gat lov tingting, na em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:6 Em i skelim grap long graun, longpela wara i stap, Lovin blong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:7 Em i mekim bikpela lait – lovinkavara i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:8 San i bosim de bilong dei, Lovin kare ba em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:9 Mun em i govnem na stas bilong nait. Lovin tingim em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:10 Em i kilim pikinini bilong Egypt we em i kam first, olsem pikinini bilong Faraoh, Lovin blong em i stap oltaim, nau na foreva.
PSA 136:11 Na God i bringim Izrael i kam aut naikai long ol, lovig devosin bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:12 Wantaim han bilong em i strong na arm bilong em i stret. Lovin bilong en i save stap oltaim.
PSA 136:13 Em i dividim Solwara Red long tu, lov bikpela blong em i stap olsem foreva.
PSA 136:14 Na God i lusim Isrel long mit blong, lovin kiligim blong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:15 Bai em i kirapim Faraon na arme bilong em long Red Si, vinivine bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:16 Em i lidim piple bilong En long bus na graun, na lovingsela bilong En i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:17 Em i kilim daun ol bikpela king, lovIN karai bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:18 Na i kilim ol kings bilong pawa — Loving-kindness bilong Em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:19 Sihon king bilong Amorites, Lovin kindness bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:20 Na Og king bilong Bashan — Lovin karai bilong en em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:21 Na em i givim kantri bilong ol long wei bilong ineritans, lovingkindness bilong Em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:22 Wanpela inheritance long servant bilong God, Israel. Lovingselo bilong En i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:23 Em i rememberim mipela long taim bilong kukuru, Lovingseli bilong En i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:24 Na em i laimim yumi long ol enemy bilong yumi, lovinkindness bilong Em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:25 Em i givim ka long ol krea. Lovin kindness bilong em i stap oltaim.
PSA 136:26 Givim tankyu long Bikpela God bilong heven! Lovting bilong em i save stap oltaim.

PSA 144:2 Em i lav bilong mi we i stap strong, em i kuskus bilong mi, em i bai het bilong mi, na em i saveman bilong mi. Em i skild bilong mi, we long em mi go bek long en, na em i kirapim ol pisin i Dai long mi.
PSA 144:3 O Pikinini Bilong God, man i wanem, dat yu givim attensin long em, pikinini bilong man, dat yu tingim long em?
PSA 144:4 Man i olsem win blong pispis; dei bilong em i olsem hed blong shaedo i go daun.
PSA 144:5 Bikpela, opim heven bilong yu, kam daun, tachim maunten, na ol bai i gat paia bikpela.
PSA 144:6 Kam bek long heven, bungim lainit, tulim ol i go wanwan; pilim banarang bilong yu, mekim ol i ran i go.
PSA 144:7 Kam daun long heven; beitim mi fri, skulim mi long solwara i go daun, long hap bilong ol man i no save tok pisin.
PSA 144:8 Maus bilong ol i tok olsem nogat tru, na lima rait bilong ol i gat bikim.
PSA 144:9 Mipela bai singim sang nupela long yu, o Bikpela; long hap bilong ten streng mipela bai mekim mosik long yu—
PSA 144:10 Long Em i givim win long king, i lukautim servis man David bilong en long sop long pait.
PSA 144:11 Friim mi, skulim mi long hap bilong ol man i kam, ol i tok bokis, na lim rait bilong ol i gat wari.
PSA 144:12 Na pikinini bilong yumi bai ol i stap olsem kala, ol meri bilong yumi olsem kokorak bilong haus, ol i wokim long lukautim hous bilong bikman, olsem taitim yet ol i kamap strong.
PSA 144:13 Stoa bilong yumi bai i kamap ful, bai bringim kain kain ka mona; ol bikman bilong yumi bai mekim tausens, ten tausens long graun bilong yumi.
PSA 144:14 Oksen bilong mipela bai kisim bikpela pe. No go stap olsem ol ples bilong mipela i bagarap, mipela no go daun long hap, na no ken harim sampela sori long ples bilong mipela.
PSA 144:15 Ol pipol i blesim long ol pipol we dispela i kamap: ol pipol i blesim we God bilong ol i LORD.
PSA 145:1 Wanpela Sang blo Praise. Bilong Daavid. Mipela bai larim yu antap longwei, o God bilong mipela, King; mipela bai givim sankyu long nem bilong yu olgeta taim, olgeta genarason.
PSA 145:2 Mi blesim Yu, na mi praisim nem bilong Yu olgeta dei, olgeta taim, olgeta genarasyon.
PSA 145:3 Bikpela i go longwe LORD, nomo bikpela long praisim; Gret bilong Em i no inap long sanap.
PSA 145:4 Wan genarasion bai tokaut long wok bilong yu, na genarasion namba tu bai kirapim strongpela wok bilong yu.
PSA 145:5 Glori bilong yu kamap strong na klostu. Na mi bai stap tingim long woks bilong yu olsem samting mak.
PSA 145:6 Ol bai tok klia pawa bilong wok bilong God i bikpela, na mi bai skelim gret nes bilong Yu.
PSA 145:7 Ol bai tok bik bilong nem bilong gutpela nidail yu na singaut wantaim hap long jastis bilong yu.
PSA 145:8 Papa God i stap graun na karim olgeta, i no ken harim bek long rausim bel, na i gat planti lav na sindaun.
PSA 145:9 GOD i givim guadi long olgeta; Karem bilong En i stap long ol samting Em i mekim.
PSA 145:10 Ol samting yu mekim bai givim sang long yu, o Bikpela, na ol sancts bilong yu bai blesim yu.
PSA 145:11 Ol bai tok bilong glori bilong Kingdom bilong Yu, na ol bai tokim olsem strongpela bilong Yu.
PSA 145:12 Mekim ol i save wok bilong yu em i bikpela, na glori na kain splenda bilong Kingdom bilong yu.
PSA 145:13 Kingdom bilong yu em i kingdom we stap oltaim, na pawa bilong yu em i save stap oltaim long genarashon ol. LORD em i triu long ol tok bilong en na gutpela long ol wok bilong en.
PSA 145:14 Bikpela i save olsem na i kamapim ol i go daun, na i lifim up ol i stap long graun, i skul.
PSA 145:15 Ai bilong ol i lukim Yu yet, na Yu givim ol kaikai bilong ol long taim bilong ol.
PSA 145:16 Yu opim han bilong Yu na yu givim ka long olgeta samting i gat laip.
PSA 145:17 Bikpela i stap rait long olgeta we bilong En, na gutpela long olgeta wok bilong En.
PSA 145:18 Papa God i stap narak long ol manmeri husat singautim em, long ol husat singaut long em wantaim treu.
PSA 145:19 Em i kamapim desai bilong ol i gat fea long em, Em i harim wail bilong ol, na em i save ol.
PSA 145:20 Bikpela i saves ol mana i givim hart long Em, na ol nogut, Em bai i birua ol.
PSA 145:21 Maus bilong me bai tokautim tok bis long LORD; olgeta krea bai blessim nem holy bilong em, long taim igo, na igo, na igo.
PSA 146:1 Aleluya! Praizim Lod, o sol bilong mi.
PSA 146:2 Mipela bai givim prais long LORD olgeta taim bilong mi; mipela bai singim sang bilong prais long God bilong mipela olsem mipela i stap yet.
PSA 146:3 No ken putim bilip long ol prins, long man i no ina spirit yet, we i no ina save im.
PSA 146:4 Taim spirit bilong em i go awe, em i go bek gen long graun; long dei ia noken, ol plan bilong em i dai.
PSA 146:5 Em i blesim husat i givim help long em i God bilong Jacob, husat i putim hope long LORD God bilong em,
PSA 146:6 Meker bilong heven na graun, solwara, na ol samting i stap insait long ol, em i stap tru long taim olgeta.
PSA 146:7 Bikpela i mekim rait long ol i katol long hap na i givim kaikai long ol i hangre. Bikpela i lusim ol prisoner fri.
PSA 146:8 Papa God i opim ai bilong ol pikinini i no save luk, Papa God i liftim up ol pikinini i stap daun long trabel, Papa God i lakem ol man i stap raite.
PSA 146:9 Papa God i lukautim manmeri ol i kam foapim, em i sapotim ol pikinini i no stap wantaim papa na mama, na ol meri i no stap wantaim husat, tasol em i bagarapim wok bilong ol samting nogut.
PSA 146:10 Bikpela i bos long taim olgeta, Bikpela God bilong yu, O Sain, long olgenarashon olgeta. Haliluya!
PSA 147:1 Haleluya! Hamamas ol i stap singim sang bilong preez long God bilong yumi, olgeta naispela na switpela preezeim Em!
PSA 147:2 Papa God i bikim Jerusalem i kamap; Em i kisim ol pipol Israel we i lus.
PSA 147:3 Em i helem ol pipol we i stap long sorere na em i holim na i bikim klea ol wund bilong ol.
PSA 147:4 Em i desisim numbr bilong sta; em i kolim ol sta long nem bilong ol.
PSA 147:5 Bikpela i God bilong yumai, i strong long pawa; Us no ken isave finis long en.
PSA 147:6 Papa God i holim na saveman bilong en, tasol i kirapim ol birua i go daun long graun.
PSA 147:7 Singim sang long Lod, bikos yumi gat tenkyu; wokim musik long hap long God bilong yumi.
PSA 147:8 Hu ikamapim skai wantaim klod, hu ipreparim ren bilong graun, hu imekim gras i karim longpela bun.
PSA 147:9 Em i givim kaikai long ol animal, na long ol yungpela korakor taim ol i singaut.
PSA 147:10 Em i no gat bikpela hap long strongpela hos, na em i no save longim lek i strong bilong man.
PSA 147:11 Papa God i ambis long ol manmeri iukim ol long hem, na ol i givim hope long karai bilong en.
PSA 147:12 Liftim up ol bikpela LORD, o Jerusalema; praezim Bikpela God bilong yu, o Sayan!
PSA 147:13 Em i strongim bek het long gate bilong yu na em i givim blesing long pikinini insait long yu.
PSA 147:14 Em i mekim pis long bikpela hed bilong yu; Em i pilim yu wantaim ka moninga klok.
PSA 147:15 Em i kirapim tok bilong En long graun; Tok bilong En i go kisim spid.
PSA 147:16 Em i skatriim snow olsem wul; Em i bromim frost olsem ases;
PSA 147:17 Em i kirapim hail bilong en olsem ston pikinini. Husat ina bai stap strong long wik bilong ais?
PSA 147:18 Em i kirapim tok bilong En, na ol i tanim; Em i lusim win bilong En, na wara i flow.
PSA 147:19 Em i tokim bekim wod bilong en long Jacob, ol laen na ol jus bilong en long Israel.
PSA 147:20 Em i mekim despela long narapela nesen nogat, ol i no save tok bilong En. Aleluya!
PSA 148:1 Haleluya! Praisim LORD long heaven; praisim em long ples i go het.
PSA 148:2 Praisim em, ol angelo bilong em; praisim em, ol spirit yu bilong heaven.
PSA 148:3 Praesim God long em, O san na mun; praesim em, all yufela sta bilong heven i shine.
PSA 148:4 Praisim Hem, O heven hiest, na yu wara i stap antap long skai.
PSA 148:5 Ol i givim prais long nem bilong LORD, bikos em i givim tok na ol i kamap.
PSA 148:6 Em i stap olsem foreva na foreva; Em i givim ka long wei no inap bagarap.
PSA 148:7 Praisim LORD long graun, olgeta bigpela creature long solwara na olgeta dip na dai buai long solwara,
PSA 148:8 Laitning na hail, snou na kloud, win powaful ikamapim i go longpela tok bilong En,
PSA 148:9 Maunten na olgeta hil, diwai i kamap strongpela frut na olgeta seda,
PSA 148:10 Ol animal balus long bus, ol katel olgeta, ol samting we i go long graun, na ol pisin balus we i flai,
PSA 148:11 Tubuna bilong graun na ol pipol, pikinini bilong king na ol gavana bilong graun,
PSA 148:12 Man meri yangpela, ol bikpela na ol liklik, ol i go long ol.
PSA 148:13 Ol i givim prais long nem bilong Bikpela, long nem bilong em tasol i go hap; glamour bilong em i go hap long gras na heven.
PSA 148:14 Em i kirapim bek long olgeta sant bilong em, peena bilong Iserel, ol manmeri i kamap klus long em. Halileya!
PSA 149:1 Halaleuya! Singim sang nupela long Lod, praes bilong em long ol man meri i gat respek long God bung.
PSA 149:2 Isrel i amamas long Meka bilong ol; pikinini bilong Sain i amamas long King bilong ol.
PSA 149:3 Ol i presem nem bilong Em wantaim dansing, na wokim musik long Em wantaim tamburin na hap.
PSA 149:4 Papa God i amende long ol pipol bilong En; Em i kisim bek long ol i stap i go daun wantaim saveman.
PSA 149:5 Ol sant i amamas long glori; ol i singaut long jog long bed bilong ol.
PSA 149:6 Het piksa bilong praizim Bikpela i stap long maus bilong ol, na sord na i gat tu aipis i stap long han bilong ol.
PSA 149:7 Long givim piksa i go long ol nesen, na penalti long ol pipel,
PSA 149:8 Ol i binim king bilong ol wantaim cheyn, na ol bikman bilong ol wantaim selib bilong aian.
PSA 149:9 Long kamapim dispensin ol i raitim gen long ol. Honor ya i go long ol sent bilong Em. Aleluya!
PSA 150:1 Haliluya! Praisim God long haus lotu bilong en. Praisim em long heben bilong em we i gat strong.
PSA 150:2 Praizim Em long strongpela wok bilong En; praizim Em long bikpela greatness bilong En.
PSA 150:3 Praizim Em long saund bilong kokis; praizim Em wantaim gita na lirai.
PSA 150:4 Praizim Em long tamborin na danis; praizim Em long string na flaut.
PSA 150:5 Praisim Hem wantaim simbal i kat hevi; praisim Hem wantaim simbal i sangut strong.
PSA 150:6 Oli samting i gat breth, mekim prais long LORD! Aleluya!
